What these screenshots establish for the corrected strategy: (a) the operator UI confirms 2-role model (Active / Maintenance), not numeric navigation; (b) Generate Version exists at Utilities → Versions → Generate Version but requires Change mode; (c) UNESCO's CGI tree currently has 0 historical snapshots in the version database — meaning the very first thing Phase 5 cutover prep must do is run Generate Version on each tree's V000 to create the V002 snapshot, so rollback is possible; (d) claim 109 is visually proven, validating the PURGE of the dormant V001 in Phase 2 Step 0.

Corrected implementation strategy — the V000 snapshot pattern

Given the SAP-correct model above, the V001 deployment must include a snapshot step BEFORE every activation in every system, not just the P01 cutover. The snapshot is what makes rollback possible. Without it, activation is one-way.

PhaseOperationSAP transaction / menuWhy this step exists
2 · 0a NEW: snapshot D01's current V000 on each of the 4 trees before any V001 work D01: tx DMEE → open tree → Utilities → Versions → Generate Version Captures D01 V000 to V002 (or next free). Enables D01-side rollback during Phase 3 unit test.
2 · 0b–0c D01-RETROFIT-01 + D01-RETROFIT-02-PMW (unchanged) STMS imports of pre-built transports Bring D01 to byte-equality with P01 (DMEE trees + 5 BAdI classes + PMW infrastructure tables)
2 · 1–8 Build V001 content (matrix rows 1–25 INSERT/MODIFY/SYNC) D01: tx DMEE → switch to Maintenance (V001) → edit nodes → save → activate → captures R3TR DMEE Workbench transport (K) The V001 row-level work. Transport class is K (Workbench), not W (Customizing). Saves into D01 V001.
2 · 9 SEPA Event 05 registration (matrix row 9) D01: tx OBPM4 → INSERT row in TFPM042FB One Customizing (W) transport — the only customizing-class change in V001 row-level work.
2 · 10 Pattern A 3-line BAdI guard (matrix row 26) D01: tx SE24 → YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FALLBACK_CM001::GET_CREDIT Workbench (K). N_MENARD-level reviewer required.
3 · pre NEW: confirm D01 V002 snapshot still exists from Phase 2 step 0a D01: tx DMEE → Utilities → Versions → Version Management → verify V002 row present Pre-flight check before the D01 activation. If snapshot missing, recreate via Generate Version.
3 · 1 Activate V001 in D01 (V001 content overwrites D01's V000) D01: tx DMEE → Tree → Activate. For large trees: SE38 → DMEE_ACTIVATE_TREE background. D01-only activation. Do NOT promote activation transport to V01 or P01.
3 · 2–4 F110 sample runs · XSD validation · simulator regression · BCM end-to-end D01: F110 + FDTA + offline XSD validator + simulator Validate V001 output against pain.001.001.03 + .09 schemas. Compare to simulator predictions (claim 105).
4 · pre NEW: snapshot V01's current V000 V01: tx DMEE → Utilities → Versions → Generate Version on each tree V01-side rollback enabler before UAT activation.
4 · 1 Promote V001 content transport D01→V01 (R3TR DMEE workbench) STMS Delivers V001 content as maintenance version in V01 (not activated).
4 · 2 Activate V001 in V01 V01: tx DMEE → Tree → Activate V001 content overwrites V01's V000. UAT can now run.
4 · 3 UAT scenarios + bank pilot via test gateway V01 F110 + bank's UAT environment Full bank-acceptance validation before P01 cutover.
5 · pre CRITICAL NEW STEP: snapshot P01's current V000 on each of the 4 trees P01: tx DMEE → Utilities → Versions → Generate Version (requires P01 DMEE-change auth) This is the rollback enabler for production. Without this snapshot, V000 is unrecoverable after V001 activation. Document the V### number assigned per tree.
5 · 1 Promote V001 content transport D01→V01→P01 STMS chain Delivers V001 content as maintenance in P01 (not activated yet — P01 still on V000).
5 · 2 Activate V001 in P01 (the cutover) P01: tx DMEE → Tree → Activate. For large trees: DMEE_ACTIVATE_TREE background. V001 content OVERWRITES P01's V000. F110 from this moment reads V001 → bank file emerges with structured address. The pre-step snapshot (V002) preserves the old V000 for rollback.
5 · 3 Post-cutover monitoring (14 days) P01 BCM Monitor + Treasury inbox + bank acks Verify bank acceptance + workflow 90000003 green + no schema errors.
5 · ROLLBACK Rollback procedure (if needed) P01: tx DMEE → Utilities → Versions → Version Management → select V002 → Retrieve → V002 copied into V001 → Tree → Activate V001 (with snapshot content) overwrites V000. F110 reads the old content again. Time: 5–15 min per tree. NOT atomic flag flip. Requires P01 DMEE-change authorization.
5+30d Optional: Delete V002 snapshots P01: tx DMEE → Utilities → Versions → Version Management → select V002 → Delete After V001 stable: free version slots. Irreversible — only after sustained bank acceptance.

Risk profile under the corrected model: previous strategy presumed "rollback in seconds via atomic flip" → low operational risk. SAP-correct reality: rollback is multi-step, requires snapshot pre-positioning, requires P01 DMEE-change authorization, and takes 5–15 min per tree. Mitigation: (a) make Generate Version mandatory in pre-cutover preparation per tree; (b) dry-run the Retrieve+Activate procedure in V01 cutover to confirm the rollback works as expected; (c) document V### snapshot numbers per tree in a runbook accessible during the cutover window; (d) ensure P01 DMEE-change authorization is provisioned for the on-call operator at cutover time. The strategy stays SAFE because of the snapshots — but it is NOT instant.

❓ Why versions exist at all — the 3 things versions give you (and the one thing they don't)

It is reasonable to ask: "if I have to deploy a new XML format anyway, why does SAP wrap that in a 'version' concept? Couldn't we just edit V000 directly, or create a separate tree?". The answer is that versions solve three deployment problems that would otherwise force a destructive edit or a much heavier change project.

What versions give you Why this matters What you'd have to do without versions
1. Staged pre-deployment Deploy V001 to P01 INACTIVE (EX_STATUS=' '). The config is physically in P01 but F110 ignores it. Separates "deploy" from "cutover" in time — weeks of stability between transport import and activation. Edit V000 directly in P01 (destructive — no rollback path) or build a separate parallel tree (much heavier, requires new T042Y + T042Z routing).
2. Atomic cutover The cutover is ONE UPDATE on one flag. Before the flip: all F110 use V000. After the flip: all F110 use V001. Zero in-between period where some payments are V000-output and others V001-output. A multi-step deployment with a window of inconsistency, where in-flight F110 batches might hit half-old / half-new config.
3. Instant rollback Flip the flag back. V000 rows are still in DMEE_TREE_NODE (Activate did not touch them). Rollback in seconds. The "preservation of V000" is automatic — you do not preserve V000 by copying it; you preserve it by simply not deleting it. Restore config from backup (hours), or re-edit V000 by hand to revert — and that's only possible if you didn't already touch V000 destructively in step 1.
What versions DO NOT give you Parallel running of V000 and V001 simultaneously serving different payments in P01. Only one version has EX_STATUS='A' at a time → all F110 against that tree use that version. For genuine parallel running (e.g. piloting V001 with one bank while V000 stays for others), the SAP-correct path is creating a new tree with a new TREE_ID (a Type 2 change in our taxonomy). That is a separate project — not what V001 is.

Most cutovers don't need parallel running. They need: (a) safe pre-deployment that doesn't disrupt production, (b) a single moment where the new format goes live without an in-between window, (c) a fast safety net if something fails. Versions give all three. Parallel running is a different problem and uses a different tool (separate tree).

Disambiguation: "Create Version" copies V000 rows into a new VERSION='001' inside the SAME tree (same TREE_ID, just a new value in the VERSION column — both versions cohabit in DMEE_TREE_NODE). This is internal to versioning. It is NOT the same as creating a new TREE_ID, which is a separate project (Type 2 change). When operators say "we'll just version it" they mean the first; when they say "we need a new tree" they mean the second.

Why we need to talk about versions before we talk about changes

If you have only seen DMEE once or twice, the natural mental model is "open the tree, edit the nodes, save". And that's basically right — except for one detail that changes everything: DMEE trees have a built-in versioning column. Every row in DMEE_TREE_HEAD and DMEE_TREE_NODE carries a VERSION field. UNESCO has been running on VERSION='000' for a decade. The Nov 2026 CBPR+ migration creates VERSION='001'.

This is the SAP-native way to ship a bank-format upgrade. It's the same mechanism a company would use to roll from pain.001.001.03 to .09, or to migrate from a regional format to a global one. The reason it matters here: V001 cohabits with V000 inside the same tree, both fully active in the same DMEE_TREE_NODE table, and only one is "active" (EX_STATUS='A') at any moment. The tree does not get cloned, replaced, or rebuilt. It gets a parallel sibling layer.

Two names for the same thing — SAP UI vs table layer

Before going further: SAP's tx DMEE screen uses different words from what I wrote in the matrix. Both describe the same concept, but the operator sees the UI words first and the matrix uses the table-level words. Bridge:

SAP UI label (what you see in tx DMEE)Table-level label (DMEE_TREE_HEAD column)What it actually is
Active versionVERSION='000' with EX_STATUS='A'The version F110 actually reads to produce today's bank file. UNESCO's V000 since 2017.
Maintenance versionVERSION='001' with EX_STATUS=' ' (blank)The draft / dormant copy. You edit it, test it, but it doesn't reach F110 until you activate it. Currently exists in D01 only (claim 109).

Read this in plain English: when SAP asks "Which version would you like to display? Active version / Maintenance version" — Active = V000, Maintenance = V001. The text below uses V000/V001 because it tracks back to the matrix CSV and the RFC verifications, but every time you read "V000" think "what tx DMEE calls Active version" and every time you read "V001" think "Maintenance version".

unesco_dmee_step_a_01.png — DME Engine Initial Screen. Tree type=PAYM, Format tree=/SEPA_CT_UNES. Display button click triggers the popup "Which version would you like to display? — Active version / Maintenance version / Cancel". This popup is the operator's first interaction with the version concept and applies identically to all 4 in-scope trees. Active version = V000 in production; Maintenance version = the dormant V001 byte-clone (claim 109).

Analogy that makes it click

Think of a DMEE tree like a Microsoft Word document with a published copy + a draft:

  • V000 (Active version) is the published copy. F110 has been reading it since 2017 and producing real bank files from it.
  • V001 (Maintenance version) is a draft saved alongside. It exists in the same DMEE_TREE_NODE table (just with VERSION='001'), can be edited and tested in tx DMEE Maintenance mode, but does not reach F110 until you activate it.
  • Activation = save the draft as the new published copy. Per SAP-official behavior, when you Activate V001 the system stores its content as V000, replacing the previous V000. The old published copy is overwritten.
  • Rollback requires a pre-saved snapshot. Before activating, you must run Utilities → Versions → Generate Version on the current V000 — SAP archives it as V002 (or next free number). To roll back: retrieve V002 from Version Management → it becomes the new V001 → activate → the snapshot content overwrites V000. NOT a flag flip; a multi-step Version Management procedure. See the corrected implementation strategy table above.

If you only remember one thing: V000 and V001 are not different trees — they are roles within the same tree (TREE_ID identical, VERSION column differs). Activation is overwrite of V000 by V001's content, not a flag flip. Rollback exists only if you snapshotted V000 to a historical version (V002+) BEFORE activating. The whole exercise is still "configuration, not migration" — just configuration with a mandatory snapshot step before each activation.

What's already in D01 today (you'd be surprised)

Until the post-VPN RFC verification (2026-04-30) we thought UNESCO had never touched V001 in any tree. Post-VPN RFC verification (claim 109) proved otherwise: D01 already has VERSION='001' rows on all 4 in-scope trees. Someone, at some undated past moment, ran tx DMEE → Tree → Versions → Create Version, and SAP duplicated every V000 row into V001. Those V001 rows are byte-identical to V000 (claim 109 — 0 differences across NODE_ID set + 7 sampled content fields). They've sat dormant ever since, never released to V01 or P01 (claim 102 — zero V001 patterns in 44 historical transports).

Read that in plain English: the "Create Version" step has effectively already been done in D01 — but as a clean clone of V000, with no actual structured-address changes inside. The dormant V001 in D01 is a placeholder. Before we add V001's real content, we PURGE the dormant clone and re-CREATE fresh, so the deployed V001 has a clean transport-trail tied to the Phase 2 transports — not to whatever happened years ago that was never released.

SystemV000V001Note
P01 (production)✓ Active (EX_STATUS='A')— absent —Live state. V001 has never reached P01.
D01 (dev)✓ Active (mirror of P01)✓ Dormant clone (byte-identical to V000)Per claim 109. To PURGE+RECREATE in Phase 2.
D01 after Phase 2 Step 0✓ Active (still mirror of P01)✓ Dormant fresh clone (transport-trailed)Same byte-identical content, but linked to Phase 2 transport ID.
D01 after Phase 2 Step B✓ Active✓ Dormant + structured-address nodes addedThe 27-row change matrix is applied here.
D01 after Phase 5 cutover✓ Dormant✓ Active (EX_STATUS='A')The atomic flip. F110 now reads V001.

Visual proof of claim 109 — V000 and V001 admin data are byte-identical

The two screenshots below are tx DMEE → Display Format Tree /SEPA_CT_UNES → Administrative data tab, taken on 2026-04-30. Left side shows V000 (the Active version). Right side shows V001 (the Maintenance version). Every metadata field matches exactly — Tree type, Short Description, Documentation pointer, Author, Created on, Created at, Last Changed By, Changed on, Changed at — except for one column: Version (0 vs 1). This is what SAP's "Create Version" operation does at the DMEE_TREE_HEAD level: full row copy, increment Version, leave everything else untouched.

Two facts the screenshots add to the brain:
(1) The SEPA tree was created by M_SPRONK on 27.11.2013 18:32:02 — i.e. 12 years ago. Last meaningful change was 23.11.2021 10:36:24. Operationally frozen for 4+ years.
(2) Both V000 and V001 share the same Changed timestamp (23.11.2021 10:36:24), which means Create Version was executed on or before that date. Consistent with claim 102 (zero V001 transports 2017–2024) — the dormant V001 has been sitting in D01 untouched for 4+ years, never released.

unesco_dmee_v000_admin.png — V000 (Active version) admin data. Tree type=PAYM · Format tree=/SEPA_CT_UNES · Version=0 · Author=M_SPRONK · Created 27.11.2013 18:32:02 · Last Changed 23.11.2021 10:36:24. The version F110 reads in production every day.
unesco_dmee_v001_admin.png — V001 (Maintenance version) admin data. Same tree, same Author, same Created/Changed timestamps. Only Version=1 differs. Visual proof of claim 109 — byte-identical clone. This is the dormant V001 we PURGE in Phase 2 Step A before creating a fresh clone tied to the Phase 2 transport ID.

This DMEE Configuration tab focuses purely on the V001 changes per tree.

DMEE Configuration · foundations — operations, mappings, runtime

↶ See DMEE Configuration · the version thing for the version mental model (V000 vs V001, "Active version" vs "Maintenance version", what already exists in D01, visual proof of claim 109). This sub-tab assumes you understand the version concept and covers what V001 actually does at the row / XML / runtime level.

Three types of DMEE configuration change — and where V001 sits

Before drilling into the V001 design surface, it helps to know where V001 sits in the broader space of DMEE-related changes. Every DMEE change UNESCO has ever made — past, present, future — falls into one of 3 mutually-exclusive types. The classification is exhaustive (no DMEE change escapes these categories) and orthogonal to the row-level operations (INSERT / MODIFY / SYNC) and the 4 XML party sections — both of which are dimensions inside Type 1. Knowing the type of a proposed change up-front tells you transport class, approval chain, reviewer requirements, and risk profile before any technical analysis.

TypeWhat it doesSAP objects touchedTransport classV001 scope
1 Modify sections within an existing tree — add or change rows targeting one of the 4 XML party sections (Dbtr / CdtrAgt / Cdtr / UltmtCdtr) of an already-defined DMEE tree. DMEE_TREE_NODE rows (INSERT / MODIFY / SYNC) · DMEE_TREE_COND empty-suppress conditions · DMEE_TREE_HEAD settings (Empty Element Processing, XSLT registration) · TFPM042F / TFPM042FB event registration Customizing (W) 100% of V001's row-level work. 22 tree-row operations + 1 OBPM4 event-registration row + per-row DMEE_TREE_COND for SEPA = matrix rows 1–25 + matrix row 9. The 4×4 matrix below is the entire Type 1 surface.
2 Create a new DMEE tree — a brand-new TREE_ID, full set of new nodes from root, plus the surrounding format definition and routing. DMEE_TREE_HEAD (new row) · DMEE_TREE_NODE (full new node set) · T042Y (new FORMI → SAPFPAYM_<format> binding) · T042Z (new (LAND1, ZLSCH, WAERS) → FORMI routing entries) Customizing (W) Not in V001 scope (zero Type 2 work). V001 reuses the 4 existing trees (SEPA, CITI, CGI, CGI_1). Type 2 would apply to onboarding a brand-new bank format, migrating to a future ISO 20022 message version (e.g. pain.001.001.10), or creating a region-specific variant. Highest risk profile of the 3 types because the new format hasn't been bank-tested.
3 Custom ABAP code that modifies tree behavior — code that runs at tree traversal time (BAdI methods called per node) or at PMW event time (FM registered in OBPM4 events) or at output-assembly time (XSLT post-processor). YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_* class family (BAdI implementations of FI_CGI_DMEE_EXIT_W_BADI — claim 69 routes 794 / 1,975 nodes through this) · per-node EXIT_FUNC handlers · Z user-exit FMs registered in OBPM4 events · custom XSLT programs (e.g. CGI_XML_CT_XSLT on CITI tree) Workbench (K) One minimal touch in V001: the Pattern A 3-line guard in YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FALLBACK_CM001::GET_CREDIT (matrix row 26 — the only ABAP edit in the entire V001, backward-compatible). Triggers N_MENARD code review. Higher regression risk than Type 1 — that's why the 3 lines are kept minimal and run in a guarded path.

V001 in the 3-type space: 100% Type 1 (configuration on the 4 existing trees) + 1 minimal Type 3 touch (Pattern A 3-line BAdI guard, matrix row 26 — backward-compatible). Zero Type 2 — V001 does not create new trees. This positioning is what makes V001 a low-risk surgical project (per claim 102 surgical envelope: 81.8% of UNESCO's 44 historical DMEE-touching transports are themselves Type 1 surgical changes touching ≤3 objects).

Why classifying matters: when a future change is proposed, the type tells you immediately — (a) transport class W or K · (b) approval chain (Type 1: M_SPRONK + Pablo config sign-off; Type 3: + N_MENARD code review; Type 2: + bank UAT before activation) · (c) testing surface (Type 1: tree-level RFC byte-equality + simulator regression; Type 3: + ABAP unit tests on the BAdI method; Type 2: + full F110-to-bank end-to-end pilot) · (d) risk profile (Type 1 ≪ Type 3 ≪ Type 2). The 4×4 matrix below is the Type 1 detail for V001; the rest of this tab walks the row-level operations, the bridge to documentation, and the runtime evidence chain — all of which apply within Type 1.

The V001 design surface — 4 XML parties × 4 DMEE trees (16 intersections, 7 active changes)

The single most important question this companion has to answer is: "for each tree, which area of the configuration affects which area of the XML?" The matrix below is that answer in one view. Rows are the four UNESCO DMEE trees; columns are the four XML address-bearing parties (each a clickable XML element). Each cell is either an active V001 change (green — with target #, matrix-row range, and a click-through to the per-tree sub-tab), not in V001 scope for that intersection (grey), or a SYNC inheritance from a sibling tree (blue). If a config change is not shown in this matrix, it is not part of V001.

The 7 green cells + 1 SYNC row are the entire action surface of V001 — every transport, every test scenario, every operator click in Phase 2 maps to one or more of these cells.

Empty-element handling differs by tree: SEPA's Empty Element Processing = "Do Not Remove" (claim 120) — every green-cell INSERT on the SEPA row carries a paired DMEE_TREE_COND empty-suppress condition (matrix rows 1–8 each, plus matrix row 9 for SEPA Event 05 registration). How we know it is exactly these 4 parties — the epistemic chain (system + SAP data only)

"4 address-bearing parties" is not a guess and it is not derived from any user opinion or business interpretation. The conclusion comes exclusively from system-side data — the ISO 20022 schema definition + RFC-extracted DMEE_TREE_NODE state in P01. Three independent system sources converge on the same answer:

SourceTypeWhat it tells us
1. ISO 20022 pain.001.001.03 XSD Authoritative schema (the LAW) The <PstlAdr> (Postal Address) element is permitted under exactly these party complex types: Dbtr, DbtrAgt, Cdtr, CdtrAgt, UltmtDbtr, UltmtCdtr, InitgPty, IntrmyAgt. The schema is the legal upper bound — no other party can carry <PstlAdr> in a pain.001.001.03 file. Of the 8 schema-permitted parties, UNESCO's actually-used set is determined by source 2.
2. RFC extraction of DMEE_TREE_NODE from P01 (h18 baseline 2026-04-06) Production-system data (the FACT on the ground) RFC_READ_TABLE on DMEE_TREE_NODE for all 4 UNESCO trees, filter TECH_NAME='PstlAdr'. Across all 1,975 nodes (SEPA 95 + CITI 610 + CGI 631 + CGI_1 639), the parent paths returned are exactly the 4 parties: Dbtr, CdtrAgt, Cdtr, UltmtCdtr. Zero PstlAdr nodes hang under any other party (no DbtrAgt PstlAdr, no UltmtDbtr PstlAdr, no InitgPty PstlAdr, no IntrmyAgt PstlAdr in any UNESCO tree). The 4 schema-permitted-but-not-used parties are simply absent from production. Brain claim 113 (leaf inventory P01 V000 verified by RFC).
3. Hierarchy-collapse RFC verification (2026-04-30) Production-system data (empirical V001 surface test) Independent RFC re-extraction with V001 design overlay applied. Of the 95 nodes in /SEPA_CT_UNES, only 2 are V001 INSERT targets — both are PstlAdr containers under exactly two of the parties from source 2 (Dbtr and Cdtr). Generalising across all 4 trees: 1,975 V000 nodes → 7 PstlAdr children + 1 SYNC. The address-bearing parties are empirically the only V001 INSERT entry points — there is no other class of node in production where V001 could land. Brain claim 117 + brain claim 109 + claim 111 + claim 112 (RFC byte-equality verification).

Convergence (system-data only): 3 independent system-side sources — 1 authoritative ISO schema + 2 RFC extractions of P01 production state — return exactly the same set of 4 parties. V001 modifies the <PstlAdr> sub-tree of these 4 parties, across these 4 trees. 16 intersections × 7 active changes (matrix above) + 1 SYNC inheritance. That is the entire V001 design surface — derived from SAP data, not from interpretation.

Note on user-side / operational sources: business users (Marlies, treasury reviewers) and bank-side rejection records are useful for cross-checking the system-derived conclusion — and in this case those sources happened to agree on the same 4 parties — but they are not the basis of the conclusion. The matrix would be the same matrix even if no user had ever opened the Excel. This is a CP-001 / CP-003 discipline: design conclusions anchor in system data and source code, not in user interpretation.

The Bridge — what documentation maps "1,975 DMEE config rows" to "4 XML party sections"

The 4×4 matrix exists because we have a bridge — a verifiable mapping that translates the complexity of the DMEE configuration tables (1,975 nodes across 4 trees, with cryptic columns like NODE_ID / PARENT_ID / FIRSTCHILD_ID / BROTHER_ID / TECH_NAME / MP_SC_TAB / MP_SC_FLD / MP_OFFSET / LENGTH) into the clean operator-facing model of "modify the <PstlAdr> sub-tree of one of 4 XML party sections per tree". Without that bridge, the operator faces a wall of 1,975 rows and no obvious entry point. With the bridge, the operator sees 7 entry points — and knows exactly which DMEE_TREE_NODE row in production corresponds to each.

The bridge is established by 5 specific documentation sources, each contributing a different layer. None of these sources individually is sufficient — the bridge requires all 5 cross-referenced. Below, the source, what it contributes, and where the artefact lives:

LayerSource / artefactWhat this layer contributes to the bridge
1. Schema layer (the legal target) ISO 20022 pain.001.001.03 XSD
+ pain.001.001.09 for forward compatibility		 Defines the legal XML output structure — which elements can appear, where, and with what nesting. Tells us "<PstlAdr> is permitted under exactly these 8 party complex types" and "<StrtNm> / <BldgNb> / <PstCd> / <TwnNm> are the structured-address atoms inside <PstlAdr>". Without this layer we wouldn't know what XML the bank expects.
2. Engine-semantics layer (the translation rule) SAP-standard DMEE engine ABAP source
extracted via RPY_CLASS_READ over P01 SNC/SSO — classes CL_FDTA_DME_TREE, CL_IDFI_CGI_CALL05_GENERIC		 Defines the runtime translation: each row in DMEE_TREE_NODE becomes one XML element; TECH_NAME is the literal XML tag name; the PARENT_ID / FIRSTCHILD_ID / BROTHER_ID graph is a depth-first XML hierarchy walk; the source-bind columns (MP_SC_TAB / MP_SC_FLD / MP_OFFSET / LENGTH) are the element-value reader. This is the row-to-tag bridge rule. Anchored in brain claims 73, 101, 118, 119.
3. DDIC layer (the table semantics) SAP DDIC tables (visible in tx SE11):
· DMEE_TREE_HEAD
· DMEE_TREE_NODE
· DMEE_TREE_COND
· TFPM042F / TFPM042FB
· T042Y / T042Z		 Documents the column meanings of every table the engine reads: which column is the parent pointer (PARENT_ID), which is the source-bind buffer name (MP_SC_TAB = "Source structure", MP_SC_FLD = "Source field"), which is the byte offset (MP_OFFSET) and length (LENGTH). Without this layer we couldn't INTERPRET the rows we extract.
4. UNESCO-internal technical spec N_MENARD's "TS DMEE CGI 2024-02-29" document
UNESCO Treasury technical specification for the CGI DMEE tree family — internally produced, TIER_1 brain anchor		 Documents UNESCO-specific decisions on top of SAP-standard: which Z-fields are wired through the BAdI chain, which custom tree forks (CGI vs CGI_1) exist and why, what the SocGen-mandated name-overflow rule is and where it fires (Pattern A territory). Without this layer we'd know the SAP-standard mechanism but not why UNESCO's trees diverge from the ECC reference implementation (Worldlink UltmtCdtr, CGI_1 SYNC twin, FALLBACK_CM001 guard).
5. Production-state extraction (the actual rows we navigate) h18 P01 RFC extraction (2026-04-06) — knowledge/domains/Payment/h18_dmee_tree_nodes.csv · 8,308 nodes · all 7 DMEE tables
+ 13 tx DMEE Display Format Tree screenshots (2026-04-30) — knowledge/domains/Payment/sap_standard_reference/dme_screenshots/
+ post-VPN RFC re-verification (2026-04-30) — claims 109/111/112		 The actual production state of every row in DMEE_TREE_NODE for the 4 in-scope trees. Without this we'd have the rules (layers 1–4) but no live data to apply them to. With this we can navigate: pick any of the 1,975 nodes, read its TECH_NAME, walk its PARENT_ID chain backward, and identify which of the 4 XML parties owns it. The 13 tx DMEE screenshots independently confirm the navigation matches what the operator sees on screen — empirical bridge between table rows and the tx DMEE UI.
How we derived this bridge — the reasoning trail

The 5 layers above did not appear pre-packaged. Each was discovered by asking one question and chasing the answer to its source. The 5 layers are forced by the structure of the runtime chain, not chosen by preference — drop any layer and the bridge breaks. The trail, in the order the project's investigation actually took:

  1. Starting question: "When the operator adds one row to DMEE_TREE_NODE, how does that turn into one XML tag at one specific position in the bank file?" An answer must come from somewhere — from code, from a table, from a schema, or from documentation. Decomposed the runtime chain (F110 → tables → events → DMEE engine → XML) and for each transition asked "what code or data defines this transition?".
  2. Layer 2 (engine source) was the first answer found: extracted SAP-standard CL_FDTA_DME_TREE + CL_IDFI_CGI_CALL05_GENERIC via RPY_CLASS_READ over P01 SNC/SSO. Reading the source revealed (a) the depth-first tree-traversal algorithm via PARENT_ID/FIRSTCHILD_ID/BROTHER_ID, (b) the per-row XML emission rule with TECH_NAME as tag literal, (c) the byte-pack of ADRC fields into FPAYHX-REF01 (positions 0–60 / 60–80 / 80–90 / 90–100). Anchored in brain claims 73 (engine catalog) and 101 (byte layout). This is the rule that turns a row into a tag — without this rule, no bridge is even possible.
  3. Layer 3 (DDIC) followed automatically: reading the engine source surfaces column names (MP_SC_TAB, MP_SC_FLD, MP_OFFSET, LENGTH, PARENT_ID, FIRSTCHILD_ID, BROTHER_ID, TECH_NAME). The SE11 dictionary documents what each column means semantically — "MP_SC_TAB = source structure name", "MP_OFFSET = byte offset into the source field", and so on. Without this layer the engine source is unreadable; with it, every column has a defined meaning.
  4. Layer 1 (XSD) added next: the engine source emits XML, but what XML structure is the bank actually willing to receive? Pulled pain.001.001.03.xsd from ISO 20022 and walked the schema for which party complex types accept a <PstlAdr> child. The schema returned 8 schema-permitted parties (Dbtr · DbtrAgt · Cdtr · CdtrAgt · UltmtDbtr · UltmtCdtr · InitgPty · IntrmyAgt). This bounds the legal target — V001 cannot land outside this 8-party set without violating the schema.
  5. Layer 5 (h18 P01 RFC extraction) was the next inevitable step: layers 1–3 describe the SYSTEM, but to identify UNESCO's actual current state we needed RFC_READ_TABLE on DMEE_TREE_HEAD / DMEE_TREE_NODE / DMEE_TREE_COND for all 4 in-scope trees in P01. The h18 extraction (2026-04-06) gave us 8,308 actionable rows. Filter WHERE TECH_NAME='PstlAdr' returned exactly the parent paths for Dbtr, CdtrAgt, Cdtr, UltmtCdtr — only 4 of the 8 schema-permitted parties are present in any UNESCO tree. This collapsed 8 → 4 by direct empirical observation. 13 tx DMEE Display Format Tree screenshots (2026-04-30) gave independent visual confirmation that the same hierarchy is what the operator sees on screen — engine rule + extracted rows + UI all agree.
  6. Layer 4 (N_MENARD TS DMEE CGI 2024-02-29) was the last layer needed: layers 1+2+3+5 explained SAP-standard mechanics + UNESCO production state — but not WHY UNESCO's trees diverge from a vanilla SAP install. Open questions remained: why does CITI's UltmtCdtr have a StrtNm node with empty source-bind? why does CGI_1 share a FIRSTNODE_ID with CGI parent? why does /SEPA_CT_UNES have Empty Element Processing = "Do Not Remove" while CITI uses XSLT auto-removal? N_MENARD's UNESCO-internal technical specification documents the historical decisions that produced these divergences (Worldlink BRL flow → UltmtCdtr exists; CGI fork for non-SEPA → SYNC twin retained for legacy compat; SocGen schema-strict expectations → Empty Element Processing setting). This is the layer that prevents misinterpreting deliberate UNESCO divergences as bugs.
  7. The walk emerged from the combination: once layers 1–5 were all on the table, "which DMEE_TREE_NODE rows correspond to which XML party section?" became a deterministic question with a deterministic answer. For every PstlAdr node returned by layer 5, walk the PARENT_ID chain backward (using layer 2's parent-pointer rule, applied to layer 5's data) until you hit an ancestor whose TECH_NAME is one of the 4 parties from layer 1. That ancestor is the owner of that PstlAdr. Repeating the walk for every PstlAdr in all 4 trees → exactly 7 PstlAdr containers, each assigned to one (Tree × Party) cell of the matrix.
  8. The matrix entries emerged from one more diff: for each of the 7 owned PstlAdr containers, ask layer 1 "what structured atoms (StrtNm / BldgNb / PstCd / TwnNm) are required by V001?" and ask layer 5 "what children does this PstlAdr currently have in production?". The set difference is the V001 INSERTs for that target. Repeated for all 7 targets → 22 row-level INSERT/MODIFY/SYNC operations. Add 1 OBPM4 event-registration row for SEPA (matrix row 9, derived from the layer 5 RFC dump on TFPM042FB) + 1 BAdI guard for CGI (matrix row 26, derived from N_MENARD TS in layer 4) + 1 master-data fix (matrix row 27, derived from a separate vendor-master DQ check) → 27 rows = the entire v001_change_matrix.csv. Every row traceable to a specific layer-cross-reference. Zero rows derived from anything other than system data.
  9. The independent re-derivation that validated the methodology: claim 117 hierarchy-collapse RFC verification (2026-04-30) re-walked the same logic from scratch on /SEPA_CT_UNES — "of the 95 nodes in this tree, how many are V001 INSERT targets?". The independent walk returned 2, matching the matrix's predicted 2 (Dbtr/PstlAdr container + Cdtr/PstlAdr container). Independent re-derivation arriving at the same answer is the confidence test that the methodology is tight, not coincidental.

Methodology summary: the bridge is not a clever invention — it is the unique result of (a) decomposing the runtime chain into transitions, (b) for each transition asking "what code or data defines this?", (c) chasing every answer to its source artefact, (d) cross-referencing the artefacts to navigate from "1,975 opaque rows" to "7 named (Tree × Party) cells". Each layer corresponds to one inevitable question along the chain. Drop any one and the bridge breaks: no XSD = don't know the legal target · no engine source = don't know the row→tag rule · no DDIC = engine source unreadable · no N_MENARD TS = UNESCO divergences look like bugs · no h18 = rules without data. The 5 layers are forced by the structure of the chain, not chosen by preference.

How the 5 layers compose into the actual bridge

The bridge is built bottom-up, each layer locking the next:

  1. Layer 1 (XSD) tells us "PstlAdr can live under Dbtr, CdtrAgt, Cdtr, UltmtCdtr (and 4 others not used by UNESCO)". This bounds where in the XML structured address can land.
  2. Layer 2 (engine source) tells us the rule: "for each DMEE_TREE_NODE row, emit an XML tag named TECH_NAME, nested according to PARENT_ID chain, with value sourced from MP_SC_TAB+MP_SC_FLD+MP_OFFSET+LENGTH". This bridges any row to its corresponding XML element.
  3. Layer 3 (DDIC) tells us how to READ a row's columns — without this, "MP_SC_FLD=REF01" is just a string; with this, we know REF01 is a 100-byte buffer field on FPAYHX whose layout is documented by claim 101.
  4. Layer 4 (N_MENARD TS) tells us why some UNESCO trees diverge from SAP-standard — required to interpret why CGI_1 inherits from CGI parent (SYNC), why CITI's UltmtCdtr exists, why /SEPA_CT_UNES has Empty Element Processing="Do Not Remove".
  5. Layer 5 (h18 RFC + screenshots) gives us the 1,975 actual rows. Combining with layers 1–4: walk every row's PARENT_ID chain backward → find the closest ancestor whose TECH_NAME matches one of the 4 XML parties (Dbtr/CdtrAgt/Cdtr/UltmtCdtr). That walk is what assigns each PstlAdr to its owning party. Result: a deterministic mapping "this NODE_ID is the PstlAdr container under Tree X / Party Y".

For each of the 7 PstlAdr containers identified by layer 5, we then ask layer 1: "what structured atoms (StrtNm, BldgNb, PstCd, TwnNm) are required by the bank under this party in V001?". The diff between "what XSD requires" and "what production currently has under this NODE_ID" produces the matrix-row INSERTs for that target. That diff, repeated for each of the 7 targets, IS the v001_change_matrix.csv — 27 rows, derived 100% from system data.

Why this bridge simplifies the work: without it, an operator looking at DMEE_TREE_NODE for the 4 trees sees 1,975 rows with no obvious organising principle — the column names are SAP-internal, the NODE_IDs are opaque (N_4754354180 doesn't tell anyone anything), and the PARENT_ID graph doesn't directly say "this is Dbtr's address". Once the bridge is built, those same 1,975 rows collapse into 4 trees × 4 XML parties = 16 buckets, of which only 7 actually need V001 work. The matrix at the top of this section is the bridge's output — operator-facing language ("modify Dbtr/PstlAdr in SEPA") on the left of the bridge, system-derived NODE_IDs and matrix rows on the right. The bridge is the reason "1,975 nodes" becomes "7 surgical changes".

Reference artefacts on disk:
· knowledge/domains/Payment/h18_dmee_tree_nodes.csv — 8,308 nodes (layer 5 extraction)
· knowledge/domains/Payment/sap_standard_reference/dme_screenshots/ — 13 tx DMEE screenshots (layer 5 visual confirmation)
· extracted_code/FI/DMEE_p01_canonical/ — extracted ABAP source of UNESCO BAdI classes (layer 4 + layer 2)
· knowledge/domains/Payment/v001_change_matrix.csv — the 27-row authoritative spec (the bridge's output)
· Zagentexecution/incidents/xml_payment_structured_address/version_difference_matrix_session63.json — RFC byte-equality verification (layer 5 — claims 109/111/112)
· xsd_validators/ — pain.001.001.03 + .09 schema files (layer 1)

How we know that "INSERT this row in DMEE_TREE_NODE → this XML tag appears here" — the evidence chain

The matrix above claims that adding a specific row to DMEE_TREE_NODE produces a specific XML element at a specific path in the bank file. That is not a guess and it is not magic — it is a 7-link runtime chain from F110 button-press to bank file, where each link is independently verified against source code, RFC-extracted production data, or empirical end-to-end validation. Without this chain the matrix would be a hypothesis. With it, every cell is an empirically-confirmed mapping. The table below walks every link and names the artefact that proves it.

#Runtime link — what physically happensHow we verified it (the investigation)Anchor
1 F110 reads FBZP → resolves (LAND1, ZLSCH, WAERS) → T042Z.FORMI (the PMW format ID, which equals the DMEE TREE_ID for tree-driven formats). RFC_READ_TABLE on T042Z from P01 (knowledge/domains/Payment/h18_dmee_tree_*) — extracted all 13 in-scope (LAND1, ZLSCH) combinations and the format ID each routes to. Cross-checked against SAP-standard SAPF110V runtime documentation. Verified that ZBUKR is NOT in T042Z keys → routing is the same across UNESCO entities (closes the "different cocode different format" risk). claim 103 (T042Z routing verified, no ZBUKR)
2 FORMI → T042Y resolves to the SAPFPAYM_<format> ABAP program + tree type PAYM + format-spec structure (e.g. FPM_SEPA). RFC_READ_TABLE on T042Y for the 4 in-scope FORMI values. Confirmed each maps to a SAP-standard SAPFPAYM_* program with TREE_TYPE='PAYM'. The mapping is a customizing entry — drift between D01 and P01 here is exactly what D01-RETROFIT-02-PMW exists to detect (see D01 ↔ P01 Checks tab). D01-RETROFIT-02-PMW source data
3 SAPFPAYM_<format> reads TFPM042F + TFPM042FB → for each event (1, 2, 3, 5, 9…) identifies the user-exit FM to call. Event 05 = address fill. RFC_READ_TABLE on TFPM042F + TFPM042FB filtered by FORMI in scope. Confirmed: CITI / CGI / CGI_1 already have Event 05 registered to FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_CGI_05 in P01. SEPA does NOT have Event 05 in P01 — that's exactly the gap matrix row 9 closes. The empty cell in this RFC dump is what told us SEPA needs the OBPM4 INSERT. matrix row 9 — derived directly from this RFC gap
4 Event 05 fires FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_CGI_05 → which calls CL_IDFI_CGI_CALL05_GENERIC::GENERIC_CALL → reads ADRC (via BAPI_COMPANYCODE_GETDETAIL for Dbtr / via partner derivation for Cdtr) → byte-packs the address fields into FPAYHX-REF01..REF10. Read the actual ABAP source code of CL_IDFI_CGI_CALL05_GENERIC (extracted via RPY_CLASS_READ over P01 SNC/SSO). The byte-packing logic literally writes:
· REF01+0(60) = ADRC.STREET
· REF01+60(20) = ADRC.HOUSE_NUM1
· REF01+80(10) = ADRC.POST_CODE1
· REF01+90(10) = ADRC.REGION
· REF06+0(40) = ADRC.CITY1
That source code is the authoritative byte layout. And: a static scan of 986 UNESCO Y/Z ABAP files returned zero writers to FPAYHX-Z* / FPAYH-REF — UNESCO has no custom code that fills those buffers, only the SAP-std exit does. So the buffer contents at DMEE-traversal time are deterministic and known.		 claim 101 (byte layout) + claim 68 (no UNESCO writers)
5 The DMEE engine walks DMEE_TREE_NODE for the active version (filtered by VERSION + EX_STATUS='A') → emits one XML element per row using TECH_NAME as the tag literal → reads the source-bound buffer slice via MP_SC_TAB / MP_SC_FLD / MP_OFFSET / LENGTH as the element value. Read the SAP-standard DMEE traversal source. Confirmed: depth-first walk via PARENT_ID / FIRSTCHILD_ID / BROTHER_ID graph; one row → one emission; TECH_NAME = literal tag; source-bind columns = element value reader. Independent visual confirmation: tx DMEE Display Format Tree shows the same indentation that appears in the output XML — UI tree-pane depth = XML element nesting depth, exactly 1:1, no transformation step (verified via the 13 tx DMEE screenshots in knowledge/domains/Payment/sap_standard_reference/dme_screenshots/). claim 73 (engine catalog) · claim 118 (UI depth = XML depth 1:1) · claim 119 (TECH_NAME path-disambiguation)
6 Per-tree Post Processing tab setting determines whether empty-source rows emit <Tag></Tag> or are suppressed. Two paths: "Do Not Remove" + DMEE_TREE_COND empty-suppress (SEPA), or XSLT post-processor auto-removes empties (CITI). Visually verified for /SEPA_CT_UNES via tx DMEE Display Format Tree → Post Processing tab screenshot (unesco_dmee_post_processing.png): Empty Element Processing = "Do Not Remove", XSLT Program = (empty). Therefore each V001 INSERT for SEPA carries a paired DMEE_TREE_COND empty-suppress condition (matrix rows 1–8 each have one). For CITI, the XSLT program CGI_XML_CT_XSLT is registered → empties auto-removed at output → no DMEE_TREE_COND needed for CITI INSERTs. For CGI/CGI_1, the Post Processing setting is part of Phase 2 Week 0 capture queue (TBD). claim 120 (SEPA Post Processing settings)
7 The DMEE engine assembles the XML in memory → SAPFPAYM writes the file → BCM picks it up → SWIFT/Alliance Lite2 transmits → bank receives. Production observation: 794 actual F110 output files in P01 over the past quarter — direct empirical evidence that the V000 chain works as described. These files validate against the pain.001.001.03 XSD; banks (SocGen / Citibank / CGI member banks) accept V000 today. The output is the proof of concept that the chain works; V001 reuses the same chain with just more rows in DMEE_TREE_NODE. P01 production output (claim 105 simulator validates against this corpus)
The simulator — the witness that closes the loop

Reading every link of the runtime chain only proves we understand the chain. To prove the chain works exactly the way we say — that "edit a DMEE_TREE_NODE row → produces this specific XML output" — we built a pure-Python re-implementation of the DMEE engine (the simulator, claim 105). The simulator is small, self-contained, and reads:

  • DMEE_TREE_NODE rows from CSV (RFC-extracted from P01 — h18_dmee_tree_nodes.csv)
  • The byte-layout for FPAYHX-REF01..REF10 (claim 101 — derived from CL_IDFI_CGI_CALL05_GENERIC source)
  • The traversal logic (PARENT_ID / FIRSTCHILD_ID / BROTHER_ID, TECH_NAME emission, MP_SC_TAB+MP_SC_FLD source-binding) reverse-engineered from the SAP-standard engine source
  • The two post-processing modes (DMEE_TREE_COND empty-suppress, or XSLT auto-removal)
  • The pain.001.001.03 + pain.001.001.09 XSDs from ISO 20022

It produces XML for any input DMEE_TREE_NODE + FPAYHX snapshot, and validates against the schemas. The validation result on the 794 historical production cases:

794 production cases × 3 schemas = 2,382 PASS, 0 FAIL
(794 × pain.001.001.03 V000 schema + 794 × pain.001.001.09 forward-compatibility + 794 × V001 design overlay — all PASS)

What that result means in plain language: for every one of 794 real production payments, the simulator's predicted XML matches what SAP F110 actually produced (within all schema-significant fields). The chain in the table above is therefore not a model we hope is right — it is a model that has been run end-to-end against production data and reproduced production output. The same chain runs for V001 (just with 7 more rows): simulator predictions for V001 inputs validate against pain.001.001.03 and .09 schemas with the same 100% pass rate. The matrix at the top of this section is what the simulator confirms is achievable.

Worked example — trace one cell of the matrix end-to-end

Pick the SEPA × Cdtr cell of the matrix above. The matrix says "Target #2 · +4 INSERT, matrix rows 1–4". The chain that connects each side:

  1. The 4 INSERTs add 4 rows to DMEE_TREE_NODE, all with VERSION='001', PARENT_ID=N_4754354180 (existing Cdtr/PstlAdr container), TECH_NAME ∈ {StrtNm, BldgNb, PstCd, TwnNm}, source-bound to FPAYHX-REF01[0..60] / REF01[60..80] / REF01[80..90] / REF06[0..40].
  2. At F110 runtime, the SAP-std exit FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_CGI_05 fills FPAYHX-REF01 / REF06 from ADRC.STREET / HOUSE_NUM1 / POST_CODE1 / CITY1 (link 4 above, claim 101).
  3. The DMEE engine walks the new V001 rows (link 5 above, claim 73 + 118), emits one tag per row, reads the buffer slice for each.
  4. The output XML for the bank acquires 4 new tags inside <Cdtr><PstlAdr>: <StrtNm>, <BldgNb>, <PstCd>, <TwnNm> — exactly where the matrix said they would appear.
  5. Empty rows are suppressed per claim 120 SEPA Post Processing setting → DMEE_TREE_COND on each new row → no schema-breaking empty tags.
  6. The simulator ran this exact configuration and produced the expected XML, schema-validated PASS — that's how we know link 1–6 chain together correctly without any uninspected step.

The de-magic'd answer to "how do we know": (a) we read the SAP-standard ABAP source for every step of the runtime chain (links 1–6); (b) we RFC-extracted every input table the chain reads and verified its current state in P01; (c) we re-implemented the chain in Python and validated 794 production payments × 3 schemas → 2,382 PASS / 0 FAIL; (d) we statically scanned 986 UNESCO custom ABAP files to confirm no Y/Z code disrupts the chain (claim 68). Every link "DMEE_TREE_NODE row → bank XML element at this exact path" is independently verified. The simulator is the witness that the chain works end-to-end. The matrix is what that witness confirms — not a hypothesis, an empirically-validated mapping.

The three operations on V001 (this is all there is)

When you switch tx DMEE to V001 and start editing, every change you can make falls into one of three categories. There is no fourth. Understanding this categorisation is what unlocks "why this is config, not code":

OperationWhat happens at table levelWhen you'd do itHow many rows in our 27-row matrix
INSERT row (ADD)New row appended to DMEE_TREE_NODE with VERSION='001' + a fresh NODE_ID + PARENT_ID pointing to an existing parent (e.g. <PstlAdr>). Source binding (MP_SC_TAB/MP_SC_FLD/MP_OFFSET/LENGTH) is set on the same row.The sub-node didn't exist in V000 at all. Most common case for SEPA (no structured atoms exist anywhere) and for CGI <CdtrAgt> (structured atoms missing for the bank).~25 of the 27
MODIFY row (UPDATE)Existing V001 row gets an UPDATE on its source-binding columns (e.g. set MP_SC_FLD='ZSTRA' where it was empty).The sub-node already exists in V001 (because it was cloned from V000) but its source binding was empty or wrong. Example: CITI <UltmtCdtr><StrtNm> exists with no source — V001 sets FPAYH-ZSTRA as the binding (claim 99).1 (row 17 — CITI UltmtCdtr StrtNm)
SYNC propagationNo direct edit — the change rides on a parent-tree edit because FIRSTNODE_ID is shared.Two trees that share a root segment. Example: /CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO_1 SYNC with parent /CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO (Phase 0 Finding D).1 (row 25)

SEPA tree V000 baseline reference: full /SEPA_CT_UNES ASCII rendering · 3 tree-pane screenshots · Dbtr/PstlAdr highlighted screenshot · 3 structural anchors (two PstlAdr instances, UltmtCdtr/UltmtDbtr Nm-only, Cdtr/Nm 2-atom concatenation) all live in Current Solution → Per-tree current state → Tree 1 of 4 · /SEPA_CT_UNES.

Where in the tree the V001 INSERTs land

The V001 INSERTs from the matrix attach to existing parent nodes deep in the hierarchy. The path the operator navigates in tx DMEE Maintenance-version edit mode:

Matrix rowsNavigation path in tx DMEEParent NODE_IDExisting children todayV001 inserts
1–4 (Cdtr)Document > CstmrCdtTrfInitn > PmtInf > CdtTrfTxInf > Cdtr > PstlAdrN_4754354180Ctry, AdrLine, AdrLine+StrtNm, +BldgNb, +PstCd, +TwnNm
5–8 (Dbtr)Document > CstmrCdtTrfInitn > PmtInf > Dbtr > PstlAdrN_9926185740Ctry, AdrLine+StrtNm, +BldgNb, +PstCd, +TwnNm

Read this in plain English: the operator does NOT touch UltmtDbtr, UltmtCdtr, CdtrAgt, InitgPty, or any other party — only the two PstlAdr containers nested under Dbtr (5 clicks deep) and Cdtr (6 clicks deep). Everything else stays exactly as V000 has it.

The bridge in one sentence

One row in DMEE_TREE_NODE = one tag in the output XML. The DMEE tree IS the XML template. F110 walks the tree top-to-bottom, and for each row it emits one XML element using TECH_NAME as the tag and the source-bound buffer slice as the value. That is the entire connection. No transformation, no codegen, no intermediate format. INSERT 4 rows under <PstlAdr> in V001 → 4 new tags appear in the XML file at cutover.

The 7 V001 INSERT/MODIFY targets are now documented inside each tree's sub-tab, side-by-side with that tree's bridge in parallel and Step A/B/C walkthrough. Single owner per fact, no cross-tab jumps:

↳ Tree 2 · CITITarget #3 (Dbtr-primary) · Target #4 (Dbtr alt-mode) · Target #5 (UltmtCdtr — MODIFY+INSERT) · Target #6 (CdtrAgt)9 ops (rows 10–18 + 19–20): 2+5+(1 MODIFY+1 INSERT)+2

Same connection, different formats — one rule across all 4 trees

The bridge holds identically for every UNESCO DMEE tree. Each tree has its own row set and produces its own XML format. Same engine, same rule.

Where the values come from at runtime

The tags appear because the source-bound buffers are populated. UNESCO's already-populated buffers do all the work — no new ABAP fills any field for V001:

  • FPAYHX-LAND1 / FPAYHX-ZLISO — 2-char ISO country code, populated by SAP-std PMW from LFA1.LAND1 (vendor master).
  • FPAYHX-REF01[0..60] = ADRC.STREET (street name slice). Populated by SAP-std CL_IDFI_CGI_CALL05_GENERIC::GENERIC_CALL when Event 05 fires (claim 101 byte-layout).
  • FPAYHX-REF01[60..80] = ADRC.HOUSE_NUM1 (building number slice). Same writer.
  • FPAYHX-REF01[80..90] = ADRC.POST_CODE1. Same writer.
  • FPAYHX-REF06[0..40] = ADRC.CITY1. Same writer.
  • FPAYH-ZSTRA / FPAYH-ZBSTR / FPAYH-ZBORT / FPAYH-ZBPST — UNESCO custom Z-fields filled by Event 05 user-exit. Already populated for CITI/CGI Cdtr today (claim 67 confirms the catalog of 25 Z-fields in FPAYHX). V001 reuses the same fields for new structured nodes.

One precondition for SEPA: FPAYHX-REF01..REF10 are populated by SAP-std Event 05 (FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_CGI_05). Today TFPM042FB has Event 05 registered for CITI and CGI trees but not for SEPA. Matrix row 9 adds the missing TFPM042FB row so the buffer fills for SEPA the same way it does for CITI/CGI. After matrix row 9, REF01[0..60] etc. carry the structured atoms for every SEPA payment, and the new V001 nodes can read them.

[Per-format V001 file deltas removed — same information now lives in the cross-tree summary table above and in each tree's sub-tab. Plan-agent-flagged duplicate dropped 2026-04-30.]

Why this is configuration not code — proven by the bridge

The bridge above shows that every new XML tag in V001 is produced by a new row in DMEE_TREE_NODE reading from a buffer field that SAP-std PMW already fills. No buffer is written by UNESCO custom code (claim 68 — static scan of 986 ABAP files returned 0 writes to FPAYHX-Z* / FPAYH-REF). No new BAdI method is implemented for the address structuralisation in V001. The matrix rows 1–25 are all DMEE_TREE_NODE / DMEE_TREE_COND / TFPM042FB INSERT or UPDATE statements — customizing transport class W. The single ABAP touch in V001 (matrix row 26 — Pattern A 3-line guard in YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FALLBACK_CM001::GET_CREDIT) is orthogonal to address structuralisation: it protects an existing SocGen-mandated name-overflow path from being clobbered by the new StrtNm node, and is workbench class K only because it edits ABAP source.

PMW program retrofit — moved to D01 ↔ P01 Checks

The DMEE tree is only one part of the F110 → bank file chain. The surrounding PMW infrastructure (T042Z routing, T042Y format definition, TFPM042F/TFPM042FB event registration, SAPFPAYM_* programs, VARI variants, OBPM2 forms, YTFI_PPC_* PPC dispatch) must also be byte-aligned D01↔P01 before Phase 3 unit testing. The full retrofit scope (D01-RETROFIT-02-PMW) — 8 objects, 5-step discovery → triage → execute → verify → gate flow — now lives in 🔍 D01 ↔ P01 Checks → "PMW infrastructure alignment" section, alongside the existing D01-RETROFIT-01 documentation. This foundations tab focuses on the DMEE tree itself; the surrounding infrastructure is a check-and-align concern, which is the natural home of the D01 ↔ P01 Checks tab.

Step-by-step in tx DMEE — the version dance, per tree

The same 3-stage dance (Step A · prepare V001, Step B · edit V001, Step C · activate at cutover) is performed independently for each of the 4 in-scope trees. Steps A and C are mechanically identical across trees; Step B differs because each tree has different INSERT / MODIFY / SYNC operations. Below is each tree's specific walkthrough plus the explicit ABAP-vs-config indicator.

Code-change inventory (across all trees): of the 4 trees, only ONE requires an ABAP code change — the CGI tree (/CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO) needs the Pattern A 3-line guard in YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FALLBACK_CM001::GET_CREDIT. SEPA, CITI, and CGI_1 are 100% configuration. Master-data fix (5 LIFNRs) is independent of any tree and owned by the Master Data team.

"And none of this is ABAP" — the headline insight

Every operation in Steps A/B/C is a UI action in tx DMEE that translates to an INSERT or UPDATE on DMEE_TREE_NODE, DMEE_TREE_HEAD, or DMEE_TREE_COND. None of this writes a single line of ABAP. The transport request type is W (Customizing) — answered by analogy from the existing 44 historical DMEE transports. KU-2026-DMEE-C ("are V001 transports W or K?") resolves to W with one exception: the Pattern A 3-line BAdI guard (matrix row 26).

Change categoryTransport typeWhyRows in matrix
Tree node INSERT/UPDATEW (Customizing)DMEE_TREE_* are customizing tablesRows 1–25 (all tree work)
OBPM4 row INSERT (TFPM042FB)W (Customizing)TFPM042FB is customizingRow 9 (SEPA Event 05 registration, Sub-option A)
SYNC across CGI / CGI_1W (Customizing)FIRSTNODE_ID inheritanceRow 25
BAdI source code edit (Pattern A guard)K (Workbench)YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FALLBACK_CM001 is ABAPRow 26 — only ABAP touch in V001
Vendor master data fix (5 LIFNRs)(no transport, master data)LFA1 + ADRC are master-data tablesRow 27 — Master Data team owns

Sanity check from history: claim 72 (TIER_1) — across 44 DMEE-touching transports 2017–2024, M_SPRONK authored 31. Every one of those was a customizing transport for tree-node configuration. The pattern of "open tx DMEE, edit, save, capture in customizing TR" is exactly what V001 follows. The only thing that's first-time-ever is the Activate-Version step at cutover (claim 102 — never exercised), which is why the dry-run protocol in knowledge/domains/Payment/dmee_versioning_procedure.md exists.

What this configuration tab changes for V001

Nothing on its own — this tab is the explanation, not the action. The actions live in Phase 2 · Config D01 (the 17-step Phase 2 checklist) and the per-tree transport plan in knowledge/domains/Payment/dmee_versioning_procedure.md. What this tab anchors is the team's shared mental model: same trees, same segments, same parents — only siblings added inside <PstlAdr>; activation is a one-column flip; rollback is the same flip in reverse. If everyone walking into Phase 2 holds that picture, the operational risk is much smaller than it looks on paper.

Notice the two PstlAdr instances: one at PmtInf level (batch debtor), one nested deeper at CdtTrfTxInf level (per-transaction beneficiary). They produce two separate <PstlAdr> blocks in the XML, at different depths, each with its own children. V001 has to INSERT 4 nodes into each one — that's why matrix row 1–4 (Cdtr/PstlAdr) and rows 5–8 (Dbtr/PstlAdr) are separate sets even though the TECH_NAMEs (StrtNm/BldgNb/PstCd/TwnNm) are identical.

      Cdtr
        Nm
        PstlAdr ←── INSERT TARGET #2
          Ctry      (FPAYHX-ZLISO)        ← V000 kept
          AdrLine   (FPAYHX-ZPFST)        ← V000 suppressed
          AdrLine   (FPAYHX-ZPLOR)        ← V000 suppressed
          StrtNm    (FPAYHX-REF01[0..60]) ← INSERT row 1

      <Nm>UNESCO</Nm>
      <PstlAdr>

                                          ← AdrLine suppressed

The connection now reads: each new line indented under PstlAdr in the UI (left) corresponds to one new tag inside <PstlAdr> in the XML (right). The 4 INSERTs at each PstlAdr produce 4 new XML tags at the matching nesting depth. The empty-suppress conditions (matrix rows 1–8) hide the legacy AdrLine entries from the output, so the bank receives clean Fully Structured PstlAdr blocks.

The whole connection in one line: UI tree indentation = XML tag nesting. Configuring at level N in tx DMEE = emitting at depth N in the XML. INSERT Element under PstlAdr = new sibling of Ctry/AdrLine in the UI = new sibling of <Ctry>/<AdrLine> inside <PstlAdr> in the XML. Same operation, two views. No translation step.

Tree 1 of 4 · /SEPA_CT_UNES

Tree summary: 95 nodes V000 → 103 nodes V001. Bank: Société Générale (SEPA-zone EUR payments). Format: pain.001.001.03. Empty Element Processing = "Do Not Remove" (claim 120) → per-node DMEE_TREE_COND empty-suppress mandatory. No XSLT post-processor.

SEPA Step A · PURGE existing dormant V001, then CREATE fresh V001

  1. tx DMEE → DME Engine: Initial Screen → Tree type = PAYM + Format tree = /SEPA_CT_UNES → click Display
  2. Popup "Which version would you like to display?" → Active version (inspect V000) → re-open with Maintenance version (confirm dormant V001 exists per claim 109)
  3. Back to initial screen → Change → choose Maintenance version
  4. Menu: Tree → Versions → Delete Version → select VERSION=001 → confirm. Save → transport D01K-RETROFIT-01-V001-PURGE
  5. Menu: Tree → Versions → Create Version → Source 000, Target 001 → confirm. Save → transport D01K-V001-SEPA-01

SEPA Step B · INSERT 8 structured nodes + 8 conditions + 1 OBPM4 row

  1. tx DMEE → open /SEPA_CT_UNES → switch tree view to VERSION=001 (Maintenance)
  2. Navigate to INSERT TARGET #1: Document > CstmrCdtTrfInitn > PmtInf > Dbtr > PstlAdr
  3. Right-click PstlAdr → Insert Element → set TECH_NAME=StrtNm, MP_SC_TAB=FPAYHX, MP_SC_FLD=REF01, MP_OFFSET=0, LENGTH=60 (matrix row 5)
  4. Repeat for BldgNb (REF01[60..80] · row 6) · PstCd (REF01[80..90] · row 7) · TwnNm (REF06[0..40] · row 8)
  5. For each new node: add DMEE_TREE_COND row with empty-suppress (emit only if source NE space)
  6. Navigate to INSERT TARGET #2: Document > CstmrCdtTrfInitn > PmtInf > CdtTrfTxInf > Cdtr > PstlAdr
  7. Repeat the same 4 INSERTs (matrix rows 1–4) + 4 conditions
  8. Save → transport D01K-V001-SEPA-01 (single transport collects all 8 INSERTs + 8 conditions)
  9. Outside tx DMEE: SM30 → V_T042Z or direct entry into TFPM042FB → INSERT row FORMI=/SEPA_CT_UNES, EVENT=05, FNAME=FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_CGI_05 (matrix row 9). Save → transport D01K-V001-OBPM4-01

SEPA Step B verification: SELECT NODE_ID, MP_SC_FLD FROM DMEE_TREE_NODE WHERE TREE_ID='/SEPA_CT_UNES' AND VERSION='001' AND PARENT_ID IN ('<Dbtr/PstlAdr>','<Cdtr/PstlAdr>') returns original 5 V000 children + 8 new children. V000 query returns unchanged 5.

SEPA Step C · ACTIVATE V001 (Phase 5 cutover)

  1. tx DMEE → open /SEPA_CT_UNES → Menu: Tree → Versions → Activate Version → select VERSION=001 → confirm
  2. SAP flips DMEE_TREE_HEAD.EX_STATUS atomically: V000 → blank, V001 → 'A'
  3. Save → cutover transport D01K-V001-CUTOVER-01 (collects activation for all 4 trees together OR staggered per tree per claim 102 surgical philosophy)
  4. From this moment, every F110 SEPA run (SOG01 EUR, payment method S) produces V001 Fully Structured XML

SEPA rollback: same dialog, activate V000. Atomic flip back; F110 idempotent on REGUH.

SEPA code change required: NONE. All matrix rows 1–9 are customizing (DMEE_TREE_NODE, DMEE_TREE_COND, TFPM042FB).

CITI Step A · PURGE + CREATE

  1. tx DMEE → Tree type = PAYM + Format tree = /CITI/XML/UNESCO/DC_V3_01 → Display → confirm V000 (Active) + dormant V001 (Maintenance)
  2. Change → Maintenance version → Tree → Versions → Delete Version 001 → Save → transport D01K-RETROFIT-01-V001-PURGE (same retrofit transport as SEPA)
  3. Tree → Versions → Create Version 000 → 001 → Save → transport D01K-V001-CITI-01

CITI Step B · 2 INSERTs primary Dbtr + 5 INSERTs alt-Dbtr + 1 MODIFY UltmtCdtr/StrtNm + 1 INSERT UltmtCdtr/BldgNb + 2 INSERTs CdtrAgt

  1. Switch tree view to V001. Navigate to Dbtr-primary/PstlAdr: Document > CstmrCdtTrfInitn > PmtInf > Dbtr > PstlAdr (primary path)
  2. INSERT StrtNm (FPAYHX REF01[0..60] · matrix row 10) + BldgNb (FPAYHX REF01[60..80] · row 11). NO DMEE_TREE_COND needed — XSLT auto-removes empty.
  3. Navigate to Dbtr-altMor/PstlAdr (alternate path PstlAdrMor in same tree)
  4. INSERT 5 nodes (matrix rows 12–16): StrtNm, BldgNb, PstCd, TwnNm, Ctry — full structured subtree, since alt-mode currently has only 3 AdrLines
  5. Navigate to UltmtCdtr/PstlAdr: ... > CdtTrfTxInf > UltmtCdtr > PstlAdr
  6. MODIFY existing StrtNm node: double-click the empty StrtNm row → set MP_SC_TAB=FPAYH, MP_SC_FLD=ZSTRA, LENGTH=70 (matrix row 17, claim 99 — Worldlink BRL UltmtCdtr resolved system-driven)
  7. INSERT BldgNb under UltmtCdtr/PstlAdr (FPAYH ZSTRA[60..75] · matrix row 18)
  8. Navigate to CdtrAgt/.../PstlAdr: ... > CdtTrfTxInf > CdtrAgt > FinInstnId > PstlAdr
  9. INSERT PstCd (FPAYH ZBPST · matrix row 19) + BldgNb (FPAYH ZBSTR[60..] · row 20)
  10. Save → transport D01K-V001-CITI-01

CITI Step B verification: count of VERSION=001 nodes = 610 + 9 = 619. UltmtCdtr StrtNm node confirms MP_SC_FLD='ZSTRA' (was empty in V000). Run F110 simulator on a Worldlink BRL run to confirm UltmtCdtr/StrtNm now populates.

CITI Step C · ACTIVATE V001

  1. tx DMEE → open /CITI/XML/UNESCO/DC_V3_01 → Tree → Versions → Activate Version → 001 → confirm
  2. Save → cutover transport (recommended: stagger after SEPA cutover validates by ≥14 days)
  3. From cutover, every F110 CITI run (CIT01/CIT04/CIT21, payment methods L/R) produces V001 XML

CITI rollback: same dialog, activate V000. Atomic flip back.

CITI code change required: NONE. The /CITIPMW/V3_GET_CDTR_BLDG exit and CGI_XML_CT_XSLT post-processor are SAP-standard and unchanged. Pattern A guard does NOT apply to CITI (CITI does not use YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FALLBACK).

    WHEN '<PmtInf><CdtTrfTxInf><Cdtr><PstlAdr><StrtNm>'.
  IF i_fpayh = mv_fpayh
     AND mv_cdtr_name+35 IS NOT INITIAL
     AND c_value IS INITIAL.            " ← V001 GUARD: only prepend if StrtNm empty
    c_value = mv_cdtr_name+35.
  ELSEIF i_fpayh = mv_fpayh
     AND mv_cdtr_name+35 IS NOT INITIAL.
    c_value = |{ mv_cdtr_name+35 } { c_value }|.   " V000 legacy preserved
  ENDIF.
    Activate → transport prompt (Workbench K) → assign to D01K-BADI-FIX-01. Reviewer: N_MENARD.

End-to-End Flow Map — all components connected

Why a single end-to-end view exists

UNESCO's payment pipeline involves 32 distinct components across config tables, ABAP code, customer enhancements, vendor master data, and SAP-standard infrastructure. Until Phase 0 closed, no one had a single view that connected all of them — the knowledge lived in separate domain docs, separate transports, separate authors' heads. This tab is the result of "tenemos que conectar todos los elementos en un flow logico" (user directive 2026-04-25): one diagram, every component, with the V001-touched ones visually highlighted so reviewers can see the change footprint at a glance.

How to read the diagram

The flow runs top-to-bottom from F110 launching to the bank file landing on Alliance Lite2. At each stage, components are arranged horizontally if they fan out (e.g., the four DMEE trees fire in parallel for different countries). Color-coding tells you at a glance what V001 does to each component:

  • Teal fill — touched by V001. These are the ~24 nodes + 1 OBPM4 row + 5 vendor records changing.
  • Orange fill — Pattern A 3-line ABAP change. The only code touched. Backward-compatible guard.
  • Grey — out of scope. BCM workflow, Alliance Lite2, ICTP trees, etc. Touching anything grey means scope creep.
  • Default styling — components V001 reads from but does not modify (FPAYHX_FREF buffer, SAP-std country classes, FBZP customizing).

Read this in plain English: if you scan the diagram and see only a few teal/orange fills, that is the V001 footprint by design. Everything else stays as-is. The wide flow chart's purpose is to show how small the change actually is relative to the moving parts of the system.

Source: knowledge/domains/Payment/phase0/e2e_flow_components_connected.md

UNESCO BCM Structured Address — End-to-End Flow Map

Status (2026-04-29): ALL components connected — V001 design closed (Q1, Q1bis, Q3 resolved)

Per user directive 2026-04-25 "tenemos que conectar todos los elementos en un flow logico". This view shows the F110→Bank pipeline with V001-touched components highlighted in teal, Pattern A code change in orange, and out-of-scope components in grey.

Master Flow Diagram (per tree)

① F110 PAYMENT RUN

Inputs: open invoices, vendor master (LFA1+ADRC), payment methods, company code, run id.
Tx F110 · ~3,000 payments/week across 9 company codes (P01 process mining, 2025+2026Q1)
▼

② T042Z LOOKUP — country + payment method → tree

Resolves the FORMI (DMEE tree id) for each payment based on (LAND1, ZLSCH). XBKKT='X' marks DMEE-enabled rows.
263 rows in P01 (Phase 0 verified) · DATA · NOT touched by V001
▼

SEPA tree

/SEPA_CT_UNES
SocGen EUR · UNES, IIEP, UIL
V000: 95 nodes · 18 cond · UNSTRUCTURED Dbtr + Cdtr (only Ctry leaf in tree, no StrtNm/BldgNb/PstCd/TwnNm — claim 113 CBPR+ HARD-STOP)
V001: +5 Dbtr structured nodes + 5 empty-suppress conds + Sub-option A (Event 05 reg)

CGI tree

/CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO
SocGen non-SEPA, Shinhan KR, Metro GB, GT NG
V000: 631 nodes · 123 cond · Dbtr ✓ Cdtr ✓ CdtrAgt unstructured
V001: fix CdtrAgt (PstlAdr → structured StrtNm/PstCd/TwnNm/Ctry from T012K/BNKA)

CGI variant 1

/CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO_1
SYNC from parent (FIRSTNODE shared)
V000: 639 nodes · 123 cond · same as CGI
V001: SYNC from parent — CdtrAgt fix propagates automatically

CITI tree

/CITI/XML/UNESCO/DC_V3_01
Citi USD + Worldlink TND/MGA/BRL
V000: 610 nodes · 350 cond · Dbtr unstructured (no Ctry!) · Cdtr mostly Structured · UltmtCdtr Hybrid
V001: +5 Dbtr structured nodes + 1 UltmtCdtr StrtNm=FPAYH-ZSTRA (Q3 RESOLVED #62)
▼

③ EVENT 05 — OBPM4 (TFPM042FB) lookup

SAP looks up the registered FM for each tree's Event 05. The FM populates FPAYHX_FREF / FPAYP_FREF buffers from ADRC + BSEC + Z-tables.
SEPA → +1 row needed (V001) CGI → FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_CGI_05 (already registered) CGI_1 → FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_CGI_05 (same FM) CITI → /CITIPMW/V3_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_05 (CITI PMW IS)
▼

CGI/SEPA path: country factory

cl_idfi_cgi_call05_factory::get_instance resolves country (format → ubiso → ubnks) → CL_IDFI_CGI_CALL05_FR/DE/IT/GB or fallback CL_IDFI_CGI_CALL05_GENERIC.
SAP-std · NOT touched by V001

CITI path: direct ADDR_GET

Direct ADDR_GET via T001-ADRNR + ZADNR; one-time vendors via BSEC table.
SAP-std (CITIPMW) · NOT touched by V001
▼

④ BUFFER POPULATION — FPAYHX_FREF + FPAYP_FREF

Universal byte layout (same in GENERIC and CITIPMW V3) — V001 reads from these buffers, does not write to them.
  • REF01[0..60] = ADRC.STREET · [60..80] BUILDING · [80..90] POST_CODE1 · [90..100] REGION · [100..110] HOUSE_NUM1
  • REF06[0..40] = ADRC.CITY1
  • REF02 = Cdtr post_code2 + house_num1 (one-time vendor BSEC path)
  • FPAYP_FREF (5 fields REF01..REF05) — same Dbtr address per line
  • Country REF14 extras: FR=SIRET 16 chars · DE=SUN+SeqTp · IT=CUP+CIG+MGO · GB=bnkid+SeqTp · GENERIC writes nothing
DDIC structures · NOT touched by V001 (read-only consumers added in V001)
▼

⑤ DMEE TREE TRAVERSAL

SAP traverses the active version's nodes. V001 nodes deployed dormant in Phase 2; activation atomic in Phase 5.
  • V000 baseline: SEPA Hybrid · CITI Dbtr unstructured · CGI Dbtr structured ✓ CdtrAgt unstructured · CGI_1 SYNC
  • V001 deltas: SEPA +5 Dbtr · CITI +5 Dbtr +1 UltmtCdtr StrtNm · CGI fix CdtrAgt · CGI_1 SYNC
Per-node processing: MP_SC_TAB+MP_SC_FLD+MP_OFFSET (read source) · CV_RULE (CL/AL.2/RP) · MP_EXIT_FUNC (call BAdI/FM) · DMEE_TREE_COND (TECH switch nodes PSTLADRMOR1/2/3)
▼

⑥ BAdI FI_CGI_DMEE_EXIT_W_BADI

Fires on 794 of 1,975 nodes (40%). Country-dispatched to UNESCO impls.
  • YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FR · get_value() → PPC dispatcher (0 rows for FR — empty result)
  • YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_DE · get_credit() → SHELL: only ClrSysMmbId override
  • YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_IT · get_credit() → SHELL: same as DE
  • YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FALLBACK · get_credit() → ⚠ NAME-OVERFLOW BUG corrupts V001 StrtNm. Pattern A 3-line guard, reviewer N_MENARD.
  • YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_UTIL · utility class (PPC reader, helpers)
CITI tree extra layer (per-node EXIT_FUNC FMs, CITI-only): /CITIPMW/V3_CGI_CRED_STREET · _PO_CITY · _REGION · _GET_CDTR_BLDG · _EXIT_CGI_CRED_NAME · _CITY · _NM2 · _GET_BANKCODE · _CGI_REGULATORY_INF
▼

⑦ XML ASSEMBLED IN MEMORY — pain.001.001.03

  • <Dbtr><PstlAdr>...</PstlAdr></Dbtr> — UNESCO debtor
  • <Cdtr><PstlAdr>...</PstlAdr></Cdtr> — vendor
  • <CdtrAgt><FinInstnId><PstlAdr>...</PstlAdr></FinInstnId></CdtrAgt> — vendor's bank (CGI tree fix here in V001)
  • <UltmtCdtr><PstlAdr>...</PstlAdr></UltmtCdtr> — Worldlink only (CITI tree, V001 unified Q3)
▼

⑧a CITI tree → XSLT post-proc

CGI_XML_CT_XSLT (12 lines) removes empty leaf nodes, identity copy otherwise.
Effect: empty structured nodes auto-disappear → CITI V001 emits all 5 Dbtr nodes unconditionally · SAP-std XSLT, NOT touched by V001

⑧b SEPA + CGI trees → no XSLT

Empty structured nodes emitted as-is unless DMEE_TREE_COND explicitly suppresses them.
→ V001 SEPA design adds COND rules per node ('source field NE space'). CGI's CdtrAgt nodes use existing TECH switch.
▼

⑨ FILE WRITE

Output path: \\hq-sapitf\SWIFT$\P01\input\aaaa_bbbb_ccxxxxxxxxyyyy.in
  • aaaa = company code (UNES / IIEP / UIL / ...)
  • bbbb = payment method (S / N / J / L / X / ...)
  • cc = format (001=pain.001.001.02 · 002=mt101 · 003=pain.001.001.03)
  • xxxxxxxx = date · yyyy = sequence
▼

⑩ BCM BATCH (Bank Communication Management)

  • Routing: 100% F110+payroll via OBPM5/TFIBLMPAYBLOCK (Claim #65)
  • Workflow 90000003: dual control approval
  • Signatories: PD objects OTYPE='RY' (Claim #42/43)
  • Status: IBC05 (Sent to Bank)
Out of scope — V001 changes XML content only, BCM workflow untouched
▼

⑪ ALLIANCE LITE2 → SWIFT → Bank

SocGen / Citi / CGI-routed banks (Shinhan, Metro, GT NG, etc.)
External SWIFT delivery — NOT touched by V001

Total surgical change scope

ABAP: 1 method (YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FALLBACK_CM001::GET_CREDIT), 3 lines (Pattern A guard) · transport D01K-BADI-FIX-01 · reviewer N_MENARD.

CONFIG (CUSTOMIZING):

- TFPM042FB: +1 row for SEPA Event 05 registration (Sub-option A)

- DMEE V001 trees (~24 nodes total):

- SEPA: +5 Dbtr structured nodes + 5 COND rules to suppress empty

- CITI: +5 Dbtr structured nodes (XSLT auto-removes empty) + 1 UltmtCdtr StrtNm node (Q3 RESOLVED #62)

- CGI: fix CdtrAgt (PstlAdr from AdrLine to structured StrtNm/PstCd/TwnNm/Ctry, ~7 nodes)

- CGI_1: SYNC from parent (FIRSTNODE shared, 0 manual nodes)

DATA: 5 vendor master cleanup (LFA1/ADRC).

Risk: LOW. All changes either additive (V001 new, V000 untouched), backward-compatible (Pattern A guarded), or data-only (vendor cleanup).

Components Map — config + code + data (31 components)

Why a "components map" instead of a flow chart

The E2E Flow tab shows when each component fires (the runtime sequence). This tab shows what each component is in catalog form: type (config / code / data / DDIC), ownership (UNESCO custom or SAP standard), V001 impact, and key properties. Think of it as the parts list: if E2E Flow is the wiring diagram, this is the bill of materials. Each row is one entity that lives in a specific table or has a specific transport-traceable identity.

How to read the table below

The 31 rows split into 5 categories, each with its own color in the header chips:

  • CONFIG — DMEE tree nodes, conditions, OBPM customizing, FBZP rules. Customizing transports.
  • CODE (UNESCO) — Y-prefix BAdI implementations and Z-prefix exits, owned by N_MENARD / UNESCO team. Workbench transports.
  • CODE (SAP std) — SAP-delivered classes, FMs, BAdIs. Never modified, only consumed.
  • DDIC — DDIC structures (FPAY*, T012K, etc.) referenced by the tree at runtime.
  • DATA — master-data tables (LFA1, ADRC, T015L) consulted at runtime but not part of customizing.

The "V001 change" column at the right says one of three things for each row: a specific delta (e.g., "+5 Dbtr structured nodes"), NO CHANGE (V000 untouched, regression-protected), or NO DIRECT CHANGE (component is read by V001 but its definition does not change). Use this column to scan the regression boundary fast.

Last update: 2026-04-25 — CITIPMW V3 extracted, byte layout confirmed identical to GENERIC · Source of truth: knowledge/domains/Payment/phase0/components_map.json

Color legend: CONFIG   CODE (UNESCO)   CODE (SAP std)   DDIC   DATA

Cardinality cheat-sheet (per claim 101 / e2e_flow_components_connected.md): T042Z routes 1:N to trees · TFPM042FB N:1 to Event 05 FMs (one FM serves CGI + CGI_1, another for CITI, V001 adds one for SEPA) · Event 05 FMs 1:1 to FACTORY (CGI path) · FACTORY 1:N to country classes · GENERIC writes 1:1 into FPAYHX_FREF (universal byte layout — claim 101 confirms CITIPMW V3 byte-identical) · Buffers M:N to trees (each tree reads many buffer fields) · BAdI 1:N to country implementations · Pattern A is a stateful coupling on FALLBACK only. The companion table below has full per-edge evidence.

Current Solution — what is actually wired and firing in P01 today

Why this section exists

The E2E Flow tab shows the runtime machinery (what can happen). The Components Map shows the moving parts (what is built). This tab answers a third, very practical question: of all the DMEE format trees declared in the system, which ones are actually called by F110 today, and which are just sitting there unused?

Knowing the difference matters for V001 scoping (don't risk tests on inactive trees), regression budgeting (less surface = less risk), and decommissioning (inactive trees are tech-debt candidates). Anyone reading the OBPM1 catalog will see ~12 custom UNESCO/ICTP format names and assume they are all in use. They are not.

The proof — T042Z, the routing table

T042Z is the SAP-standard routing table that maps (country LAND1, payment method ZLSCH) → format ID FORMI (where FORMI = the OBPM1 format name = the DMEE TREE_ID, per the invariant we covered earlier). If a format has no T042Z entry, F110 will never invoke it, regardless of whether OBPM1 declares it or DMEE_TREE_HEAD stores nodes for it. T042Z is the single deterministic source of truth for "is this format wired to anything?"

Source query (Gold DB p01_gold_master_data.db):

SELECT FORMI, LAND1, ZLSCH, XBKKT, TEXT1
FROM T042Z
WHERE FORMI LIKE '/%UNES%' OR FORMI LIKE '/%CITI%' OR FORMI LIKE '/CGI%'
   OR FORMI LIKE '/SEPA%' OR FORMI LIKE '/CHECK%' OR FORMI LIKE '/CMI%'
ORDER BY FORMI, LAND1, ZLSCH;

Result: 19 routing rows across 8 distinct custom formats. Compare with OBPM1 catalog which shows 12+ custom formats declared. 4 custom formats are declared in OBPM1 but have ZERO T042Z routing — they are inactive.

The 3-tier reality of UNESCO custom DMEE formats

Read this before the tables → A format being declared in OBPM1 + having a tree in DMEE_TREE_HEAD is not proof of activity. Activity = an entry in T042Z. The 3 tiers below sort UNESCO custom formats by their T042Z presence: actively wired and in V001 scope · actively wired but out of V001 scope · declared but unused (decommissioning candidates).

▸ Tier 1 — UNESCO V001 active (the 4 trees the project actually changes)

Consistency check: D01 vs P01 node counts. Source: knowledge/domains/Payment/h18_dmee_d01_vs_p01_comparison.csv + h18 findings (2026-04-06). When D01 has substantially more nodes than P01, it means D01 carries untransported draft versions never released to production. Only P01 is the trustworthy source for live config analysis (per existing brain rule).

Reading the diff column (REVISED (RFC verification 2026-04-30, claims 109 + 111 + 112)): The original h18 baseline (2026-04-06) framing of "2× drift" is REPLACED by precise RFC verification. D01's apparent "2× node count" is exactly VERSION=000 + VERSION=001 cohabitation — V001 is a byte-identical clone of V000 created via DMEE Tx → Create Version dormantly (claim 109). Full 48-field byte-level RFC diff confirms SEPA / CITI / CGI all 3 are BYTE-EQUAL D01=P01 (zero deltas each); only CGI_1 has 12 deltas. Retrofit scope is therefore ~1-2h surgical (12 CGI_1 nodes + dormant V001 PURGE on all 4 trees + 5 P01-only ABAP retrofit), NOT the originally-feared multi-tree retrofit.

⚠ Open finding — `/CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO_1` reconciliation needed → Brain claim 102 + the V001 versioning procedure list this as one of 4 V001-scope trees. But T042Z has zero rows referencing it. It does exist in DMEE_TREE_HEAD with 639 nodes (P01) and shares the FIRSTNODE_ID with its parent /CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO. Three plausible explanations: (a) it is a draft/legacy peer that never got production-routed (most likely — making it tech debt, not V001 scope); (b) a different routing mechanism we have not extracted (unlikely — T042Z is the canonical source); (c) implicit invocation via shared FIRSTNODE_ID (possible but undocumented). Action item: confirm with M_SPRONK whether this format was historically routed and if so where; then either remove from V001 scope or document the implicit-routing mechanism. Either way, the brain claim 102 needs a "caveat: 1 of 4 trees has no T042Z routing" note.
