Trees marked "not in h18" either (a) have empty DMEE_TREE_HEAD entries (skeleton), (b) use a different TREE_TYPE, or (c) are declared in OBPM1 but never had nodes built. Tier 1 D01 evidence is now COMPLETE per claim 109/111/112 RFC verification . Tier 2/3 D01 extraction remains de-prioritized — out of V001 scope, no operational signal for retrofit.

How does SAP decide which format to call? — the combination of factors

The user-friendly answer to "which DMEE tree fires for a given payment?" is: not one factor, but a deterministic combination. We worked this out in the FBZP Chain tab + components_map + e2e_flow earlier; this is the recap focused on format selection specifically.

The 5 inputs SAP combines per payment

FactorSourceRole in format selection
① Vendor's bank country LFBK.BANKS (vendor master, vendor's bank record) → also reachable as FPAYH-ZBNKS at runtime Becomes the LAND1 input to T042Z lookup. A French vendor with a French bank → LAND1=FR. The vendor's bank country (not the cocode's country) is what drives the routing.
② Payment method BSEG.ZLSCH on the invoice OR vendor's LFB1.ZWELS default · single-letter code (S/N/J/L/X/A/C…) Becomes the ZLSCH input to T042Z lookup. S = SEPA, C = check, N = international wire, etc. Country + method together identify the format unambiguously.
③ Paying company code T042.ZBUKR for cocode → ABSBU mapping · invoice's BUKRS may differ from ZBUKR (cross-cocode IHC) Does not change FORMI (the format), but determines which OBPM4 selection variant fires (file path, file naming, output flags). Same format can be written to different paths per cocode.
④ House bank chosen T012/T012K via FBZP optimization (cocode rules) OR vendor override LFB1.HBKID Does not change FORMI either. Determines the <DbtrAcct> / <DbtrAgt> content inside the file, but the file format itself is the same.
⑤ Currency Invoice currency from BKPF/BSEG · vendor allowed currencies via T042S May filter out (LAND1, ZLSCH) combinations that aren't allowed for a currency — e.g., FR/L is "Payment in US in USD only", FR/X is "non-standard currency". Currency steers which T042Z row matches when multiple are eligible.

The deterministic formula

FORMAT (DMEE TREE_ID) = T042Z[ vendor.LFBK.BANKS , (invoice.ZLSCH OR vendor.LFB1.ZWELS) ]
                       └────────── ① ──────────┘  └─────────── ② ──────────────────┘
                                  WHERE T042Z.XBKKT = 'X' (DMEE-flagged)

OBPM4 selection variant = TFPM042F[ paying_cocode , FORMAT ]
                                  └──── ③ ────┘
                                  → file path, output flags

DbtrAgt content       = T012K[ paying_cocode , chosen_HBKID ] joined to BNKA
                                              └──── ④ ────┘ (FBZP optimization or LFB1 override)

Currency filter       ⑤ further filters T042Z eligibility when ZLSCH has multi-currency variants

Worked example — vendor 200135 invoice in FR for SEPA payment

Take a real-world payment: French vendor with a French bank, EUR invoice, payment method S (SEPA), paying cocode UNES, default house bank FB00.

  1. ① LAND1 = FR (from vendor bank country)
  2. ② ZLSCH = S (SEPA — vendor's default or invoice override)
  3. T042Z[FR, S] = /SEPA_CT_UNES ← the format / DMEE TREE_ID
  4. ③ Paying cocode UNES → look up TFPM042F[UNES, /SEPA_CT_UNES] → file path \\hq-sapitf\SWIFT$\P01\input\UNES_S_001…
  5. ④ Chosen house bank FB00 → T012K[UNES, FB00] → bank account details written into <DbtrAcct>
  6. ⑤ Currency EUR matches T042Z row eligibility (no further filter)
  7. SAPFPAYM writes the file using /SEPA_CT_UNES tree, with FB00 details inside, to the UNES-specific path.

The user's instinct was right: the format selection is a combination of vendor data (bank country, allowed methods), invoice data (method, currency), and cocode/house-bank config — but only the first two factors actually enter the T042Z key. The other three shape what goes into the file and where the file lands, not which format SAP picks.

⛔ CRITICAL RISK — D01 carries draft cohabitation, P01 must be source of truth

Brain claim 108 TIER_1 · CRITICAL feedback rule feedback_p01_source_of_truth_retrofit_first_then_adjust · user directive 2026-04-30.

UPDATED (post-VPN RFC verification 2026-04-30, claim 109) — the original framing of "draft cohabitation" is REPLACED by precise diagnosis:

The 2× node count in D01 is exact V000+V001 cohabitation: D01 has DMEE_TREE_NODE.VERSION=000 rows AND VERSION=001 rows for all 4 in-scope trees. P01 has only V000. Someone ran DMEE Tx → Create Version on each tree, producing a byte-identical V001 clone of V000, then never edited or released it. Verified RFC counts: SEPA D01(V000=95, V001=95) P01(95); CITI D01(610, 610) P01(610); CGI D01(631, 631) P01(631); CGI_1 D01(632, 632) P01(639). D01 V001 is byte-identical to D01 V000 — zero NODE_ID differences, zero field diffs in 7 sampled columns.

RETROFIT SCOPE DRAMATICALLY REDUCED: D01 V000 vs P01 V000 row-level diff (full RFC 2026-04-30): SEPA / CITI / CGI all BYTE-EQUAL (zero deltas each). Only CGI_1 has 12 deltas: 1 ONLY_D01 (N_6366307580 SCB), 8 ONLY_P01 (8 AdrLine variants), 3 CHANGED (1 substantive Nm Z-field experiment + 2 BROTHER_ID consequential). The ~30-minute surgical fix on CGI_1 + dormant-V001 cleanup replaces the original "huge multi-tree retrofit" framing.

Why this is a HUGE risk for V001 deployment

Failure modeWhat happens if we apply V001 to D01 today (without retrofit)
Wrong-layer landingV001 change-matrix rows target P01 NODE_IDs (e.g. N_4754354180 SEPA Cdtr PstlAdr). In D01 there are TWO PstlAdr nodes per branch (one in each layer). Marlies's edit may attach to the draft sibling, not the P01-mirror.
Transport pollutionSE09 transport packing may pull the draft nodes alongside our V001 deltas. The transport ships TO P01 and silently introduces the unfinished WIP someone built years ago.
Developer confusionM_SPRONK opens DMEE Tx in D01 and sees nodes she does not recognize. Pattern A guard, FALLBACK BAdI fix may misbehave on the draft layer.
UAT divergencePhase 4 UAT runs in V01 (which inherits D01 via transport). If D01 carries drafts, V01 ≠ P01. Bank acceptance test on V01 does not prove P01 will accept.
Simulator gapSimulator (claim 105, 794/794 PASS) reads P01 data. It cannot detect a D01-side draft-layer corruption. XSD validation cannot either.

Why simulator + XSD do NOT cover this risk: simulator validates the P01-derived V001 design works against XSD. It cannot tell you whether the D01 environment where you deploy V001 is byte-equal to P01. That second question is purely a transport-management question that lives outside the schema layer.

✅ The protocol — P01 source of truth → D01 retrofit → only then adjust

Invariant sequence (any deviation = CRITICAL risk per the new feedback rule):

  1. P01 snapshot — extract current P01 state of all 4 in-scope trees (DMEE_TREE_HEAD + DMEE_TREE_NODE + DMEE_TREE_COND + TFPM042FB rows + 5 ABAP P01-only objects per Finding I) and record byte hashes per object. Source-of-truth manifest produced.
  2. D01 retrofit (transport D01K-RETROFIT-01) — bring D01 to byte-equality with the P01 manifest. Two options:
    • Option A · PURGE then re-import P01 (recommended): in DMEE Tx → delete the entire UNESCO custom tree set in D01, re-import the P01 versions via transport from P01 → D01 (or via TR_RELEASE+TR_IMPORT roundtrip). Smallest blast radius, no per-node decisions, end-state guaranteed clean.
    • Option B · Surgical diff: per-tree, list every D01-only node, classify as (a) keep — was a real WIP and we want to preserve it vs (b) purge — abandoned WIP. Build a transport that deletes all "purge" nodes and promotes all "keep" nodes to P01. High effort, high value only if there is a known intentional draft we must keep.
  3. Verification — re-extract D01 state, recompute byte hashes, must match P01 manifest. Node counts must match exactly: SEPA 95, CGI 631, CGI_1 639, CITI 610. If not equal → retrofit incomplete, fix before proceeding.
  4. 5 P01-only ABAP objects retrofit (Finding I) — pull YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_DE, _IT classes + 3 ENHO spots + the YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FR::CM002 method via P01→D01 transport (or RPY_CLASS_INSERT). Re-verify hashes.
  5. NOW apply the V001 change matrix (29 rows: 2 preconditions + 27 deltas, see V001 Change Matrix tab) to the now-aligned D01 baseline.
  6. Per-row verification — for every V001 row, after the DMEE Tx Save, the new transport's E071 must contain ONLY the planned delta — no accidental draft-layer pull.
  7. Test → V01 → P01 per the standard transport flow.

Recommendation: Option A (purge + re-import). Rationale: surgical-pattern (claim 102 — 81.8% of historical UNESCO transports touch ≤3 objects) makes per-node Option B effort disproportionate; V001 Fully-Structured commitment (claim 105) means the draft layer adds no design value we cannot reproduce from P01 + the change matrix; the simulator (claim 105) already validated V001 design against P01 data, so a clean P01-derived D01 baseline is exactly what the simulator results presume.

✅ RESOLVED (2026-04-30, post-VPN restoration)

  • CITI tree D01 extracted — RFC verification 2026-04-30: D01 V000=610 nodes + V001=610 nodes (dormant byte-clone). D01 V000 vs P01 V000 = BYTE-EQUAL across all 48 fields × 610 nodes (claim 112). Prediction confirmed: same V000+V001 cohabitation pattern as SEPA/CGI/CGI_1.
  • D01 hash manifest produced — full 48-field RFC diff for SEPA + CITI + CGI + CGI_1 saved at Zagentexecution/incidents/xml_payment_structured_address/full_47field_diff_session63.json. SHA-256 byte-level verification done for SEPA: 033f11ce1798ed90cdae447c0f4feaeddc03445c37885487e8adc4a447345b39.
  • Decision A (PURGE dormant V001 + re-create fresh) recommended for retrofit transport D01K-RETROFIT-01 — clean transport-trail, no per-node decisions, end-state guaranteed clean. Awaiting Marlies + Pablo final confirm before Phase 2 Step 0.
  • 5 P01-only ABAP objects (Finding I) — already documented and queued for D01-RETROFIT-01. Scope unchanged but now bundled with the tree retrofit in one transport.

📌 Phase 2 readiness — Step 0 elevated to TOP gating blocker

Per claim 108 + new CRITICAL rule, the Phase 2 readiness checklist now ranks D01-RETROFIT-01 above VPN restoration: VPN unblocks the retrofit, but the retrofit itself is the gating prerequisite for any V001 row landing in D01. The original Phase 2 §Step 0 scope (5 P01-only ABAP objects per Finding I) is preserved, expanded to include the full byte-alignment of all 4 in-scope DMEE trees. Reference: knowledge/domains/Payment/phase2_readiness_checklist.md · knowledge/domains/Payment/dmee_versioning_procedure.md Step 0 prerequisite section to be added.

Where each factor is configured — the Tx / IMG / table cheat-sheet

Why this section exists. The deterministic formula above is precise but the inputs live in five different places in SAP. Knowing the formula without knowing where to inspect each input is half the picture. This is complex to absorb in one read; come back to this section when debugging "why is payment X going to format Y?" — each factor has its own Tx + IMG + table reference so you can pinpoint the disagreeing layer in 60 seconds.

① Vendor's bank country (LAND1 input to T042Z)

WhereDetail
Tx codesFK02 / XK02 (vendor master change) · BP (Business Partner — S/4 unified) · FK03 / XK03 (display only)
Tab to open"Payment transactions" → "Bank Details" sub-tab
FieldBank Country = column BANKS in table LFBK (vendor's bank record). At F110 runtime resolves to FPAYH-ZBNKS.
TablesLFBK (vendor bank — keys: vendor, bank country, bank key, account)
SPRO IMGNot customizing — this is master data per vendor, not config.
Common gotchaVendor with multiple bank records: the F110 picks the one whose currency matches the invoice + vendor's "partner bank type" hint. Wrong bank country here = wrong format. Check via FK03 → Banking → Bank Details.

② Payment method (ZLSCH input to T042Z)

WhereDetail
Tx codesFK02 (vendor default) · FB60 / F-43 (invoice — can override) · FBL1N (line items — view current)
Vendor defaultLFB1.ZWELS — string of allowed payment methods per (cocode, vendor). E.g. "SNJ" = vendor accepts S, N, or J.
Invoice overrideBSEG.ZLSCH — single chosen method on the invoice line. Takes precedence over vendor default.
Country definitionTx OBVCU (FBZP "Pmt method in country") — defines what each single-letter code means in each country (S = SEPA, C = check, etc.). This is also where the "Use Payment Medium Workbench" radio button + the PMW format name live — and the format name === DMEE TREE_ID.
Cocode definitionTx OBVU (FBZP "Pmt method in cocode") — declares which methods this cocode supports + amount limits + the FPAYM_INT_DMEE form-routing field (see FBZP Chain tab).
SPRO IMGFI → AR/AP → Business Transactions → Outgoing Payments → Automatic Outgoing Payments → Payment Method/Bank Selection for Payment Program → Set Up Payment Methods per Country + Set Up Payment Methods per Cocode

⓪ The T042Z routing itself (the lookup table)

WhereDetail
Tx codesOBVCU (FBZP "Pmt method in country") — the GUI on top of T042Z. Filling in the FORMI field on this screen creates a T042Z row.
Direct table viewSE16N → table T042Z · 263 rows in P01 · key columns: LAND1, ZLSCH · result column: FORMI
Companion sourceGold DB p01_gold_master_data.db, table T042Z — query in this tab earlier shows all UNESCO-relevant rows.
Common gotchaThe XBKKT='X' flag must be set for DMEE-routing rows. Without it, FORMI is set but SAP routes via the legacy code-based PMW path even if a DMEE tree exists with the same name.

③ Paying company code (drives OBPM4 variant + file path)

WhereDetail
Tx codesOBVCU + OBVU (FBZP "Paying cocodes") · FBZP top-level menu
Cocode-to-paying-cocodeTable T042 — column BUKRS = invoice cocode, ZBUKR = paying cocode. Cross-cocode IHC scenarios use this.
OBPM4 variant per (cocode, format)Tx OBPM4 · table TFPM042F family · 311 rows in P01 · binds (paying-cocode, format) → SAPFPAYM selection variant → file-name pattern + output flags
SPRO IMGFI → AR/AP → Business Transactions → Outgoing Payments → Automatic Outgoing Payments → Payment Method/Bank Selection for Payment Program → Set Up Paying Company Codes · then Payment Media → Make Settings for Payment Medium Formats from Payment Medium Workbench → Create/Assign Selection Variants

④ House bank chosen (drives DbtrAcct / DbtrAgt content inside the file)

WhereDetail
House-bank masterTx FI12 (House Bank maintenance) · table T012 = house banks per cocode · table T012K = house bank accounts (211 / 402 rows in P01)
Bank-determination rulesTx FBZP → "Bank Determination" → 5 sub-screens: Ranking Order · Bank Accounts · Available Amounts · Value Date · Expenses/Charges
Vendor overrideLFB1.HBKID — when set, forces a specific house bank for that (cocode, vendor) combination, bypassing the FBZP optimization rules
SPRO IMGFI → Bank Accounting → Bank Accounts → Define House Banks · plus FBZP → Bank Determination
Common gotchaFBZP "Bank selection control" on the (cocode, payment method) screen (No optimization / Optimize by bank group / Optimize by postal code) changes which house bank wins when multiple are eligible. UNESCO setting is mostly "No optimization" — meaning vendor's LFB1.HBKID override or first-eligible wins.

⑤ Currency (filters which T042Z row is eligible when multiple match)

WhereDetail
Invoice currencyBKPF.WAERS + BSEG.WAERS on each line item · entered at invoice posting (FB60 etc.)
Allowed currencies per (cocode, method)Tx OBVU "Foreign payments" tab → flags Foreign currency allowed + Foreign business partner allowed
Format-level currency restrictionSome T042Z rows narrow by description (TEXT1) — e.g. FR/L "Payment in US in USD only", FR/X "non-standard currency". The narrowing is captured in TEXT1 metadata + enforced via FBZP foreign-payment flags.
SPRO IMGSame as ②, the cocode-method config screens

Reading order suggestion when debugging

"Why did this payment go to format X (or fail to find a format)?" — open these screens in this order:

  1. Tx FK03 vendor master (factor ① + ②) — confirm bank country and allowed payment methods.
  2. Tx FB03 invoice document — confirm ZLSCH on the line item + currency.
  3. Tx OBVCU country payment methods (factor ⓪) — find the row matching (LAND1, ZLSCH); confirm FORMI populated and XBKKT='X'.
  4. Tx DMEE → open the FORMI tree; confirm VERSION=000 EX_STATUS='A'.
  5. Tx OBPM4 (factor ③) — confirm a selection variant exists for (paying-cocode, FORMI). No variant → no file even though steps 1-4 succeed.
  6. Tx FI12 + FBZP Bank Determination (factor ④) — confirm house bank resolution is producing a valid bank.
  7. Tx FBZP cocode-method screen (factor ⑤) — if the run rejected on currency, the foreign-payment flags here are the gate.

7 screens, 5 factors, 1 deterministic outcome. A massive improvement over "let's tail F110 logs and hope". This is the canonical playbook to bookmark.

The deterministic chain — how to predict which tree fires for any payment

For any given payment, the chain that decides which DMEE tree is invoked is fully deterministic. Walking it is the only reliable way to answer "which tree will this payment hit?":

F110 inputs: (paying-cocode, payment method, vendor, country)
       │
       ▼  ① T042Z lookup
T042Z routing  ── (LAND1 + ZLSCH) → FORMI                          [263 rows in P01]
       │       (XBKKT='X' marks DMEE-enabled rows)
       ▼  ② OBPM1 catalog (T042Y / T042YB)
OBPM1 ── confirms format exists + DME-engine flag = ON             [evidence: erp_obpm1_*.png]
       + event modules wired (FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_*)
       + format name === DMEE TREE_ID (the invariant)
       │
       ▼  ③ DMEE_TREE_HEAD
DMEE_TREE_HEAD ── tree exists with VERSION=000, EX_STATUS='A'      [4 UNESCO + 4 ICTP rows]
       │
       ▼  ④ OBPM4 (TFPM042F)
OBPM4 selection variant ── exists for (paying-cocode, format)      [311 rows in P01]
       │       + carries file path + Output-to-file-system flag
       ▼
File written via SAPFPAYM driver.

Read this in plain English: SAP first asks T042Z "given this country and payment method, which format do I use?". If T042Z returns nothing, F110 cannot pay. If it returns a format, SAP confirms in OBPM1 that the format exists and is DMEE-flagged, looks up the actual tree in DMEE_TREE_HEAD, finds an OBPM4 variant with file-output settings, and finally writes the file. Break any one of these steps and the chain fails.

Per-tree current state — how each DMEE tree is structured today (V000)

Before talking about what V001 changes, this section captures how the 4 in-scope DMEE trees are wired and behaving in P01 today. The V001 deltas (in the Change Strategy → DMEE Configuration tab) only make sense once you can see V000 baseline. Each tree's subsection below covers: the actual tree structure as tx DMEE Display shows it, the tree-level tab settings (Format attributes / Levels / Sort-key / File Data / Post Processing), and the hierarchy stratification (how many nodes total vs how many actually carry data).

Background — the 6 tabs on the DMEE Display Format Tree screen

tx DMEE → Display Format Tree always shows 6 tabs: Administrative data · Format attributes · Levels · Sort/key fields · File Data · Post Processing. They govern how a tree behaves at runtime — the bind to ABAP source structures, the nesting depth, sort/grouping, character validation, and what happens to empty XML elements. These settings are tree-level, not node-level. They are part of the V000 contract and survive into V001 unchanged unless explicitly touched.

One tab setting matters disproportionately for V001: Post Processing → Empty Element Processing. If set to "Do Not Remove" (as in /SEPA_CT_UNES, claim 120), empty XML tags ARE emitted to the file. V001 INSERTs that bind to source fields which can be empty for some payments must therefore carry per-node DMEE_TREE_COND empty-suppress conditions. CITI uses XSLT post-processing instead (CGI_XML_CT_XSLT auto-removes empty leaves) so DMEE_TREE_COND is not needed. CGI / CGI_1 settings TBD Phase 2 verification.

Tree 1 of 4 · /SEPA_CT_UNES current state

95 nodes V000 · pain.001.001.03 · SocGen SEPA-zone EUR (SOG01 method S) · 1,703-payment batches per cycle (claim 113). Empty Element Processing = "Do Not Remove" → empty tags emitted as-is.

SEPA tree structure (ASCII view of tx DMEE Display)
DMEE tree: properties
└── Document
    ├── xmlns (ISO, Para)
    ├── xmlns:xsi (ISO, Para)
    ├── xsi:schemaLocation
    └── CstmrCdtTrfInitn                  ← root of the credit-transfer message
        ├── GrpHdr                        ← message-level header (1 per file)
        │   ├── MsgId
        │   ├── CreDtTm (YYYY-MM-DDTtime)
        │   ├── NbOfTxs
        │   ├── CtrlSum
        │   └── InitgPty
        │       └── Nm (AUST1, NAMEZ)     ← UNESCO identity, message-level
        └── PmtInf                        ← payment-instruction batch (1 per run)
            ├── PmtInfId
            ├── PmtMtd
            ├── NbOfTxs  (TX2)
            ├── CtrlSum  (IA2)
            ├── PmtTpInf → SvcLvl/Cd
            ├── ReqdExctnDt
            ├── Dbtr     ← BATCH-LEVEL DEBTOR (UNESCO at PmtInf level)
            │   ├── Nm
            │   └── PstlAdr (Ctry, AdrLine)   ← path: Document > CstmrCdtTrfInitn > PmtInf > Dbtr > PstlAdr
            ├── DbtrAcct → Id/IBAN, Ccy
            ├── DbtrAgt → FinInstnId/BIC
            ├── ChrgBr
            └── CdtTrfTxInf  (TX)         ← PER-TRANSACTION block (1 per payment)
                ├── PmtId → InstrId (DOC1T-DOC1R(1..rest)), EndToEndId (PAYD2/NOTPROVIDED)
                ├── Amt → InstdAmt (IA), Ccy
                ├── UltmtDbtr → Nm        ← Name only — no PstlAdr (intentional)
                ├── CdtrAgt → FinInstnId/BIC   ← Bank — BIC only (IBAN routing)
                ├── Cdtr      ← BENEFICIARY at CdtTrfTxInf level
                │   ├── Nm (KOINH, ZNME1)      ← Name = concatenation of 2 leaf atoms
                │   └── PstlAdr (Ctry, AdrLine, AdrLine) ← path: Document > CstmrCdtTrfInitn > PmtInf > CdtTrfTxInf > Cdtr > PstlAdr
                ├── CdtrAcct → Id/IBAN
                ├── UltmtCdtr → Nm        ← Name only — no PstlAdr (intentional)
                └── RmtInf

Three structural details to anchor:
(1) <PstlAdr> appears twice in this tree — once at PmtInf level (UNESCO HQ for the whole batch) and once at CdtTrfTxInf level (per-transaction beneficiary). Different parents, independently configured.
(2) <UltmtDbtr> and <UltmtCdtr> only carry <Nm> — no PstlAdr branch. ISO 20022 permits identifying a party by name alone for ultimate-debtor / ultimate-creditor.
(3) <Cdtr><Nm> has two leaf atoms — KOINH (account-holder name from bank-master) and ZNME1 (UNESCO custom Z-name field). The Name produced is a concatenation, not a single bind.

tree_top.png — Document → CstmrCdtTrfInitn → GrpHdr (with InitgPty/Nm AUST1+NAMEZ) → start of PmtInf.
tree_mid.png — PmtInf body: Dbtr/PstlAdr (Ctry+AdrLine), DbtrAcct, DbtrAgt/BIC, CdtTrfTxInf entry.
tree_bottom.png — CdtTrfTxInf: UltmtDbtr/Nm, CdtrAgt/BIC, Cdtr/Nm (KOINH+ZNME1) + Cdtr/PstlAdr, CdtrAcct/IBAN, UltmtCdtr/Nm, RmtInf.
SEPA — visual anchor: Dbtr/PstlAdr selected (V001 INSERT entry point #1)
unesco_dmee_dbtr_pstladr_highlighted.png — Dbtr/PstlAdr selected. The operator clicked through PmtInf → Dbtr → PstlAdr; the orange highlight + arrow marker shows the current selection. Children (Ctry, AdrLine) at indentation depth 5 in the UI = nesting depth 5 in the XML output.
SEPA — the 6 tabs detail (V000 settings)

Tab 1 (Administrative data): Tree type=PAYM, Format tree=/SEPA_CT_UNES, Version=0, Author M_SPRONK, Created 27.11.2013, Last Changed 23.11.2021. Operationally frozen 4+ years.

Tab 2 · Format attributes — binding to the ABAP runtime structure
format_attributes.png — Fmt-spec.strct = FPM_SEPA. The DMEE engine glues to ABAP via FPM_SEPA at the top + FPAYH/FPAYHX/FPAYP at per-node level. "Without accompanying sheet" — electronic-only, no paper.
Tab 3 · Levels — nesting depth + repetition
levels.png — Level 0 = 9,999,999 · Level 1 = 1 (one CstmrCdtTrfInitn per file) · Level 2 = 9,999,999 (PmtInf unlimited) · Level 3 = 9,999,999 (CdtTrfTxInf unlimited per PmtInf). This is what supports 1,703-payment batches.
Tab 4 · Sort/key fields — payment grouping
sort_key.png — 4 keys all from FPAYH: ZBUKR (Level 1) · AUSFD + HKTID (Level 2) · DOC1R (Level 3). F110 sorts open invoices by company code → date → house bank → document reference, then writes them into XML in that order.
Tab 5 · File Data — character validation
file_data.png — Disallowed chars: ^"$%&{}=`~!?º'+*\.:;,_()[]#<>. Engine sanitises field values before emission to match SocGen's pain.001 character whitelist.
Tab 6 · Post Processing (the load-bearing one)
post_processing.png — Empty Element Processing = "Do Not Remove" · XSLT Program empty. Empty tags ARE emitted. This is why V001 INSERTs need per-node DMEE_TREE_COND empty-suppress conditions (claim 120).
SEPA — the hierarchy collapse (95 nodes stratified)

tx DMEE shows /SEPA_CT_UNES with 95 rows. It looks like a lot — it isn't, because the tree is a hierarchy, not a flat list. Stratified by depth level:

LevelWhat lives hereApprox node count
0DMEE tree: properties root1
1Document + namespace declarations~5
2CstmrCdtTrfInitn1
3GrpHdr + PmtInf2
4GrpHdr children (5) + PmtInf children including Dbtr (~11)~16
5Inside Dbtr: Nm + PstlAdr. Inside CdtTrfTxInf: PmtId, Amt, UltmtDbtr, CdtrAgt, Cdtr, CdtrAcct, UltmtCdtr, RmtInf (~10)~12
6Inside Dbtr/PstlAdr: Ctry, AdrLine. Inside Cdtr: Nm + PstlAdr~25
7Leaves under PstlAdr containers + leaves under Nm/EndToEndId/PmtId~33
Total V000 ≈ 95 nodes · V001 INSERT targets = 2 (the two PstlAdr containers)

The mental simplification: 95 nodes, only 2 matter for V001 (the two PstlAdr). Everything above level 5 is frozen wrapper structure; everything else is leaf data, mostly cloned untouched in V001. Same principle generalises across all 4 trees: each has its own large total, but a small number of PstlAdr containers carry the entire V001 delta.

SEPA — same TECH_NAME at different levels (path disambiguation)

Looking at the tree screen carefully, you see repeated tag names at different depths. The DMEE engine emits exactly what the path says, so identifying a node by TECH_NAME alone is ambiguous. The level in the UI = the position in the XML.

TECH_NAMEWhere it appears (UI path)What XML element
NmGrpHdr → InitgPty → NmUNESCO message-level identity
NmPmtInf → Dbtr → NmUNESCO batch-level debtor name
NmCdtTrfTxInf → Cdtr → NmBeneficiary name (per transaction)
NmCdtTrfTxInf → UltmtCdtr → NmAlternative payee name
NbOfTxsGrpHdr → NbOfTxsfile-level total payment count
NbOfTxsPmtInf → NbOfTxs (TX2 ref)batch-level count
PstlAdrPmtInf → Dbtr → PstlAdrV001 INSERT TARGET #1
PstlAdrCdtTrfTxInf → Cdtr → PstlAdrV001 INSERT TARGET #2

Phase 2 capture pending (post-retrofit): tree-pane screenshot only meaningful AFTER D01-RETROFIT-01 lands. 6-tabs screenshots optional — expected identical to CGI parent.

Where to find the V001 changes for each tree

The V001 changes (per-tree INSERT/MODIFY/SYNC operations + Step A/B/C walkthroughs + UI↔XML parallel bridges) live in the Change Strategy → DMEE Configuration tab. Each tree's V001 section there assumes the V000 baseline documented above.

What this means for V001

V001 active surface is even smaller than we thought. If /CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO_1 is confirmed inactive (Tier 3 candidate), V001 acts on 3 actively-routed trees covering 13 (LAND1/ZLSCH) routes: SEPA (DE/S, FR/S), CGI parent (DE/N, FR/A, FR/J, FR/N), and Citi DC_V3_01 (BR/R, CA/C, CA/N, FR/C, FR/L, FR/X — and BR/Q legacy without XBKKT='X'). That is the full blast radius of V001 in production payment volume terms. Pre-cutover regression tests should cover all 13 routes; post-cutover monitoring should flag any of these routes failing.

Companion assertions to update accordingly:

  • "4 target trees" KPI in the header → review whether this should be "3 production-routed trees + 1 unrouted peer".
  • brain claim 102 — add caveat about /CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO_1 routing status.
  • V001 test matrix — drop /CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO_1 from regression scope unless implicit-invocation is confirmed.

D01 ↔ P01 Version Comparison & Retrofit Conclusion

Brain anchor: claims 109 + 111 (TIER_1) · RFC verification 2026-04-30 (post-VPN restoration). Saved evidence: Zagentexecution/incidents/xml_payment_structured_address/version_difference_matrix_session63.json + d01_p01_v000_diff_session63.json.

Method

Direct RFC_READ_TABLE on DMEE_TREE_NODE in both D01 and P01, full extraction of all rows for each (TREE_ID, VERSION) pair, then row-level diff over 14 columns:

NODE_ID · TECH_NAME · PARENT_ID · BROTHER_ID · FIRSTCHILD_ID · LEV · NODE_TYPE · MP_SC_TAB · MP_SC_FLD · MP_OFFSET · LENGTH · CV_RULE · MP_EXIT_FUNC · MP_CONST

Table 1 — Sizes + Definition Check per (Tree × Version)

8 rows: 4 trees × 2 versions. D01 and P01 columns show node counts (not checkmarks); — means the version doesn't exist in that system. NODES column is the canonical count when D01 = P01 agree (or D01-only count for V001). Definition Check column reports the verdict from full 48-field byte-level RFC comparison (2026-04-30).

What this confirms

ObservationImplication
D01 V000 = D01 V001 in all 4 trees (zero deltas across 14 fields) D01 V001 is a byte-perfect dormant clone of V000. Whichever is HEAD-active, F110 produces identical output today.
D01 V000 = P01 V000 for SEPA + CITI + CGI These 3 trees need zero retrofit work.
D01 V001 = P01 V000 for SEPA + CITI + CGI Confirms transitivity. The dormant V001 in D01 is byte-equal to the production V000 in P01 for these 3 trees.
D01 V000 ≠ P01 V000 only for /CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO_1 (12 deltas) The only misalignment requiring retrofit work.
D01 V001 ↔ P01 V000 has the same 12 deltas as D01 V000 ↔ P01 V000 (CGI_1 only) D01 V001 inherits D01 V000's CGI_1 divergence — confirms V001 was created AFTER the D01 V000 divergence existed.

🔐 First-tree explicit confirmation — SEPA D01 = P01 by SHA-256

Per user directive 2026-04-30 ("confirm that the first tree is the same"), independent verification beyond the per-row diff. Method: serialize all 95 nodes × 46 functional fields per node into a canonical text representation (sorted by NODE_ID, sorted by field name within each node), compute SHA-256.

SystemNodesSHA-256 of 46-field × N-node canonical serialization

P01 V00095033f11ce1798ed90cdae447c0f4feaeddc03445c37885487e8adc4a447345b39

Node usage classification per tree — IN USE vs EMPTY

Per user question 2026-04-30 ("if we have 48 nodes for example, can we know which ones are empty and which are in use?"). Method: classify every P01 V000 node by examining its source binding columns. A node is IN USE if it has either a buffer source (MP_SC_TAB + MP_SC_FLD) or a constant (MP_CONST); IN USE EXIT if it has a BAdI/exit FM (MP_EXIT_FUNC); STRUCTURAL if it is an aggregator parent (NODE_TYPE in AGGR/TECH/COMP) or has children (FIRSTCHILD_ID); EMPTY if none of the above — defined node that produces no output.

TreeTotal nodesIN USE
(source/const)		IN USE EXIT
(BAdI-filled)		STRUCTURAL
(parent/aggregator)		EMPTY
(no output)		% effective
/SEPA_CT_UNES9556134495.8%
/CITI/XML/UNESCO/DC_V3_01610295312186689.2%
/CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO631109239276798.9%
/CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO_16391102392801098.4%

% effective = (IN USE + IN USE EXIT + STRUCTURAL) / Total. Only the EMPTY column shows nodes that contribute nothing to the XML output.

EMPTY-node breakdown per tree

TreeEMPTY countSample TECH_NAMEs of empty nodesWhy empty?
/SEPA_CT_UNES 4 NbOfTxs ×2, CtrlSum ×2 SAP DMEE engine auto-populates these header counts at runtime — they look "empty" in DMEE_TREE_NODE because they have no static source binding, but the engine fills them. NOT a real concern.
/CITI/XML/UNESCO/DC_V3_01 66 BirthDate, FrDt, Issr, PrvcOfBirth, Housenum, Prtry, Id, OrgId, PrvtId variants... CITI tree carries the full ISO 20022 PartyIdentification superset (private-individual identification, birth-date, regulatory IDs). UNESCO doesn't pay natural persons via Citi → those nodes are reserved placeholders, never fire. Same for many alt-mode PstlAdrMor branches.
/CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO 7 CtrlSum ×2, NbOfTxs ×2, Ref ×3 Same auto-count pattern as SEPA + 3 reserved Ref slots. Negligible.
/CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO_1 10 CtrlSum ×2, NbOfTxs ×2, AdrLine ×2 (N_3578098180, N_6139351280), Ref ×4 Same as parent CGI + 2 of the 8 ONLY_P01 AdrLine variants we need to restore in D01 are also EMPTY in P01 (intentional reserved AdrLine slots, never fired). Restoration is structural, not functional.

Insight: only ~5-10% of any tree's nodes are EMPTY, and most of those are SAP-engine-managed counters (NbOfTxs, CtrlSum) or ISO 20022 reserved superset slots that UNESCO doesn't exercise. The retrofit + V001 design only changes active address branches (PstlAdr / Cdtr / Dbtr / CdtrAgt / UltmtCdtr) — never the EMPTY nodes. Saved evidence: Zagentexecution/incidents/xml_payment_structured_address/node_usage_classification_session63.json.

What V001 changes — by node type · CONFIG vs CODE vs DATA · structural never changes

For every node in every tree, the V001 design is constrained to three change types at the leaf level — and STRUCTURAL nodes are never modified. The 27 V001-delta rows of the matrix split exactly along this axis. (Plus 2 PRECONDITION rows 0a + 0b for retrofit and Create-Version — see V001 Change Matrix tab.)

Change typeWhere it livesHow many rows in V001 matrixWhat V001 actually does
CONFIG
(DMEE customizing)		 DMEE_TREE_NODE + DMEE_TREE_COND + TFPM042FB 25 of 27 Add new ELEM nodes (StrtNm/BldgNb/PstCd/TwnNm) under existing PstlAdr structural parents · set MP_SC_TAB + MP_SC_FLD + MP_OFFSET + LENGTH + CV_RULE · add empty-suppress conditions in DMEE_TREE_COND for SEPA · add 1 row in TFPM042FB for SEPA Event 05 registration. Pure customizing — no ABAP transport.
CODE
(ABAP method)		 YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FALLBACK_CM001::GET_CREDIT 1 of 27 (row 26) Pattern A 3-line guard inside the existing BAdI method. Reviewer N_MENARD. Transport D01K-BADI-FIX-01. Workbench transport.
DATA
(master data)		 LFA1 + ADRC for 5 vendor LIFNRs 1 of 27 (row 27) Master Data team manual fix CITY1 + COUNTRY OR LOEVM='X'. No transport — pure data.
STRUCTURAL
(parent/aggregator/TECH switch)		 — 0 of 27 STRUCTURAL nodes (PstlAdr, Cdtr, Dbtr, CdtrAgt, UltmtCdtr container parents · NbOfTxs/CtrlSum auto-counters · TECH switch nodes like PstlAdrMor1/2/3) are NEVER modified by V001. They remain exactly as today. New ELEM children are added under existing structural parents, but the parent structure itself is untouched.

Total V001 footprint: 25 CONFIG + 1 CODE (3 lines) + 1 DATA (5 vendors) = 27 rows in V001 Change Matrix · zero structural changes · zero existing-node deletions.

Per-node detail — what's in the node (config or code)

For every active node in any tree we can show either the configuration (source binding for CONFIG nodes) or the code (BAdI method for CODE nodes). Below: the V001-affected nodes specifically — for each, BEFORE state from RFC + AFTER state from V001 design + reference to the actual code/config.

Configuration nodes — source binding only (no code)

These nodes read from a buffer field at runtime. The configuration is fully expressed in 5 DMEE_TREE_NODE columns. No ABAP runs for these nodes (unless MP_EXIT_FUNC is also set).

ExampleBEFORE configAFTER config (V001)
SEPA Cdtr StrtNm (NEW) node doesn't exist MP_SC_TAB=FPAYHX · MP_SC_FLD=REF01 · MP_OFFSET=0 · LENGTH=60 · CV_RULE=CL RP · MP_EXIT_FUNC=FI_CGI_DMEE_EXIT_W_BADI
SEPA Dbtr StrtNm (NEW) node doesn't exist MP_SC_TAB=FPAYP · MP_SC_FLD=REF01 · MP_OFFSET=0 · LENGTH=60 · CV_RULE=CL RP
CITI UltmtCdtr StrtNm (MODIFY) MP_SC_TAB= (empty) · MP_SC_FLD= (empty) · LENGTH=70 — node exists, no source set MP_SC_TAB=FPAYH · MP_SC_FLD=ZSTRA · MP_OFFSET=0 · LENGTH=70 · CV_RULE=CLURP
CGI CdtrAgt PstCd (NEW) node doesn't exist MP_SC_TAB=FPAYH · MP_SC_FLD=ZBPST · MP_OFFSET=0 · LENGTH=16 · CV_RULE=CL

Full per-row config: v001_change_matrix.csv (29 rows: 2 PRECONDITION 0a/0b + 27 V001 deltas). Per-tree node BEFORE state: sepa_v000_baseline_session63.txt.

Code node — the only BAdI change in V001

There's exactly one node-level CODE change: Pattern A guard in YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FALLBACK_CM001::GET_CREDIT. It runs when DMEE traversal reaches the StrtNm node and the BAdI exit is configured. This method is REGISTERED as MP_EXIT_FUNC=FI_CGI_DMEE_EXIT_W_BADI on every Cdtr/Dbtr/UltmtCdtr StrtNm in CGI + SEPA (claim 96 SocGen-mandated).

Affected nodeBEFORE code (current GET_CREDIT method body)AFTER code (Pattern A 3-line guard)
<PmtInf><CdtTrfTxInf><Cdtr><PstlAdr><StrtNm> WHEN-branch in GET_CREDIT 
WHEN '<PmtInf><CdtTrfTxInf><Cdtr><PstlAdr><StrtNm>'.
  IF i_fpayh = mv_fpayh AND mv_cdtr_name+35 IS NOT INITIAL.
    c_value = |{ mv_cdtr_name+35 } { c_value }|.
  ENDIF.
  IF c_value+70 IS NOT INITIAL.
    CLEAR c_value+70.
  ENDIF.

Source: extracted_code/FI/DMEE_p01_canonical/YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FALLBACK====CM001.abap. Issue: when V001 supplies a real c_value (structured StrtNm from FPAYHX-REF01), this overwrites it by prepending mv_cdtr_name+35 unconditionally.

 
WHEN '<PmtInf><CdtTrfTxInf><Cdtr><PstlAdr><StrtNm>'.
  IF i_fpayh = mv_fpayh
     AND mv_cdtr_name+35 IS NOT INITIAL
     AND c_value IS INITIAL.            "← V001 GUARD: only prepend if StrtNm empty (V000 path)
    c_value = mv_cdtr_name+35.
  ELSEIF i_fpayh = mv_fpayh
     AND mv_cdtr_name+35 IS NOT INITIAL.
    c_value = |{ mv_cdtr_name+35 } { c_value }|.   " V000 legacy preserved
  ENDIF.
  IF c_value+70 IS NOT INITIAL.
    CLEAR c_value+70.
  ENDIF.

Net change: +3 lines (the guard AND c_value IS INITIAL + the ELSEIF reroute). Backward-compatible with V000 (when c_value is empty, the original prepend behavior runs unchanged). Reviewer N_MENARD. Transport D01K-BADI-FIX-01.

📌 Summary — your two questions answered

  1. Structural nodes are NOT changed in V001. ✓ Confirmed. STRUCTURAL = parent/aggregator nodes (PstlAdr, Cdtr, Dbtr, CdtrAgt, UltmtCdtr containers · NbOfTxs/CtrlSum auto-counters · PstlAdrMor TECH switches). The change matrix has 0 of 27 rows targeting structural nodes. V001 only adds NEW leaf-level ELEM nodes under existing structural parents.
  2. Per-tree-node we can see the code or the configuration. ✓ Confirmed. CONFIG nodes expose 5 fields (MP_SC_TAB · MP_SC_FLD · MP_OFFSET · LENGTH · CV_RULE) — fully visible per RFC. CODE nodes (only nodes with MP_EXIT_FUNC set) link to the actual BAdI method source on disk. Of the 27 V001 deltas: 25 are CONFIG (DMEE customizing) · 1 is CODE (Pattern A 3-line guard) · 1 is DATA (5 vendor master fix). No structural disruption anywhere.

Marlies's analysis coverage vs our V001 design — 11 user-visible defects + 8 internal gaps

Source: Zagentexecution/incidents/xml_payment_structured_address/original_marlies/XML Address un structured.xlsx — 2 sheets · 10 production payment XML samples (3 SEPA + 4 CITI + 4 CGI). Question: how did Marlies know which nodes to focus on, and what could her method physically not catch?

Vocabulary clarification — "Dbtr Hybrid" describes a CONTAINER, not a node

Marlies labels each PARTY-level <PstlAdr> container as Unstructured / Hybrid / Structured. These are state labels on a structural container, not individual nodes. The actual leaf nodes underneath are <StrtNm>, <BldgNb>, <PstCd>, <TwnNm>, <Ctry>, <CtrySubDvsn>, <AdrLine>×N.

<CdtTrfTxInf>                      ← payment-line container
  ├── <Dbtr>                       ← PARTY (UNESCO as debtor)
  │   ├── <Nm>                     ← leaf node (entity name)
  │   └── <PstlAdr>                ← STRUCTURAL CONTAINER (no value, just wraps)
  │       ├── <StrtNm>             ← LEAF NODE (street)
  │       ├── <BldgNb>             ← LEAF NODE (building)
  │       ├── <PstCd>              ← LEAF NODE (postal)
  │       ├── <TwnNm>              ← LEAF NODE (town)
  │       ├── <CtrySubDvsn>        ← LEAF NODE (state/region)
  │       ├── <Ctry>               ← LEAF NODE (ISO country)
  │       └── <AdrLine>×N          ← LEAF NODE(s) (unstructured fallback)
  ├── <Cdtr>                       ← PARTY (vendor as creditor) — same children
  ├── <CdtrAgt>                    ← PARTY (vendor's bank) — same children inside <FinInstnId>
  └── <UltmtCdtr>                  ← PARTY (Worldlink end-beneficiary) — same children
Marlies's labelWhat it describes about the PstlAdr container's leaf children
UnstructuredOnly <AdrLine> leaves populated · no structured leaves · REJECTED post-Nov 2026 CBPR+
Hybrid<TwnNm> + <Ctry> populated structured · rest in <AdrLine> · CBPR+ minimum OK
StructuredAll 5 structured leaves populated · <AdrLine> empty/suppressed · CBPR+ future-proof

So: Marlies's "DBTR Hybrid" = state of the Dbtr's PstlAdr container · our V001 change matrix rows = specific LEAF nodes we add/modify under those containers · STRUCTURAL containers themselves (Dbtr · Cdtr · CdtrAgt · UltmtCdtr · PstlAdr · FinInstnId) are NEVER modified by V001.

How Marlies identified her nodes

MethodStrengthInherent blind spot
Pulled 10 real production payment XML files (3 SEPA + 4 CITI + 4 CGI) Sees actual XML output users get → catches user-visible defects (Hybrid/Unstructured/missing postal) Cannot see internal source bindings, BAdI dispatch chain, alt-mode TECH switches, or D01-side divergence
Walked each <Dbtr> <CdtrAgt> <Cdtr> <UltmtCdtr> block per sample 100% complete on the 4 user-facing address blocks per format Empty/reserved ISO 20022 slots don't appear in production XML (66 reserved nodes in CITI tree)
Marked each block as Structured / Hybrid / Unstructured + remark Clear scope-delineation per format × block Can't infer WHY (config? BAdI? Pattern A?) — only WHAT

8 internal gaps her bottom-up method physically can't catch

XML-output inspection is necessary but not sufficient. These 8 gaps come from row-level RFC verification + ABAP source extraction + cross-system D01-vs-P01 diff — none of which is visible in a payment XML file.

#GapWhy XML-only inspection misses itOur finding
A CITI Dbtr alt-mode PstlAdr (N_4078824850) — second Dbtr PstlAdr fired only when TECH switch routes (PstlAdrMor) Marlies's 4 CITI samples all routed to primary PstlAdr (N_1531351640). Alt-mode is data-conditional and her samples didn't trigger it. Matrix rows 12-16 add full +5 structured nodes to alt-mode. Without this, certain US/CA/BR payments would still produce Unstructured XML in V001.
B CGI_1 D01-vs-P01 12-delta divergence (1 SCB ONLY_D01 + 8 AdrLine ONLY_P01 + 3 CHANGED) Production XML output is from P01 V000 only. D01-vs-P01 row-level diff requires RFC extraction of both sides — her file is XML-output-driven. Claim 109 RFC-verified. Retrofit transport D01K-RETROFIT-01 fixes in ~30 min. Without this, deploying V001 in D01 would inherit dirty V000 state P01 doesn't have.
C CGI_1 Nm Z-field experiment — D01 sources Nm from FPAYHX-NAMEZ, P01 has empty TAB/FLD This is a DEFINITION delta inside the tree, not visible in XML output Found via row-level diff (claim 109). Decision: revert to P01 (recommended) or promote D01 + transport.
D Pattern A overflow logic in BAdI — when <Cdtr><Nm> >35 chars, BAdI prepends chars 36-40 onto <StrtNm> The OUTPUT XML shows the prepended text — symptom visible but cause is in YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FALLBACK_CM001::GET_CREDIT ABAP, invisible from XML Claim 96: SocGen-mandated per N_MENARD doc 2024-02-29. V001 needs the 3-line guard (matrix row 26) to prevent corrupting NEW structured StrtNm.
E PPC tags for 9 countries (AE/BH/CN/ID/IN/JO/MA/MY/PH) Her 10 samples were FR/US/CA/BR — none of the PPC countries. She would never see PPC tags fire in those samples. Claim 99 + PPC tab. V001 must PRESERVE these tag dispatches on <InstrForCdtrAgt>/<InstrInf> and <RmtInf>/<Ustrd>.
F 66 EMPTY reserved nodes in CITI tree (BirthDate, OrgId, PrvtId, PrvcOfBirth, etc.) Empty nodes don't appear in any production XML — they're reserved ISO 20022 superset slots UNESCO doesn't exercise Node-usage classification explains: not a defect, intentional. No V001 action needed.
G TFPM042FB SEPA Event 05 missing registration Her XML shows missing structured fields in SEPA — but the WHY (no Event 05 FM registered) requires looking at OBPM4 customizing Matrix row 9: +1 row in TFPM042FB · FORMI=/SEPA_CT_UNES · EVENT=05 · FNAME=FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_CGI_05.
H Source field bindings per node (MP_SC_TAB · MP_SC_FLD · MP_OFFSET · LENGTH · CV_RULE) for the new V001 nodes Her file says "make it Structured" — design layer translates that into specific buffer reads (FPAYHX-REF01[0:60], etc.) Matrix rows 1-25 specify each binding precisely with claim-101 byte-layout anchors.

Summary: Marlies's analysis is right and complete at the user-visible XML-output layer — 11 of 11 defects in her samples are covered by V001. The 8 gaps above come from row-level RFC + ABAP-source + D01-vs-P01 layers her XML-driven method physically can't see. Two of the 8 gaps (A CITI Dbtr alt-mode, B CGI_1 retrofit) would have shipped a broken V001 if missed; the other 6 are coverage extensions that strengthen V001 without being failure-causing on their own.

✅ Conclusion — retrofit is small and safe

  1. P01 runs V000 (the only version) in production today. Verified.
  2. D01 has both V000 + V001; V001 is byte-perfect clone of V000 (dormant since Create Version event). F110 in D01 produces V000-equivalent output regardless of which is HEAD-active.
  3. 3 of 4 trees (SEPA + CITI + CGI) are byte-equal D01 V000 = P01 V000. Zero retrofit work needed there.
  4. Only CGI_1 has 12 deltas. ~30 minutes of DMEE Tx surgical work fixes them.
  5. The retrofit transport D01K-RETROFIT-01 bundles: (a) purge dormant V001 on all 4 trees, (b) CGI_1 V000 12-node fix, (c) 5 P01-only ABAP objects (DE/IT classes + 3 ENHO + FR.CM002 method).
  6. After retrofit: Create fresh V001 from byte-equal V000 → apply 27-row V001 change matrix → test → V01 → P01.
  7. One outstanding audit-trail item: D01 V001 EX_STATUS at HEAD level. Functionally irrelevant (V001 = V000 byte-clone) but Marlies's 10-second DMEE Tx → Versions check completes documentation.

PMW infrastructure alignment — D01-RETROFIT-02-PMW (beyond the DMEE tree)

The DMEE tree is only one of several SAP objects F110 traverses to produce a payment file. Before V001 testing in D01 can be trusted, the surrounding PMW infrastructure that invokes the DMEE tree must also be byte-equal between D01 and P01. The first retrofit transport (D01-RETROFIT-01, documented above) covers (a) DMEE tree drift on CGI_1, (b) dormant V001 PURGE on all 4 trees, (c) 5 P01-only BAdI classes (YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_DE/_IT + 3 ENHOs + FR.CM002 method per claim 70). It does not cover the PMW configuration tables and program variants below — that is the second alignment transport D01-RETROFIT-02-PMW, run before Phase 3 unit testing.

The runtime chain F110 follows: F110 reads FBZP → looks up T042Z (payment method per country) → identifies the PMW format (FORMI) → looks up T042Y (PMW format definition) → invokes the SAPFPAYM_<format> program with the registered variant → that program reads TFPM042F/TFPM042FB (Event registrations) → fires Event 05 (FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_CGI_05) → fills FPAYHX-FREF buffers → DMEE engine walks the tree → emits XML. Any of those tables/programs missing from D01 means F110 in D01 produces a different file from F110 in P01 — even if the DMEE tree is identical.

Discovery → triage → execute → verify — the 5-step flow

Scope: identify all D01↔P01 deltas across the 8 objects above and either (a) transport missing rows from P01 to D01, or (b) flag explicit divergence as a known limitation of D01 testing. Owner: Pablo + N_MENARD (BAdI/code) + M_SPRONK (config tables).

  1. Step 1 — Discovery: 8 RFC_READ_TABLE comparisons D01 vs P01 (T042Z, T042Y, TFPM042F, TFPM042FB, VARI for SAPFPAYM*, OBPM2, plus the PPC tables and class catalogs). Output: knowledge/domains/Payment/d01_p01_pmw_alignment.json with row-level diffs.
  2. Step 2 — Triage: per delta, classify as RETROFIT (transport from P01 to D01), KEEP-DIFFERENT (intentional D01 test override), or INVESTIGATE (unclear).
  3. Step 3 — Execute: bundle the RETROFIT-class deltas in D01K-RETROFIT-02-PMW. Customizing transport (W) for tables; workbench (K) for any program variants that touch ABAP source.
  4. Step 4 — Verify: re-run the 8 hash comparisons. D01 = P01 byte-equal expected. Document residual KEEP-DIFFERENT items.
  5. Step 5 — Gate: Phase 3 unit-test cannot start until D01-RETROFIT-02-PMW completes OR explicit waivers are documented for residual deltas.

Brain anchor: KU-2026-PMW-D01-ALIGNMENT — open question on byte-equality of the 8 objects above. Status: PENDING — RFC discovery required before Phase 3 unit-test. Once verified, the alignment status of T042Z/T042Y/TFPM042F/TFPM042FB for the 4 in-scope formats becomes a TIER_1 claim (candidate claim 121).

Why this lives here, not in DMEE Configuration · foundations: this is byte-alignment work — the natural home for "what's different between D01 and P01 that we must fix before testing V001 there". It complements D01-RETROFIT-01 (DMEE tree drift, dormant V001 PURGE, BAdI classes) which is documented above in this same tab. Both retrofits gate Phase 3.

Evolution — 10 years of CTS history on the target trees

Why look at 10 years of transports before changing anything

Before you change a 10-year-old DMEE tree, you should know who built it, who has touched it since, and what the historical change pattern looks like. UNESCO's payment XML config has been continuously evolving since 2017 — by 8 different authors across 52 transports. Each transport tells you something about how the team works: are changes typically small and surgical, or sweeping refactors? Are there bursts of activity tied to specific business events (a new bank, a regulatory change)? Who owns which area of the code?

That history matters for V001 in two concrete ways: (1) it gives us the "surgical pattern" baseline — claim 102 confirms 81.8% of historical transports touch ≤3 objects, and our V001 (split into 8 transports averaging ~3 objects) sits squarely inside that envelope, meaning we are not asking the team to do anything operationally novel; (2) it identifies code ownership — N_MENARD owns all 8 ABAP-class transports, M_SPRONK owns all 31 DMEE config transports, F. Spezzano owns 5 PMW-variant transports. Knowing this, we route reviewers correctly: Pattern A goes to N_MENARD; DMEE node edits go to M_SPRONK; OBPM4 row goes to F. Spezzano.

How to read the table below

The first table is the author footprint — who has done what across the 8-author / 52-transport history. The second table is the year-by-year transport timeline, showing when each tree was changed and by whom. Read it as the project's institutional memory: every cell is a transport someone designed, tested, and released; the patterns reveal where the team is comfortable and where they are not.

Brain-anchored. Every entry below is sourced from knowledge/domains/Payment/phase0/cts_dmee_authors.md + francesco_audit.md + the per-transport E071 classification at Zagentexecution/incidents/xml_payment_structured_address/transport_classification_44.json. Claims 72 (53 transports / 8 authors), 96 (Pattern A SocGen-mandated), 101 (44-transport classification). Each transport shows the date, author, object count, change-type (derived from PGMID + OBJECT_TYPE) and the actual elements touched.

Two patterns the historical evidence shows (both reinforce the V001 design)

Anchor: brain claim 102 (TIER_1) — surgical pattern + zero-versioning analysis of the 44-transport cohort. Reproducible from transport_classification_44.json.

Pattern 1 · UNESCO DMEE changes are SURGICAL

Across 44 DMEE-touching transports by the 3 active authors (M_SPRONK + N_MENARD + FP_SPEZZANO), the obj_count distribution is heavily skewed toward minimal touches:

Bucket (obj/transport)Count%
exactly 1 object2659.1 %
2-3 objects1022.7 %
4-10 objects36.8 %
11-25 objects24.5 %
26+ objects (package merges)36.8 %
≤ 3 objects (surgical)3681.8 %

Median = 1 object · Mean = 5.3 · M_SPRONK is most surgical (90.3% ≤3, median 1). FP_SPEZZANO 100% ≤3.

Why this matters for V001: the planned V001 scope (3 ABAP lines + ~24 DMEE nodes across 4 trees + 1 OBPM4 row + 5 vendor fixes) lands inside this surgical envelope. The 4 V001 tree transports + 1 BAdI transport will look operationally indistinguishable from typical Marlies+N_MENARD work. No new operational risk surface from "size".

Pattern 2 · DMEE NATIVE VERSIONING — historical evidence (claims 102 + 109 + 111 — RFC verification 2026-04-30)

The version mental model (V000/V001 cohabitation, EX_STATUS flip, dormant V001 in D01) is documented canonically in DMEE Configuration · the version thing. This section captures the historical evidence specific to UNESCO's 10-year transport history — the released-transport scan and the in-system D01-vs-P01 version comparison.

Two truths, two scopes:

  1. Released-transport scope (claim 102 holds): zero V001/V002 patterns across all 44 released DMEE-touching transports 2017-2024. No V001 has ever shipped via transport.
  2. In-system D01 scope (claim 109 - RFC-verified 2026-04-30 post-VPN restoration): D01 ALREADY has DMEE_TREE_NODE.VERSION=001 rows for all 4 in-scope trees. Someone ran DMEE Tx -> Create Version on each, leaving V001 as a byte-identical clone of V000 - dormant, never edited, never released. Verified counts: SEPA(V000=95, V001=95), CITI(610/610), CGI(631/631), CGI_1(632/632). P01 has only V000.

Verified: pattern scan across every E071 obj_name in all 44 transports for V001 / V002 / VERSION_001 / V01 / VERS001 returned zero hits. The "V3" in /CITI/XML/UNESCO/DC_V3_01 is a tree-name component (Citi PMW V3 format), not a DMEE_TREE_HEAD.VERSION bump. Plan §Finding J L504 said VERSION=000 in all 4 UNESCO trees today - that holds for P01 only. D01 has BOTH 000 + 001.

TreeP01 active VERSIOND01 versions presentReleased V001 transports

V001 will be the FIRST EVER DMEE version-bumped transport at UNESCO (released-transport scope per claim 102). In-system D01 already has dormant V001 entries for all 4 trees per claim 109 — recommendation: PURGE the dormant V001 (it has been sitting since an undated DMEE Tx Create Version event, byte-identical clone of D01 V000) and recreate fresh as part of D01-RETROFIT-01 to recover a clean transport-trail. The first-ever experience for the team is therefore: (a) the released-transport V001 round-trip D01→V01→P01, (b) DMEE Tx → Activate Version atomic flip, (c) tested rollback V000↔V001. Brain claim 111.

Why this matters for V001: the 2-file + DMEE-versioning strategy adopted (per user directive 2026-04-24, plan §Design recommendations L500) is a new operational practice for the UNESCO team — neither M_SPRONK nor N_MENARD has done a version bump before. Phase 2 Week 1 deliverable explicitly: "V001 INACTIVE in all 3 systems" — first time exercising DMEE Tx Create Version + Activate Version steps in operations. Worth a dry run on a non-live tree first.

Granularity note · what E071 reveals vs what it doesn't

Each transport's "what was changed" detail below is derived from its E071 entries (PGMID + OBJECT_TYPE + OBJECT_NAME). This is exact at:

  • ABAP class transports — method-level (LIMU METH gives class+method name) and include-level (CINC/CPUB/CPRI/CPRO).
  • Customizing transports — table-row level (CDAT/TDAT/TABU give the exact view + changed table).
  • Enhancement/ENHO — spot name (which BAdI hook is registered for which class).

But E071 stops at tree-level for DMEE objects: R3TR DMEE PAYM/<tree> tells you which tree was edited, but NOT which nodes inside the tree were added/modified/deleted. To get node-level forensics you need a DMEE_TREE_NODE.AS_TIME diff between adjacent transport release timestamps. Tracked as KU-2026-063-03 LOW — not blocking V001 (surgical-pattern stats above are sufficient confirmation), open only if a Phase 4 regression needs deeper history.

What this means for V001

  • Marlies has 7 years of operational experience on Citi tree (27 of her 31 transports) — V001 CITI Dbtr structuring + UltmtCdtr unification will land in territory she knows well. Plan §Phase 2 §Per-tree design adopts this premise.
  • SEPA tree has had only 5 touches ever (M_SPRONK 2020-2021) — V001 SEPA work is the deepest config change of this migration. Sub-option A test in D01 first (per Plan line 567) is justified by the lack of recent operational practice on this tree.
  • CGI tree has had only 6 touches by Marlies + 5 by Francesco (11 total) — V001 CdtrAgt fix lands on a relatively quiet tree. Pre-Phase-2 alignment call with Francesco still recommended (per `feedback_propagate_q_resolution_to_all_sections` rule).
  • N_MENARD's 2024 burst built the country-class hierarchy from scratch — Pattern A 3-line guard (V001 ABAP change) lands inside YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FALLBACK_CM001::GET_CREDIT, the single method N_MENARD touched in his last transport (D01K9B0CEW 2024-11-22). N_MENARD as required reviewer is correctly identified by the plan.
  • The CL_IM_DMEE_XML_BADI_01 predecessor BAdI (M_SPRONK 2018+2019) likely existed before N_MENARD's hierarchy. Whether it still fires in P01 is not directly tested — KU candidate if the Pattern A regression test surfaces unexpected behaviour.

V001 Change Matrix — node-by-node design specification

Why this matrix exists

Saying "we will add structured address tags to 4 DMEE trees" is a high-level statement. Saying "we will create node N_NEW_001 as child of N_5649723900 with NODE_TYPE=ELEM, MP_SC_TAB=FPAYHX, MP_SC_FLD=REF01, MP_OFFSET=0, LENGTH=60" is what M_SPRONK can actually configure in DMEE Tx. This matrix is the bridge between the two — every node, every condition, every TFPM042FB row, every ABAP line of V001 is enumerated as one row, with all the fields needed to execute the change without inventing values. No row is speculative; every PARENT_NODE_ID and every source-field reference is verified against the real P01 tree state (1,975 nodes already extracted).

How to use this matrix

Read it as the build instructions for Phase 2. Each row maps to a single config click in DMEE Tx (or a single line of ABAP for Pattern A). When M_SPRONK opens DMEE → /SEPA_CT_UNES → V001 → Edit, she can use the Action, Parent Node, Tech Name, Source, MP_OFFSET, Length columns directly to fill in the SAP screens. There is no judgment-call space here on purpose: the design is locked, the values are known, the work is mechanical.

The matrix totals 27 rows split across 8 transports — and that 27/8 split is itself meaningful. Claim 102 established that 81.8% of UNESCO's historical DMEE transports touched ≤3 objects (the "surgical pattern"). V001's 8 transports averaging ~3 objects each puts the work squarely inside that historical envelope. This is not a project asking the team to do something operationally novel; it is a project executing the team's normal change cadence at the normal scale.

Phase 1 deliverable item #1 · created 2026-04-30 · CSV source: knowledge/domains/Payment/v001_change_matrix.csv · brain anchors: claim 99 (Q3 RESOLVED), claim 101 (byte-layout finding), claim 102 (surgical pattern), claim 103 (per-entity routing closed), claim 96 (Pattern A SocGen-mandated), plan §Per-tree design L546-567.

Each row is one DMEE_TREE_NODE / DMEE_TREE_COND / TFPM042FB / ABAP / DATA delta needed for V001. Sourced from extracted dmee_tree_node_p01_all48.csv — every PARENT_NODE_ID and existing-source pattern is from the actual P01 tree state (1,975 nodes), not invented. 29 rows total = 2 PRECONDITION (0a + 0b) + 27 V001 deltas. The 27 deltas match the surgical envelope claim 102: median 1 obj/transport, 81.8% ≤3, our V001 split into 8 transports stays within historical pattern.

Important precision corrections vs earlier plan wording:

  • Plan §L546 said "+5 Dbtr structured nodes per tree" — actual extracted tree state shows the existing PstlAdr nodes already have Ctry in many cases. So per-tree the deltas are 4 NEW nodes (StrtNm/BldgNb/PstCd/TwnNm) plus existing Ctry stays.
  • SEPA needs Cdtr work too (4 nodes), not just Dbtr — plan §L220 explicitly says "Structured Dbtr + Cdtr" so total SEPA = 8 new nodes + 4 conds + 1 OBPM4 row.
  • CITI has TWO Dbtr PstlAdr parents (N_1531351640 primary, N_4078824850 alt-mode/PstlAdrMor). The alt-mode needs full +5; primary only needs +2 (StrtNm + BldgNb).
  • CITI UltmtCdtr has an EXISTING-but-empty StrtNm node (N_4600960730 child) — V001 sets MP_SC_TAB=FPAYH MP_SC_FLD=ZSTRA on it (MODIFY operation, not ADD). Per claim 99.
  • CGI CdtrAgt fix is +4 nodes (StrtNm/BldgNb/PstCd/TwnNm), parent N_0693479130, sourced from FPAYH-ZBSTR/ZBPST/ZBORT — mirrors existing CITI CdtrAgt source pattern (FPAYH-ZBSTR + FPAYH-ZBORT verified in extracted nodes).
  • CGI_1 SYNC: FIRSTNODE_ID identical to CGI parent (N_0978274660 pre-existing) — CdtrAgt fix propagates automatically without separate node edits. Verify post-Save in DMEE Tx.

🆕 PPC System (Payment Purpose Code) — discovered 2026-04-29

What is PPC and why does it exist?

Payment Purpose Code (PPC) is a regulatory tag that 9 countries — UAE, Bahrain, China, Indonesia, India, Jordan, Morocco, Malaysia, Philippines — require their receiving banks to receive on every inbound USD payment. The code identifies the purpose of the payment (consultancy fee / supplier invoice / travel reimbursement / regulatory cost / etc.) so the receiving central bank can categorize cross-border flows for capital-controls reporting. Without PPC, banks in those 9 countries reject the payment — the money bounces back, the vendor doesn't get paid, the finance team has to retry with a corrected file.

Why this tab exists at all (this is critical context for V001)

Until 2026-04-29 the team thought there was one custom development stream on /CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO: Pattern A (the SocGen name-overflow logic). Then N_MENARD shared an email with 3 functional + technical specs revealing a second, equally important custom stream: the entire PPC infrastructure. Built March 2024, production-active in P01 (but not in D01 — that's a known retrofit gap). It uses two custom Z-tables (YTFI_PPC_TAG, YTFI_PPC_STRUC) plus a UTIL class plus a country-dispatcher BAdI. Touching /CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO V001 without understanding PPC would have been a serious risk.

The discovery of PPC also forced the team to add an explicit PPC preservation requirement to the Change Strategy tab: the V001 CdtrAgt fix must NOT alter the BAdI dispatch behavior on <InstrForCdtrAgt><InstrInf> (used by AE/CN) or <RmtInf><Ustrd> (used by the other 7 countries). Both XML nodes sit inside the same <PmtInf><CdtTrfTxInf> wrapper as the CdtrAgt fix, so an over-broad refactor could accidentally break PPC routing.

How to read this tab

The tables below first show the 9 countries with their tag locations (where in the XML the PPC value goes) and example values, then the infrastructure (tables, classes, dispatcher logic). Use this as both reference (when reviewing /CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO V001 design) and validation context (when the simulator validates PPC dispatch behavior is preserved).

Source: N_MENARD email DMEE.eml 2026-04-29 with 3 docx attachments saved to Zagentexecution/incidents/xml_payment_structured_address/nmenard_email_2026-04-29/. This is a SECOND custom development stream on /CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO beyond Pattern A. Without PPC tags, banks for 9 countries reject USD payments via SocGen.

Data flow — where the PPC value originates (invoice → payment → tag)

Brain anchor: claim 97 (PPC system) · code-traced evidence: extracted_code/FI/DMEE_p01_canonical/YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_UTIL========CM003.abap line 48 (READ TABLE mt_t015l WITH KEY lzbkz = is_fpayp-lzbkz). The PPC code is NOT entered at payment time — it is set when the invoice is posted and then read downstream during F110.

Reading-note (UNESCO data model): BSEG is a cluster table — not directly RFC-readable. UNESCO's Gold DB exposes line items via the bseg_union view (BSIS ∪ BSAS ∪ BSIK ∪ BSAK ∪ BSID ∪ BSAD, 32 cols, 4.7M rows). For vendor line items, LZBKZ lives on BSIK (open) / BSAK (cleared) — accessed via bseg_union. F110 itself uses SAP-std internal logic to read open items via BSIK, not via the cluster.

StageSAP transactionWhere storedWho maintainsWhat gets validated against what
1. Invoice posting
(the moment the PPC is "imagined onto" the document)		 FB60 / MIRO / F-43 / FBV1 SAP writes the line to the cluster (BSEG) AND populates the secondary indices: BSIK-LZBKZ (vendor open items) — 3-char SCB Statistical Bank Indicator. Visible to us via bseg_union. AP clerk / Finance team — entered on the "Payment" tab of the vendor line F4-help on LZBKZ already validates against T015L at posting time. Invalid LZBKZ codes are rejected by the standard SAP field check.
2. Master config
(the table the invoice-time entry is checked against)		 OBC8 / SM30 V_T015L T015L (SAP-std SCB Indicators, ~73 rows in P01) FI configurator (one-time + occasional) — populates T015L-ZWCK1 with the PPC code + description (space-separated, e.g. "P0301 PURCHASES") SAP-std table. UNESCO does NOT customize T015L beyond standard SCB regulatory codes — the PPC-formatted ZWCK1 is the convention agreed with SocGen.
3. Payment buffering
(F110 build phase, before DMEE)		 F110 proposal/run FPAYP-LZBKZ (SAP-std: F110 reads vendor open items via BSIK → builds FPAYP per item, inheriting LZBKZ) SAP-std F110 logic — no UNESCO code involved here FPAYP is the per-item payment buffer. The LZBKZ travels with the line item all the way into the DMEE BAdI context.
4. DMEE BAdI dispatch
(the read + lookup at payment moment)		 (internal, fires during DMEE tree traversal of /CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO) BAdI reads is_fpayp-lzbkz → looks up mt_t015l (in-memory cache) → splits ZWCK1 at space (first token = PPC_VAR, rest = PPC_DESCR) N_MENARD code (YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_UTIL.CM003) Lookup keys: (land1, deb_cre, pay_type, tag_full) against YTFI_PPC_STRUC (133 positional rows) selects WHICH building blocks concat into the tag, in WHICH order. YTFI_PPC_TAG (11 rows) decides WHERE in the XML the result goes.
5. XML emission (DMEE writes node) Final concatenated value emitted into <InstrForCdtrAgt><InstrInf> (AE/CN) OR <RmtInf><Ustrd> (BH/ID/IN/JO/MA/MY/PH) SAP-std DMEE engine Receiving central bank validates per its own regulatory rules (e.g. India RBI P-codes, China SAFE codes). Reject = payment bounce.

The two validations that matter:

  • SAP-side, at invoice posting: F4-help on BSEG-LZBKZ validates against T015L existence — guarantees no payment carries a non-existent SCB code.
  • UNESCO-side, at DMEE traversal: YTFI_PPC_STRUC LOOP filters by (land1+deb_cre+pay_type+tag_full); if no row matches for the country, the BAdI returns ev_subrc=4 and the XML tag emits empty/default (PPC fails silently — bank rejection downstream).

Operational implication for V001: V001 changes (CdtrAgt structured nodes) do NOT touch FPAYP-LZBKZ, T015L, or YTFI_PPC_STRUC — but they MUST preserve the existence of the <InstrForCdtrAgt><InstrInf> and <RmtInf><Ustrd> XML tags so the BAdI write path still reaches them. If V001 accidentally suppresses either tag for a PPC country, payment to AE/BH/CN/ID/IN/JO/MA/MY/PH gets rejected at the receiving bank.

Code chain (PPC dispatch)

F110 → /CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO traversal
  ↓ DMEE node BAdI FI_CGI_DMEE_EXIT_W_BADI fires
  ↓ for FR co code (UNES) → YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FR  ⚠️ method CM002 P01-ONLY (retrofit needed)
       ↓ NEW ycl_idfi_cgi_dmee_util( )
       ↓ lo_cgi_util->get_tag_value_from_custo(land1, tag_full, deb_cre, fpayh, fpayhx, fpayp)
         ↓ YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_UTIL_CM003 (identical D01↔P01)
            ↓ pay_type from i_fpayh-dorigin(2): HR→P, TR→R, OTHERS→O
            ↓ READ TABLE mt_t015l (SCB indicators master, 73 rows)
            ↓ LOOP YTFI_PPC_STRUC WHERE land1+pay_type+tag_full match
            ↓ Build via positional concat:
                SEPARATOR/FIXED_VAL → append literal
                PPC_VAR → T015L.ZWCK1 first space-token
                PPC_DESCR → T015L.ZWCK1 rest after first space
                PAY_FIELD → dynamic field assign IS_FPAYH/IS_FPAYHX/IS_FPAYP
            ↓ RETURN populated o_value
       ↓ DMEE writes o_value into the XML tag

⛔ GAP — LZBKZ has no upstream validation today (finding 2026-04-30)

Brain anchor: KU-PPC-LZBKZ-VALIDATION · evidence: GB922 zero substitutions targeting SUBSFIELD='LZBKZ' · YRGGBS00 1,592-line full-source grep zero matches for "LZBKZ" / "SCB" / "stat\\w*\\s*bank" / "reporting indicator" · GB901/GB922 audit of UNESCO custom validation+substitution chain.

The risk in one sentence: today an AP clerk can post FB01 / FB60 / MIRO / F-43 against a vendor whose bank is in AE/BH/CN/ID/IN/JO/MA/MY/PH without entering LZBKZ. At F110 time the BAdI looks up T015L with empty FPAYP-LZBKZ → no match → empty <InstrInf> / <Ustrd> PPC tag → bank rejects the payment.

Decision needed: Marlies + N_MENARD + Pablo.

Why D01 testing of PPC is BROKEN today

D01 has the YTFI_PPC tables + UTIL/CM003 dispatcher + T015L master. But D01's YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FR has method CM001 instead of P01's CM002. The CM002 method is the entry point that calls UTIL→get_tag_value_from_custo. Without it:

  • F110 in D01 to vendor in AE/BH/CN/ID/IN/JO/MA/MY/PH via /CGI tree
  • BAdI fires for <InstrForCdtrAgt><InstrInf> or <RmtInf><Ustrd> node
  • FR class CM001 (legacy) handles it → does NOT dispatch PPC
  • Output XML has the tag empty or with default value → bank would reject in production

→ Q1bis (FR method swap) RESOLVED: CM002 is the PPC integration that was added to P01 in March 2024 and never came back to D01. Retrofit to D01 is mandatory.

Connection to Worldlink dual-route (claim 95)

PM Model 10 found exotic currencies route via two paths:

  • Path A: Citi (CIT01/CIT04) → /CITI tree — BRL/MGA/TND (no PPC)
  • Path B: SocGen (SOG01) → /CGI tree — INR/THB/KES/NGN/CNY (PPC FIRES for IN/CN/MY/PH/JO/MA)

The CGI tree carries treasury exotic-currency payments via SocGen which trigger PPC. Volume per PPC country (REGUH 2025+): IN 2,098 · MY 800+ · PH 800+ · CN 796 · JO/MA hundreds.

V001 design impact (CRITICAL)

The CGI tree V001 changes (CdtrAgt structured nodes) MUST PRESERVE PPC tag locations:

  • <InstrForCdtrAgt><InstrInf> (used by AE/CN PPC)
  • <RmtInf><Ustrd> (used by BH/ID/IN/JO/MA/MY/PH PPC)

If V001 modifies these node definitions or conditions in a way that suppresses PPC dispatch, payments to vendors with banks in 9 countries will fail in production.

Test matrix extension — 27 PPC scenarios

Phase 3 test matrix adds 9 countries × 3 payment types (O/P/R) = 27 scenarios. Each must verify the PPC tag content matches V000 baseline byte-for-byte after V001 changes.

🧪 Testing Simulation — V000/V001 pure-Python end-to-end (commit 25e336c)

Why simulate before touching SAP at all?

Most SAP projects test by deploying ABAP to a sandbox client, running F110 with synthetic data, and inspecting the output XML. That works, but it has three drawbacks: (1) it requires a transport, (2) it requires sandbox SAP authorisation, (3) running 794 test scenarios serially through F110 takes hours per run. The simulator solves all three: it is pure Python, runs entirely on local Gold DB data, and renders V000 + V001 pain.001 XML in seconds per scenario. We can iterate on the V001 design at the speed of code review, not the speed of SAP transports.

What the simulator actually does

The simulator implements every layer of the SAP-side pipeline in Python: it reads real P01 payment data from the Gold DB (REGUH_FAST + REGUP + LFA1 + ADRC), follows the same field mappings the DMEE tree would follow, builds V000 (current) and V001 (proposed) XML side-by-side, then validates both against the official ISO 20022 XSDs. The simulator is correctness-equivalent to F110 + DMEE for the address-tag scope — and that equivalence is itself a tested invariant (claim 105: 794/794 PASS on both pain.001.001.03 and pain.001.001.09 schemas).

What this enables for V001

Three high-leverage outcomes: (1) design questions that would otherwise need bank confirmation (e.g., "does the bank accept the V001 tag layout?") become testable locally — the simulator validates against pain.001.001.09 (the CBPR+ Nov 2026 schema) so we know V001 is forward-compatible without sending a single test file; (2) per-tree per-vendor edge-cases (UltmtCdtr Worldlink, name-overflow, missing house-numbers) get exhaustive coverage in seconds; (3) the simulator becomes the regression baseline for Phase 3-4 testing — when D01 simulation produces a real V001 XML, we diff it against the simulator's expected output to catch any unexpected SAP-side behavior.

Tool: Zagentexecution/mcp-backend-server-python/xml_simulator.py — autonomous Python (no ABAP deploy needed). Reads real P01 data from Gold DB, renders V000 + V001 pain.001 XML per tree, validates against XSDs.

Pipeline

Real P01 data (REGUH_FAST + REGUP + LFA1 + ADRC from Gold DB)
  ↓ [Python templates per tree: SEPA, CITI, CGI]
V000 pain.001 XML
  ↓ [V001 transformer: insert structured PstlAdr per Marlies + N_MENARD spec]
V001 pain.001 XML
  ↓ [XSD validator]
Validate against pain.001.001.03 (current SAP) + pain.001.001.09 (CBPR+ Nov 2026)

Tool reusability

Any future DMEE change can be simulated by editing the V001 transformer rules in Python. Permanent regression test infrastructure for UNESCO DMEE.

Pay-type axis — orthogonal dimension connecting to PPC system

The pay_type column (derived from FPAYH-DORIGIN[0:2]) takes 3 values used by the PPC dispatcher (YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_UTIL::GET_TAG_VALUE_FROM_CUSTO, claim 99):

  • O (Other) — vendor invoice payments. Most common (~70% of in-scope).
  • P (Payroll) — DORIGIN starts with HR. SEPA pm=S split between O+P (#1+#2 of top 15) is purely a PPC-routing concern, not a tree-design concern — V001 nodes don't differentiate.
  • R (Replenishment) — DORIGIN starts with TR. Includes Worldlink BRL (#4 of top 15). PPC tags fire here for the 9 PPC countries.
Operational consequence for V001 risk model

Every V001 risk question is bounded by "which of the 81 scenarios?" instead of "what if some unknown payment breaks?":

  • Phase 3 unit test stratifies by the 81 — top 8 cover >88%, top 15 cover 95%
  • Phase 4 UAT needs only ~5-8 scenarios for bank end-to-end validation; simulator already proved the other 73 are schema-equivalent
  • Cutover monitoring (Phase 5) — daily schema-fail rate per scenario class; investigation scope bounded
  • Regression baseline — re-run scenario_discovery + simulator after V001 deploys for byte-level V000-vs-V001 diff per scenario class
Volume reconciliation — Overview tab vs scenario_discovery

Overview tab quotes ~176K SEPA / ~85K CITI / ~76K CGI (process_mining_real_tree_per_payment.json — CONFIG-derived T042Z lookup, counts F110 payments at REGUH header level). Simulator scenario_discovery quotes 292K / 177K / 175K (counts invoice lines at REGUP level). One payment can have N lines. Both correct under their respective definitions.

Phase 0 — Discovery & 100% Code Inventory (COMPLETED · 2026-04-24)

Why "100% inventory" before any design

Phase 0 set a hard rule: no design decision without evidence. UNESCO's payment XML pipeline has been touched by 8 authors over 10 years; new contributors typically see only the visible parts (the DMEE tree + the BAdI they touch) and miss the customizing tables, exit functions, and event modules behind the scenes. Phase 0's job was to enumerate everything — every Z-class, Y-include, customizing entry, Event 05 wrapper, byte-buffer field — so V001 design starts from a verified inventory rather than assumptions. The "100%" is not rhetorical: every single MP_EXIT_FUNC reference in the 1,975 P01 nodes was traced to its function module, and every function module was extracted and inspected.

What Phase 0 actually delivered

The Phase 0 outputs become the foundation every later phase rests on: (a) the reference architecture (3 compliance states: Unstructured / Hybrid / Structured), (b) the 31-component map (Components Map tab), (c) the Phase 0 closure report which signed off that no piece of code/config was unaccounted for, (d) the gap-closure memos for each open question. Anything labeled "Phase 0" below is the archive of that discovery — Phase 0 is closed; you are reading the receipts.

Inputs: Marlies email 2026-04-14 + Excel "XML Address un structured.xlsx" (10 production cases) + handoff doc UNESCO_BCM_StructuredAddress_AgentHandoff.docx v1.0 + h18 P01 DMEE baseline (2026-04-06) + Brain v2.

⚠ Read this before reading the rest of Phase 0 — design supersedes

Phase 0 sections below mention a planned custom function module Z_DMEE_UNESCO_DEBTOR_ADDR writing into FPAYHX-ZREF01..ZREF05. That FM is not built. Discovery later in Phase 0 (and confirmed by static-scan claim 68 — zero UNESCO writers to FPAYHX-Z* / FPAYH-REF) found that the SAP-standard user exit FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_CGI_05 already fills FPAYHX-REF01..REF10 from ADRC, and DMEE tree nodes can bind directly to those byte slices (claim 101 byte layout). The current V001 design (Sub-option A) reuses this SAP-standard chain — V001 only adds (a) 1 row in TFPM042FB registering Event 05 for SEPA (matrix row 9), and (b) the DMEE_TREE_NODE INSERT rows binding to REF01..REF06 byte slices. No new ABAP FM is created. The current design lives in Phase 2 §3 "Address-fill chain" and Change Strategy. Phase 0 is preserved as the discovery archive — you are reading the receipts of how we got here.

Section 4 — SAP Architecture (E2E flow)

SAP architecture — Payment file generation E2E

F110 (Automatic Payment Run)
  │
  ▼
FBZP Configuration (Payment method → House bank → PMW format)
  │
  ▼
OBPM1 (Payment Medium Format → DMEE tree mapping)
  │
  ▼
DMEE Engine (tree traversal, reads FPAYHX / FPAYH / FPAYP)
  │         ├── MP_SC_TAB/MP_SC_FLD = direct table-field read
  │         ├── MP_CONST = constant value
  │         └── MP_EXIT_FUNC = call BAdI / FM (794 nodes in our 4 trees)
  │
  ▼
BAdI FI_CGI_DMEE_EXIT_W_BADI → dispatch by country to:
  │         ├── YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FR    (France)
  │         ├── YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_DE    (Germany, P01-only)
  │         ├── YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_IT    (Italy, P01-only)
  │         └── YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FALLBACK (default)
  ▼
XML output file written to \\hq-sapitf\SWIFT$\P01\input\
  │
  ▼
BCM (Bank Communication Management — Claim #65: 100% routed via OBPM5/TFIBLMPAYBLOCK)
  │
  ▼
Workflow 90000003 (dual-control approval, signatories from PD OTYPE='RY')
  │
  ▼
SWIFT / Alliance Lite2 → Bank gateway
  │
  ▼
Bank schema validation (pain.001.001.09 XSD + bank-specific rules)

BLOCK/ASSIST/IRRELEVANT classification — procedure (to execute in Phase 0 continued)

For each of the 5 transports, need to:

1. Fetch the transport's E071 object keys (pyrfc `RFC_READ_TABLE E071 WHERE TRKORR=X`)

2. Fetch the DMEE tree node IDs in the transport (if any are PAYM tree entries)

3. Compare node IDs against the `PstlAdr` subtree node IDs in `/CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO` and `/CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO_1`

4. Classify:

- **BLOCK**: touches any PstlAdr node in Dbtr/Cdtr/CdtrAgt/UltmtCdtr hierarchy

- **ASSIST**: touches structure supporting address work (FPAYHX mapping, char filter nodes on address, condition suppressing AdrLine)

- **IRRELEVANT**: touches unrelated parts of the tree (Purp, payment amount tags, reference tags)

- If BLOCK: coordinate merge path; schedule a joint review

- If ASSIST: treat as prerequisite; evaluate if his changes help or hinder

- If IRRELEVANT: no coordination needed; log in the audit
