Vendor Master Data Quality

Vendor Master Data Quality — ADRC Compliance Audit

**Phase 0 deliverable** · 2026-04-24 · Evidence tier: TIER_1 (SQL against Gold DB `p01_gold_master_data.db`)

Query — handoff doc §7.2 (adapted to Gold DB)

SELECT COUNT(*)
FROM LFA1 l
JOIN ADRC a ON l.ADRNR = a.ADDRNUMBER
WHERE (a.CITY1 IS NULL OR a.CITY1 = '' OR a.COUNTRY IS NULL OR a.COUNTRY = '')
  AND (l.LOEVM IS NULL OR l.LOEVM = '')

CBPR+ compliance impact

Per handoff doc §2.1 and §7.2, **only `TwnNm` (=CITY1) and `Ctry` (=COUNTRY) are MANDATORY** under ISO 20022 structured or hybrid address. All other fields (StrtNm/BldgNb/PstCd) are recommended but their absence only downgrades to Hybrid mode, which is still CBPR+-valid through 2026 (and beyond, with stricter bank spec).

Compliance levelVendor count readyVendor count blocked
**Survival (Hybrid minimum: TwnNm+Ctry)**111,236 (99.995%)**5**
Preferred (full structured: all 5 fields)~32,000~79,000 (missing BldgNb/StrtNm/PstCd)

[VERIFIED] conclusion

**Compliance survival is secured.** Only 5 vendors need manual cleanup of CITY1/COUNTRY before go-live. This is a **hard-fail-if-missing** fix, not a systemic cleanup.

The BldgNb (HOUSE_NUM1) 68.8% miss is cosmetic — under Hybrid mode, missing BldgNb does not reject the file. Some banks may push for fully-structured stricter compliance post-2026; in that case, vendor master cleanup becomes a separate project (out of scope here).

Implications for the plan

1. **Phase 1**: request the 5 specific vendor IDs from Master Data team; fix by manual LFA1/ADRC update before V01 UAT

2. **Phase 2**: no data-cleanup blocker for config start

3. **Phase 3-4**: Hybrid-mode tests will pass for 99.995% of vendors; the 5 are the known edge cases

4. **Post-go-live**: monitor ADRC data quality; new vendors must have CITY1+COUNTRY populated or F110 rejects the item

Risk level: **LOW**

Previously in the plan this was flagged as a potential major risk gating Phase 3. This audit downgrades it to LOW.

Query for the 5 vendors (execute in Phase 1 for cleanup)

SELECT l.LIFNR, l.NAME1, a.CITY1, a.COUNTRY, a.STREET, a.POST_CODE1, a.HOUSE_NUM1
FROM LFA1 l
JOIN ADRC a ON l.ADRNR = a.ADDRNUMBER
WHERE (a.CITY1 IS NULL OR a.CITY1 = '' OR a.COUNTRY IS NULL OR a.COUNTRY = '')
  AND (l.LOEVM IS NULL OR l.LOEVM = '')
ORDER BY l.LIFNR;

✅ Phase 0 — CONCLUSION

What we delivered

  • Complete data-mutation chain decoded: F110 → PMW → OBPM4 Event 05 → SAP country factory → FPAYHX_FREF/FPAYP_FREF buffers → DMEE tree traversal → TECH switch nodes (-DBTRPSTLADR/-PSTLADRMOR1/2/3/etc.) → BAdI UNESCO impls → CV_RULE transformations → XSLT post-proc (CITI) → file → BCM → SWIFT
  • 5 of 8 gaps CLOSED, 2 PARKED, 0 blocking: GAP-003 (AE/BH don't exist in P01) · GAP-004 (FPAYHX Z-fields real names) · GAP-005 (zero UNESCO writes to Z-fields) · GAP-006 (1,975 nodes + 614 conditions + 26-field headers extracted) · GAP-008 (T042 mapping confirmed) · GAP-001/007 parked
  • 12 Findings A-L documented in plan with evidence tier (TIER_1)
  • D01 vs P01 anomaly identified: 5 P01-ONLY objects (YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_DE/IT + 3 ENHO) — D01 retrofit required before Phase 2
  • Vendor DQ risk downgraded HIGH→LOW: only 5/111,241 vendors miss mandatory CITY1/COUNTRY
  • Francesco classified: 5 transports 2025 Q1 are PMF variant config (VC_TFPM042F), not tree structure — ASSIST/IRRELEVANT
  • Brain v2 enriched: +7 claims (id 66-72, TIER_1), +3 feedback rules
  • Companion v1 built (16 original flat tabs → now restructured by phase)
  • 4 local commits (f1d1598, e3bf312, a01857a, 5dff1e8)

What we learned that changed the design

  • Handoff doc §5 had wrong field names: FPAYHX-ZSTRA/ZHSNM/ZPSTL/ZORT1/ZLAND do NOT exist. Real fields: ZPFST/ZPLOR/ZLISO/ZLNDX/ZREGX/ZREF01..ZREF10. FPAYH has ZERO REF fields; buffers live in FPAYHX-ZREF01..ZREF10.
  • Event 05 FMs already exist and are SAP-standard: FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_CGI_05 + /CITIPMW/V3_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_05 registered for CGI and CITI. SEPA has NO Event 05. UNESCO doesn't need to write Z_DMEE_UNESCO_DEBTOR_ADDR from scratch (handoff doc pattern was correct but unnecessary for CGI/CITI).
  • PSTLADRMOR1/2/3 are TECH scaffolding nodes, not magic parameters: they group address sub-elements and emit conditional on FREF data availability — SAP-native multi-mode.
  • DMEE VERSION column supports 2-file strategy natively: VERSION=000 current, create VERSION=001 structured in parallel, atomic activation/rollback.
  • Hybrid (single file mixed) REJECTED per user directive — too risky, hard to rollback, parser confusion. 2-file + versioning chosen instead.
  • BAdI version-awareness needed: YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FALLBACK_CM001 has stateful name-overflow-into-StrtNm quirk that would corrupt V001 structured StrtNm. Pattern A fix (structure-aware guard, 1-2 lines) required.

Blockers for Phase 2 (to resolve in Phase 1)

  • D01 retrofit from P01: 5 P01-only objects must be synced to D01 via pyrfc extraction + transport
  • Extract YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_DE + _IT source (currently blocked by RFC auth, use ADT/SE24 export)
  • Extract XSLT CGI_XML_CT_XSLT content (SAP-std, devclass ID-DMEE)
  • Q3 Worldlink UltmtCdtr data source (CITI WHO/ICC case) — needs Citi TRM + DBS input
  • N_MENARD alignment: BAdI Pattern A fix review + D01 retrofit approval
  • Francesco courtesy alignment: disclose his 2025 Q1 transports are context-only, no conflict

Phase 1 starts from

  1. Bank spec TRM outreach (SocGen / Citi / CGI-routed) — 7-day window
  2. Resolve the 5 DQ vendors manually
  3. Resolve Q3 data source
  4. Schedule N_MENARD + Francesco alignment calls
  5. Build change_matrix.csv with per-node action (ADD/MOD/DEL/KEEP) for V001

Phase 1 — Config matrix + bank specs (CLOSED · 2026-04-30)

Why Phase 1 sits between Discovery and Build

Phase 0 told us what exists. Phase 2 will build. Phase 1 is the bridge: it locks the per-tree / per-node design at the level of detail M_SPRONK can configure with no judgment calls remaining, and it closes any external open question (bank-specific strictness, pre-Phase-2 retrofit gaps) so Phase 2 starts unblocked. If Phase 2 ever has to pause to ask "should we do X or Y here?", Phase 1 left a gap — so Phase 1's discipline is to enumerate every decision and document the resolution.

How Phase 1 closed

Three deliverables: (1) the V001 Change Matrix (full node-by-node spec, see Matrix tab), (2) the resolution of each "open architectural decision" (Q1 Pattern A, Q1bis FR/CM002 retrofit, Q3 UltmtCdtr Worldlink — all closed), (3) the bank-strictness assessment via simulator + brain claim 105 (Fully-Structured satisfies CBPR+ regardless of per-bank strictness, removing TRM dependency from the critical path). Phase 1 closure means Phase 2 has zero design questions to resolve.

Owner: Pablo + Marlies + TRM network

Section 4 — Vendor DQ remediation (5 vendors)

Query to run in Phase 1 to get the 5 specific LIFNRs missing CITY1 or COUNTRY, then coordinate with Master Data team for manual LFA1/ADRC fix.

SELECT l.LIFNR, l.NAME1, a.CITY1, a.COUNTRY, a.STREET, a.POST_CODE1
FROM LFA1 l
JOIN ADRC a ON l.ADRNR = a.ADDRNUMBER
WHERE (a.CITY1 IS NULL OR a.CITY1 = '' OR a.COUNTRY IS NULL OR a.COUNTRY = '')
  AND (l.LOEVM IS NULL OR l.LOEVM = '')
ORDER BY l.LIFNR;

Phase 2 — Config D01: D01-RETROFIT + V001 + Pattern A (PENDING · May 2026)

Why Phase 2 starts with a retrofit, not the V001 build

Logically, "build V001 in D01" sounds like the obvious first step of Phase 2. But D01 is not currently equal to P01 — and (post-VPN RFC verification 2026-04-30, claims 109 + 111) precisely diagnosed the drift. The retrofit scope is now surgical, not "huge multi-tree". DMEE side: SEPA / CITI / CGI are byte-equal D01=P01 V000 (zero deltas); only CGI_1 has 12 deltas — 1 ONLY_D01 SCB + 8 ONLY_P01 AdrLine + 3 CHANGED (Nm Z-field experiment + 2 BROTHER_ID consequential). Plus all 4 trees carry a dormant V001 entries (byte-identical clone of V000, never released — claim 109) that needs PURGE before fresh V001 creation. ABAP side: 5 P01-only retrofit objects (DE/IT classes + 3 ENHO + FR.CM002 method). Step 0 of Phase 2 is therefore D01-RETROFIT: ~1-2h surgical (12 CGI_1 nodes + dormant V001 purge + 5 P01-only ABAP retrofit) before V001 build. User directive 2026-04-29 made this explicit.

How Phase 2 sequences (5 steps)

Step 0 — D01 retrofit (eliminate drift). Step 1 — Pattern A 3-line BAdI fix in D01 (the only ABAP change). Steps 2-4 — Build V001 nodes in each of the 4 target trees, one tree per transport, V001 deployed dormant alongside live V000. Each step is its own transport with its own review and its own verification gate. Phase 2 is the longest phase in calendar terms (~4 weeks) because it is also the highest-judgment phase: every node placement is verified against the matrix before save.

Owner: Pablo (config) + N_MENARD (ABAP review) + Marlies (verification)

⚠ FIRST EVER released-transport V001 at UNESCO — operational dry-run mandatory

Per brain claim 102 TIER_1: zero V001/V002 patterns in any of 44 historical transports 2017-2025 (released-transport scope). Per claim 109: P01 is on VERSION=000 only across all 4 trees; D01 already carries dormant V001 entries (byte-identical clone of V000, never released — to be PURGED at retrofit Step 0). Phase 2 Steps 2-4 (PURGE dormant V001 + CREATE fresh V001 + edit nodes) + Phase 5 Step (V001 activate) are: (a) PURGE — never exercised on UNESCO trees, (b) CREATE — was exercised once in D01 dormantly (different operators, undated), (c) ACTIVATE — never exercised on UNESCO trees. The transport-released round-trip D01→V01→P01 of V001 is also a first.

Mandatory pre-Phase-2 dry-run procedure: knowledge/domains/Payment/dmee_versioning_procedure.md. Verifies (a) authorization profile allows Activate Version in D01, (b) transport prompt UX is understood, (c) reversibility (V000↔V001 atomic flip) works as designed.

Transport ID assignment table (8 transports planned for V001 deployment): see linked procedure doc — this closes the missing-deliverables gap.

Section 3 — Address-fill chain + BAdI Pattern A fix

Address-fill chain — Sub-option A (reuse SAP-std, register Event 05 for SEPA only)

Design correction: an earlier draft of this section described creating a new user-exit FM Z_DMEE_UNESCO_DEBTOR_ADDR writing into FPAYHX-ZREF01..ZREF05. That FM is not built. Static analysis of 986 ABAP files (claim 68) confirmed UNESCO has zero writers to FPAYHX-Z* / FPAYH-REF custom buffers. The address atoms (street/building/postcode/city) are already available at runtime via the SAP-standard Event 05 user exit FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_CGI_05, which fills FPAYHX-REF01..REF10 (the SAP-standard buffers, not the Z-buffers) by calling CL_IDFI_CGI_CALL05_GENERIC::GENERIC_CALL against ADRC. The byte layout (claim 101) is REF01[0..60]=street, REF01[60..80]=building, REF01[80..90]=postcode, REF01[90..100]=region, REF06[0..40]=city. V001 reuses this existing infrastructure — no new FM, no new ABAP — by binding the new DMEE_TREE_NODE rows directly to those byte slices.

What V001 actually does for the address-fill chain

The work splits into two parts: register Event 05 where it isn't yet, and add tree-node rows that read the buffers. Both are customizing transport class W. No workbench (K) for the address chain itself — the only ABAP touch in V001 is the unrelated Pattern A 3-line guard in the CGI BAdI (matrix row 26).

TreeEvent 05 status todayAction in V001Matrix row
/SEPA_CT_UNESNOT registered in TFPM042FB+1 row in TFPM042FB linking format → FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_CGI_05 at Event 05. After this, F110 fires Event 05 for SEPA payments and REF01..REF10 buffers fill the same way they do for CITI/CGI today.Row 9 (precondition for SEPA INSERTs to emit non-empty tags)
/CITI/XML/UNESCO/DC_V3_01Registered (presumed in P01)None — buffers already fill—
/CGI_XML_CT_UNESCORegistered (presumed in P01)None — buffers already fill—
/CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO_1Registered (presumed in P01)None — SYNC inheritance from CGI parent—

D01 verification of "presumed in P01" rows is part of D01-RETROFIT-02-PMW — see 🔍 D01 ↔ P01 Checks → "PMW infrastructure alignment" → TFPM042F/TFPM042FB row.

The TFPM042FB INSERT (matrix row 9)

Customizing transport D01K-V001-OBPM4-01 contains a single SM30 / OBPM4 maintenance: add one row binding format /SEPA_CT_UNES + Event 05 → user-exit FM FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_CGI_05 (SAP-standard, already shipped). No ABAP source change, no FUGR, no new SE37 object.

The DMEE tree-node rows that read the buffers

For SEPA Cdtr/PstlAdr (matrix rows 1–4) and SEPA Dbtr/PstlAdr (matrix rows 5–8), the new DMEE_TREE_NODE rows have MP_SC_TAB='FPAYHX', MP_SC_FLD='REF01' or 'REF06', with the MP_OFFSET/LENGTH taken from the byte layout above. CITI / CGI similar — all 22 INSERT operations across the 4 trees bind to the same SAP-standard REF01..REF10 buffer layout.

Example V001 row — SEPA Cdtr/PstlAdr/StrtNm (matrix row 1):
  TREE_ID    = /SEPA_CT_UNES
  VERSION    = 001
  PARENT_ID  = N_4754354180   (Cdtr/PstlAdr existing parent, V000 carried)
  TECH_NAME  = StrtNm
  NODE_TYPE  = T (Element)
  MP_SC_TAB  = FPAYHX
  MP_SC_FLD  = REF01
  MP_OFFSET  = 0
  LENGTH     = 60

Why this is configuration, not code: the address atoms are produced by SAP-standard infrastructure (Event 05 user exit + ADRC read). UNESCO's V001 only adds (a) one TFPM042FB row registering Event 05 for SEPA — closing a gap that exists for historical reasons — and (b) DMEE tree-node rows reading the now-populated buffers. Both are class W customizing transports. The "create a Z FM" path in earlier drafts was an unnecessary detour: it would have duplicated work that FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_CGI_05 already does for CITI and CGI, and it conflicted with the static-scan finding (claim 68) that no UNESCO buffer-writers exist or are needed.

Pattern A — the ONLY ABAP change in V001 (CGI tree, 3 lines)

Separately from the address-fill chain, the CGI tree's BAdI fallback class YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FALLBACK_CM001::GET_CREDIT needs a 3-line guard so the new StrtNm node does not get clobbered by the legacy SocGen-mandated name-overflow logic. Workbench transport D01K-BADI-FIX-01 (class K). Reviewer: N_MENARD (DMEE BAdI code owner — claim 70 + 9 DMEE class transports 2024). Backward-compatible with V000.

Reviewers and ownership

N_MENARD — Pattern A guard code review (matrix row 26). F. Spezzano (FP_SPEZZANO) — historical OBPM4 / TFPM042F maintenance experience (5 DMEE transports 2025) — useful peer reviewer for matrix row 9 if available. M_SPRONK — DMEE tree-node design + business sign-off.

Phase 3 — Unit Test D01/V01 (PENDING · June 2026)

Why Phase 3 is "Unit Test" and Phase 4 is "UAT"

Phase 3 is where developers and testers verify V001 produces correct XML — not where business users sign off (that is Phase 4). The distinction matters because the cost of a bug found in Phase 3 is hours; the cost of the same bug found in Phase 4 is days plus stakeholder confidence. Phase 3 catches everything mechanical: schema validation against pain.001.001.03 XSD, BAdI regression on Pattern A, byte-level diff of V000 vs V001 output. Phase 3 fails fast and loud so Phase 4 can focus on judgment calls (does the bank accept this in their test gateway? does Marlies confirm the field mapping matches the source XLS?).

Where Phase 3 runs

Two environments: D01 for DMEE simulation (no real F110, no real REGUH) plus V01 for end-to-end F110 runs with the V001 dormant tree active for Z-payment-method test routes only. Production V000 stays untouched. Bug found = transport reverted in D01, regenerated, retested. Each test scenario from the matrix in this tab maps to one verifiable XML output.

Owner: Pablo + DBS + Marlies

Phase 4 — UAT V01 + bank pilot (PENDING · July 2026)

Why Phase 4 has TWO audiences (business + bank)

Phase 4 is where V001 graduates from "validates against ISO XSD" to "real banks accept it". Two different audiences sign off in parallel: (1) business users at UNESCO HQ + IIEP + UIL (Marlies + per-entity finance leads) verify that the file content matches their expectation — that vendor names appear correctly, that PPC tags fire for the 9 PPC countries, that intercompany payments still route correctly; (2) banks (SocGen TRM, Citi TRM, sometimes the receiving banks at vendor end) accept V001 files in their test gateways and issue written acceptance. Both must complete before Phase 5 cutover.

Why bank acceptance is in UAT and not earlier

You might think bank acceptance should happen in Phase 3 (unit test). But sending files to a bank test gateway is itself a costly, slow, calendar-bound activity — TRMs respond on their own SLA, not ours. Doing it in Phase 3 would gate Phase 3 on external dependency. By keeping bank pilot in Phase 4, we ensure all the mechanical validation passes first (Phase 3 green), and when we approach the bank we are confident our file is XSD-correct. That preserves credibility with TRMs and reduces back-and-forth iterations. Brain claim 105 (Fully-Structured satisfies CBPR+ regardless of per-bank strictness) further reduces the bank dependency to a 1-page logistics confirmation rather than a multi-week negotiation.

Owner: Marlies + per-entity finance leads + bank TRMs

UAT scenarios (handoff §8.2)

See Test Matrix — UAT section. Plus:

  • Monthly EUR salary/vendor via SocGen (UNES + IIEP + UIL) — SEPA V001 output
  • USD international vendor payment via Citi — CITI V001 output
  • Worldlink TND (Tunisia) + MGA (Madagascar) + BRL (UBO) — CITI V001 output with unified UltmtCdtr (Q3 RESOLVED #62, claim 99)
  • Non-SocGen EUR via CGI — CGI V001 output
  • Non-Latin character vendor addresses (Arabic etc.) — char filter regression

Bank pilot validation

  • Send V001 file per bank to their TEST gateway (separate from live)
  • Collect written acceptance email per bank
  • If rejection: diagnose + fix in V001 + re-send

  • Phase 5 starts with: [ready to cutover / blocked on bank X]

Phase 5 — Deploy P01 staged (PENDING · Aug-Nov 2026 · CBPR+ hard deadline Nov 1)

Why Phase 5 is staged, not big-bang

By Phase 5, V001 has passed unit tests (Phase 3) and UAT + bank acceptance (Phase 4). One option would be to flip all 4 trees from V000 to V001 simultaneously and be done. Phase 5 deliberately rejects that approach. Cutting over one tree at a time, with a 14-day monitoring window between trees, gives us three safety nets: (a) if a tree's V001 has an unexpected bank-side issue, only that one tree is affected and we can roll back without disturbing the other 3; (b) 14 days is enough to catch slow-burn bugs (delayed bank rejections, monthly reporting glitches, edge-case vendor combinations); (c) the team gets to tune their monitoring and rollback muscle on the lowest-risk tree first before proceeding to higher-risk ones.

Why the order is CGI → SEPA → CITI

Order matters in staged cutover. We go from narrowest blast radius to widest. CGI first because the V001 change there is just the CdtrAgt fix — small surface area, no PPC interaction risk during the address-tag verification window. SEPA second because it has full V001 node additions but only DE/FR routing (modest volume). CITI last because it carries the highest payment volume across BR/CA/FR plus the Worldlink UltmtCdtr edge case — most exposed if anything fails. By the time we get to CITI, we have already seen V001 succeed in production on two trees, monitoring playbook is proven, rollback has been rehearsed.

The Nov 1 2026 deadline pressure

CBPR+ goes live Nov 1, 2026. After that date, banks will reject pain.001 files with only unstructured <AdrLine> addresses. Phase 5 must complete before Nov 1. Aug-Sep-Oct gives us roughly 12 weeks for 3 staged cutovers with 14-day buffers and slack — comfortably within the schedule, with room for one rollback-and-retry cycle if needed. Slipping into Oct 25 or later would leave no slack for an unexpected rollback, so the working target for last-tree-cutover is mid-October.

Owner: DBS (transport) + Pablo (monitoring) + Marlies (business confirmation)

Cutover order (staggered 2-week windows)

  1. CGI trees first — narrowest change scope (CdtrAgt only), lowest volume per week
  2. SEPA_CT_UNES — medium volume, Sub-option dependent on Phase 2 choice
  3. CITI/XML/UNESCO/DC_V3_01 last — highest volume, Worldlink edge cases

Rollback plan (per tree)

Trigger: >2 bank rejects in 24h attributable to address format
        OR XSD validation failure rate >1%
        OR Marlies/Treasury-head override

Action:  DMEE activate V000 / deactivate V001 atomically in D01
         Transport to P01 via emergency path
         V001 preserved inactive for investigation
         SLA: cutover <60 minutes from decision

Post-rollback:
  Diagnosis of V001 failure
  Fix in next V001 iteration (or V002)
  Re-cutover in 2-week cycle

Post-go-live monitoring (14 days per tree)

  • Daily BCM batch reject count per tree (existing Zagentexecution/bcm_dual_control_monitor.py extended)
  • Schema validation fail rate (should be 0%)
  • Vendor-specific errors (expected <0.01% per active-vendor pop)
  • Bank confirmations of file acceptance (daily check)

V000 decommission (Phase 5+30 days)

  • After 30 days of stable V001 in prod across all 4 trees
  • Delete V000 from DMEE tree headers
  • Clean transport to remove V000 nodes from all 3 systems
  • Final plan retrospective + brain session close

Timeline — 5 phases (gated)

Why "gated" matters more than "scheduled"

Most project plans are calendar-driven: "Phase X starts April 27, ends April 30". This timeline is gate-driven instead: each phase has an explicit deliverable that must be signed off before the next phase opens. The calendar dates are targets, not commitments — a phase whose gate is not met does not advance just because the date arrives. The point is to protect downstream phases from upstream incompleteness: if Phase 1 closes without a complete change matrix, Phase 2 will discover the gap mid-build, and unwinding is more expensive than waiting.

How to read the timeline below

Each row is one phase. The Gate column is the actual exit criterion — the artefact that must exist + be signed before the next phase starts. The Status column tells you where we are right now. The end-to-end sequence runs from Discovery (April 2026) to V000 decommissioning (~December 2026, 30 days after final cutover).

The Plan (live) — rendered from plan file

Why this tab exists separately from the others

Every other tab in this companion is curated, structured, and aimed at a specific audience (Scope for V001 deliverables · Strategy for the deployment decision · Phase tabs for execution sequence · etc.). This tab is the raw, unedited plan file — the long-form working document the team uses for in-flight design discussions. It is preserved verbatim because some sentences ("Q3 BLOCKED", "deferred to V002", "depends on Citi spec") capture the history of the plan, not just the current state — and that history matters per CP-001 (knowledge over velocity): future readers should be able to reconstruct how decisions evolved, not only what they ended up as.

How to read this tab vs the others

If you want the current state of any decision, read the curated tabs (Scope, Strategy, Phase tabs). If you want to understand how a question was raised, debated, and closed, read the relevant section of the live plan below. Where the curated tabs and the plan disagree (e.g., Q3 was BLOCKED in the plan and is RESOLVED in the curated tabs), the curated tabs reflect the current state and the reading-guidance callout below points to the resolution. Treat the live plan as institutional memory, not a source of truth for current design.

# Plan — UNESCO DMEE Structured Address Migration (CBPR+ Nov 2026) > **⚠️ Phase 0 is IN EXECUTION. Major findings that supersede earlier assumptions are captured in the "Phase 0 execution findings" section below (between Reference architecture and Phase 0 spec). Read that section BEFORE the phase specs below — Phase 1-5 specs still reflect the original (pre-probe) assumption in some places; the "findings" section is the current source of truth.** ## Reading order for this document (history-preserving) This plan is written as a **combined history**: every step we did, every correction, every finding stays in place. Nothing is overwritten — later sections supersede earlier ones when they conflict, and we flag those conflicts explicitly (like the "Phase 0 execution findings" section). Per CP-001 ("Preserve first, context is cheap"), we add instead of consolidate. **Sections in execution order** (each one captures a step we took and the reasoning behind it): 1. **Context** — why this change exists (email thread + bank mandate) 2. **Reference architecture** — how we interpreted the handoff doc as the technical anchor 3. **BCM context from brain v2** — what we pulled from the project's existing knowledge 4. **Brain ↔ Plan feedback loop** — the bidirectional pattern for this project 5. **Phase 0 execution findings (2026-04-24)** ← the current active execution pass, supersedes earlier assumptions where flagged 6. **Phase 0 spec** — the original design of Phase 0 (history) 7. **Phase 1-5 specs** — original design (history; may contain pre-correction statements — check findings section first) 8. **Companion HTML structure** — the live deliverable 9. **Critical files / References / Verification / Timeline** — the execution shape **How to tell what is current**: any claim that appears in both Phase 0 findings AND a phase spec — **the Phase 0 finding wins**. Phase specs are preserved as the original agreed scope so later sessions can see what we planned vs what we discovered. **Date**: 2026-04-24 · **Session**: #62 · **Project**: abapobjectscreation **Drivers**: Marlies Spronk (FIN/TRS) email 2026-04-14 + `UNESCO_BCM_StructuredAddress_AgentHandoff.docx` v1.0 --- ## Context — Why this change Banks will reject XML payment files with **only unstructured `<AdrLine>`** addresses starting **November 2026** (ISO 20022 CBPR+ mandate, enforced by SocGen / Citi / CGI member banks). UNESCO runs **3 custom DMEE trees** in P01 that currently emit Hybrid or fully Unstructured addresses. Marlies (treasury, also the historical author of 28 DMEE transports 2017-2024) has analyzed 10 real production payments, identified which tags need structuring per tree, and requested technical support to execute the change in 2026. **The change is bank-driven** (not just regulatory) — a specific "request from the banks" per the user. Each bank's exact strictness may differ from the CBPR+ minimum (`TwnNm` + `Ctry` mandatory, rest optional under Hybrid), so per-bank spec acquisition is gate zero. **Coexistence strategy** (user-confirmed): we run **old AdrLine-based format and new structured format in parallel** during transition — not a hard cutover. Hybrid (structured + AdrLine side-by-side) is valid CBPR+ through 2026, giving a rollback safety net and a migration buffer for vendor master data quality fixes. **Intended outcome**: by 2026-11-01, every outgoing pain.001 from UNESCO has at minimum `<TwnNm>` + `<Ctry>` + preferably the full 5-tag structured PstlAdr in Cdtr and Dbtr blocks, with AdrLine removed or deprioritized per tree. --- ## Reference architecture — interpreted from `UNESCO_BCM_StructuredAddress_AgentHandoff.docx` v1.0 This doc is not an input among many — it is the **technical reference we execute against**. Three interpretive conclusions from reading it end-to-end shape the plan: ### Conclusion 1 — Compliance has 3 states, not 2 | State | Example | Validity after Nov 2026 | Our use | |---|---|---|---| | **Unstructured** | `<AdrLine>...</AdrLine><Ctry>FR</Ctry>` | REJECTED | Today's state in SEPA + CITI trees | | **Hybrid** (min viable) | `<TwnNm>Paris</TwnNm><Ctry>FR</Ctry><AdrLine>...</AdrLine>` | OK — `TwnNm`+`Ctry` are the ONLY two mandatory, rest optional | **Minimum survival target per tree** | | **Fully Structured** | `<StrtNm>…</StrtNm><BldgNb>…</BldgNb><PstCd>…</PstCd><TwnNm>…</TwnNm><Ctry>…</Ctry>` | OK + future-proof | Long-term target, gradual migration | **Priority order for our work**: guarantee `TwnNm` + `Ctry` on every `<PstlAdr>` across 3 trees FIRST (= compliance survival). Then add `StrtNm`/`BldgNb`/`PstCd` (= preferred). This makes phase 2 gradual, not all-or-nothing — and matches the user directive "2 formatos que podrán coexistir". ### Conclusion 2 — Three asymmetric technical patterns by XML party The doc's section 5 makes clear that Cdtr, Dbtr, and UltmtCdtr each require a **different mechanism**: | Party | Data source today | Change mechanism | |---|---|---| | **Cdtr** (vendor) | SAP auto-populates `FPAYHX-Z*` (ZSTRA/ZHSNM/ZPSTL/ZORT1/ZLAND) from LFA1→ADRC at payment-run time | **DMEE tree configuration only** — add 5 child element nodes under `Cdtr/PstlAdr` sourced from FPAYHX Z-fields. No ABAP needed. ⚠ Depends on GAP-005 confirming the Z-field populator. | | **Dbtr** (UNESCO) | NOT in FPAYHX or FPAYH — must be produced at runtime | **User exit ABAP** (new FM `Z_DMEE_UNESCO_DEBTOR_ADDR`) + registration in OBPM4 **Event 05** + DMEE nodes reading `FPAYH-REF01..REF05`. **Same FM registered in all 3 PMW formats** per doc recommendation. | | **UltmtCdtr** (Worldlink only — CITI) | **UNKNOWN** per doc Q3 "confirm data source with DBS before coding" | **BLOCKED — cannot plan config until source resolved**. Candidates: vendor master, Z-table, separate user exit. | ### Conclusion 3 — 17-step checklist in doc §9 replaces inventing our own Phase 2 Handoff doc §9 is a turnkey May 2026 execution checklist: steps 1-17 covering tree confirmation, transport creation, per-tree node changes, user exit creation, OBPM4 registration, test F110 runs, XSD validation, screenshots, and release to V01. Phase 2 of this plan adopts those 17 steps directly instead of paraphrasing. ### Reference SAP Notes ranked by actionability From doc §10 (we fetch from SAP Launchpad, not in our repo): 1. **1665873** — CGI_XML_CT full introduction guide (59 pages). **Canonical source** for the CGI tree we copy as template. Processes 1+2 may route via different config. Phase 1 confirms which trees each of 4 processes uses. ### Implications for future change decisions (beyond this one change) Consolidating what brain tells us about the BCM stack — this plan is ONE change in a bigger picture. Future decisions shaped by the brain: 1. **Any BAdI we create (e.g. `Z_DMEE_UNESCO_DEBTOR_ADDR`) should be BCM-aware**: read `T001-ADRNR` via `BAPI_COMPANYCODE_GETDETAIL` per SAP Community pattern. Preserve compatibility with future BCM enhancements (structured vendor name, CtctDtls email, etc.). 2. **If a future change needs preventive address validation**: follow the H39 pattern (separate BAdI, not DMEE config) — brain has this documented as the correct architecture for cross-cutting validation. 3. **Vendor master cleanup is cross-cutting**: the DQ audit in Phase 0 feeds multiple tracks (structured address, BR substitution H39, carry-forward 2026, future MDM efforts). Output belongs in the shared knowledge base, not buried in this project. 4. **Coexistence strategy (Hybrid transition)** extends to future format changes too: any future migration (pain.001.001.09, new countries, new UltmtCdtr tags) should default to additive/coexistence, not replacement. 5. **Signatory workflow immutability during this change**: we change what gets rendered to approvers but not how they approve. Probed TADIR on both D01 and P01 for DMEE/payment/address components. Result: **zero objects are D01-only** (reassuring). **But five objects are P01-ONLY — a reverse anomaly**: | Object | Type | In D01? | In P01? | Author | Devclass | |---|---|---|---|---|---| | `YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_DE` | CLAS | ❌ | ✅ | N_MENARD | YA | | `YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_IT` | CLAS | ❌ | ✅ | N_MENARD | YA | | `Y_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_COUNTRIES_DE` | ENHO | ❌ | ✅ | N_MENARD | YA | | `Y_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_COUNTRIES_FR` | ENHO | ❌ | ✅ | N_MENARD | YA | | `Y_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_COUNTRIES_IT` | ENHO | ❌ | ✅ | N_MENARD | YA | **Interpretation [INFERRED]**: DEV (D01) is **incomplete vs PROD (P01)** for the DMEE BAdI ecosystem. Likely cause: objects were transported to P01 but later removed from D01 (system refresh gap, transport-of-copies, or D01 rebuild). N_MENARD's 9 transports 2024 may have rebuilt parts of this in D01 but not all. **This is a BLOCKER for Phase 2**: if we edit `YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FALLBACK` in D01 and release the transport to P01, we risk: - Activation failures (BAdI dispatcher expects `_DE` and `_IT` country classes to be registered; if `Y_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_COUNTRIES_FR` enh impl doesn't exist in D01, the FR dispatch logic breaks) - Regression in Italian/German payments (those impls exist in P01, are called at runtime, but can't be modified/tested from D01) - Inconsistent transport state that may be flagged at import **Required action before Phase 2**: 1. **Retrofit D01 from P01**: extract source of `YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_DE/_IT` + 3 enhancement impls from P01 via pyrfc `RPY_CLASS_READ` / `RPY_PROGRAM_READ`, re-deploy to D01 in a **sync transport** so D01 and P01 match. 2. **Document the anomaly** in a brain claim so future sessions know D01 baseline is partial. 3. **Alignment with N_MENARD** (BAdI owner) on why the divergence exists — might be intentional (e.g., test version in D01) but we need to know. **Source**: `knowledge/domains/Payment/phase0/d01_vs_p01_inventory.csv` + `.json`. Note on probe limitations: my patterns missed DMEE tree objects (needed a different query — DMEE OBJECT in TADIR doesn't use standard name prefix). Tree-level D01 vs P01 divergence was already captured in h18 baseline (2026-04-06): D01 has 2× node count vs P01 on `/CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO` (1,262 vs 631) — those extra D01 nodes are draft work unrelated to structured address (per h18 finding (2026-04-06)). ### Finding J — Transition strategy via DMEE VERSION column (user-requested 2026-04-24) User directive: *"podemos hacer 2 files para cada banco, sino no podemos hacer roll back luego o será más difícil salvo que haya una forma de manejar versiones"*. **DMEE does support versioning** — confirmed via round 1 probe: `DMEE_TREE_NODE` has a `VERSION` column (4th in the schema: `TREE_TYPE, TREE_ID, VERSION, NODE_ID, ...`). We can: 1. **Keep current tree as version V1 (current production, AdrLine-heavy)** 2. **Create new version V2 with structured address nodes** 3. **Activate V2 for SOME payment methods while keeping V1 for others** (via T042Z configuration) 4. **Rollback = switch T042Z back to V1 tree** Alternative 2-file strategy (user's preferred framing): - For the SAME payment batch, generate TWO files: one with old format (V1/AdrLine-heavy) sent to bank's test/secondary channel, one with new format (V2/structured) sent to bank's primary channel - Compare bank acceptance of both - Cut over when new format confirmed accepted - Rollback = disable generation of V2, keep V1 **Assessment of 2-file strategy**: - **Pros**: true parallel validation; real rollback path without config switch; allows gradual bank-by-bank cutover - **Cons**: doubles F110 processing time per batch; requires bank to accept dual-channel testing (most banks support this via a test gateway); doubles DMEE config work (have to maintain both trees until cutover); risk of duplicate payment if both channels succeed simultaneously (mitigation: always one is test/no-post, one is live) **Assessment of DMEE version strategy**: - **Pros**: single-tree, single-file per batch; SAP-native; activation is one config switch (T042Z tree_version); rollback is one-click - **Cons**: version activation is ALL-or-NOTHING per payment method — can't run V1+V2 side-by-side for the SAME method; no parallel validation of outputs **Recommended combination** (current design): 1. **Phase 2 deploys V2 of each tree to D01** (V1 stays intact as the active version) 2. **Phase 3 unit tests V2 in D01 via DMEE simulation + F110 proposal** — uses T042Z override per payment method to force V2 3. **Phase 4 UAT in V01 runs BOTH V1 and V2** side-by-side for select test batches: - V1 generates the real file sent to bank (production path, backed up) - V2 generates a parallel file sent to bank's **test gateway** for format validation - Bank confirms V2 structured address is accepted before cutover 4. **Phase 5 go-live** switches T042Z from V1 → V2 per payment method, **staggered**: low-volume CGI methods first, CITI Worldlink last 5. **Rollback**: flip T042Z back to V1; V1 config never touched during the change, so rollback is instant and data-safe **Plan impact**: this changes the Phase 2 config spec. Instead of modifying the existing tree nodes, we **copy the existing tree to V2 and modify V2**. V1 remains frozen. The 17-step checklist from handoff §9 adapts: - Step 2 creates a transport for NEW tree versions, not modifications to existing - Steps 3-8 add structured nodes **to V2**, not to the current (V1) tree - Step 16 before/after screenshots compare V1 vs V2 output - Step 17 release promotes V2 to V01/P01 in INACTIVE state; activation is a separate customizing decision ### Finding K — DMEE data-mutation chain fully decoded (2026-04-24, Phase 0 round 3) After extracting all 48 DMEE_TREE_NODE columns + DMEE_TREE_COND (614 rows) + DMEE_TREE_SORT (39 rows) + DMEE_TREE_HEAD (26 fields × 4 trees) + source of `FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_CGI_05` + `FPAYHX_FREF` / `FPAYP_FREF` schemas + CL_IDFI_CGI_CALL05_* factory inventory (20+ country classes SAP-std), the complete data-mutation pipeline is now understood: ``` F110 payment run ↓ PMW auto-populates FPAYHX (SAP-standard, NO UNESCO code) ↓ OBPM4 Event 05 FM fires (table TFPM042FB registration): /CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO → FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_CGI_05 (SAP std) /CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO_1 → FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_CGI_05 (SAP std) /CITI/XML/UNESCO/DC_V3_01 → /CITIPMW/V3_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_05 (CITI PMW) /SEPA_CT_UNES → NO EVENT 05 REGISTERED ⚠️ ↓ FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_CGI_05 = thin wrapper: CALL METHOD cl_idfi_cgi_call05_factory=>get_instance(...) CALL METHOD instance->fill_fpay_fref(...) ↓ Factory dispatches to SAP country class CL_IDFI_CGI_CALL05_{AT|BE|CH|CZ|DE|DK|ES|FI|FR|GB|HR|IT|LU|PT|RO|SK|TH|GENERIC} Each implements interface IF_IDFI_CGI_CALL05 Writes structured address components to FPAYHX_FREF + FPAYP_FREF buffer fields ↓ FPAYHX_FREF structure = 16 fields: REF01..REF15 (CHAR 264 each) + CURNO (NUMC 24) FPAYP_FREF structure = 5 fields: REF01..REF05 (CHAR 264 each) Generic buffers — meaning of each REF is defined per DMEE tree configuration ↓ DMEE tree traversal — structured nodes read from FREF buffers: (verified: CGI tree uses FPAYP-REF01 for StrtNm AND BldgNb AND PstCd — differentiated by MP_OFFSET / MP_SC_OFFSET substring positions) ↓ TECH switch nodes (NT=TECH, MP_SC_TAB empty) — structural scaffolding: N_9020685600 REF=-DBTRPSTLADR → Debtor PstlAdr N_2938451040 REF=-CDAGPSTLADR → Creditor Agent PstlAdr N_6304594040 REF=-PSTLADRMOR2 → Creditor PstlAdr (Cdtr) N_7541094900 REF=-PSTLADRMOR1 → Ultimate Debtor PstlAdr (UltmtDbtr) N_4036970840 REF=-PSTLADRMOR3 → Ultimate Creditor PstlAdr (UltmtCdtr) ⬅ Marlies Q3 blocker N_2326418530 REF=-PSTLADRMORE → general PstlAdr_More_Nodes N_6123792920 REF=-CTRYOFRES → Country of Residence N_4647535410 REF=-CTRYOFRES1 → CtryOfRes variant ↓ DMEE_TREE_COND: each structured element's emission gated by its parent TECH node's state (parent TECH node "active" = FREF data available from Event 05) ↓ BAdI FI_CGI_DMEE_EXIT_W_BADI fires per-node (794 nodes / 40%) — UNESCO impls IF_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_COUNTRIES interface — YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FR/FALLBACK/UTIL/DE/IT Can mutate c_value per node (e.g., FALLBACK_CM001 name-overflow-into-StrtNm quirk) ↓ CV_RULE applied (426 nodes / 21.6%) — transformations like AL.2 (amount align), CL (lowercase), CL RP X (lowercase+replace), CL R0 (right-pad 0) ↓ For CITI: XSLT CGI_XML_CT_XSLT post-processes (author=SAP, devclass=ID-DMEE) ↓ File write to \\hq-sapitf\SWIFT$\P01\input\ ↓ BCM batch (Claim #65 routing via OBPM5/TFIBLMPAYBLOCK) ↓ Alliance Lite2 → Bank ``` ### Two separate UNESCO code layers, different interfaces | Hook | Interface | UNESCO impls | When | |---|---|---|---| | Event 05 | `IF_IDFI_CGI_CALL05` | **NONE** — SAP std `FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_CGI_05` + country factory | Pre-tree (once per payment) | | BAdI FI_CGI_DMEE_EXIT_W_BADI | `IF_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_COUNTRIES` | YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FR / FALLBACK / UTIL / DE / IT | In-tree (per node with MP_EXIT_FUNC) | Our 5 UNESCO classes DO NOT touch Event 05. They are in-tree per-node mutators. Earlier plan assumption that Z_DMEE_UNESCO_DEBTOR_ADDR would be a new Event 05 handler was **correct pattern, wrong field names** (handoff doc said FPAYH-REF which doesn't exist; reality is FPAYHX_FREF / FPAYP_FREF). **But even that FM is likely unnecessary for CGI and CITI** — SAP already covers those via country factory. ### Design recommendations — revised Phase 2 (user-directed 2-file + versioning strategy) **User feedback 2026-04-24**: "why Hybrid? why not 2 files and change configuration. No hay manejo de versiones en algo tan complejo?" → **Hybrid rejected. 2-file + DMEE versioning promoted to default**. **DMEE supports native versioning** (confirmed via `DMEE_TREE_NODE.VERSION` column + DMEE_TREE_HEAD.VERSION + standard tx DMEE Create/Activate Version). Currently `VERSION=000` in all 4 UNESCO trees. We create `VERSION=001` per tree with structured nodes. Only one version active at a time per tree; activation is atomic config. **Strategy**: ``` Phase 2 (May 2026): /CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO V000 ACTIVE (Francesco's 2025-03-20 state) → unchanged, still produces prod file /CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO V001 INACTIVE (our new structured work, deployed dormant) /CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO_1 same pattern /CITI/XML/UNESCO/DC_V3_01 same pattern /SEPA_CT_UNES same pattern (V001 with structured add) Phase 3 unit test (June 2026): Create Z-payment method routing V001 F110 with regular method → V000 (production output, untouched) F110 with Z-method → V001 (structured output, tested in isolation) Phase 4 UAT (July 2026): Send V001 output via bank test gateway for schema + acceptance validation V000 continues to handle live production payments Zero production risk Phase 5 cutover (Nov 2026): Once bank validates V001: - Deactivate V000, Activate V001 atomically in D01 → transport to P01 - All F110 now produce structured Rollback (if bank/BCM rejects): - Activate V000, deactivate V001 → instant revert, no data loss ``` ### Why 2-file + versioning beats Hybrid | Criterion | Hybrid (single file, mixed) | 2-file + DMEE versioning | |---|---|---| | Rollback | Config switch, mid-file risk | Atomic version flip — seconds | | Bank validation | All-or-nothing sent to live | Parallel via test gateway, zero prod risk | | File content | Structured + AdrLine coexist (parser confusion risk) | Clean single-mode file | | CBPR+ compliance | Minimum viable (TwnNm+Ctry) | Fully structured (future-proof) | | Testability pre-cutover | Production-risky | **Fully isolated — V001 dormant until activated** | | SAP-native | Manual dual-node hack | **Native — DMEE Create Version / Activate Version** | | Vendor DQ edge cases | Silent AdrLine fallback (wrong-file risk) | F110 errors clearly signal missing data | ### Per-tree design with 2-file strategy **For CGI trees** (`/CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO` + `_1`): - Create V001 as copy of V000 - In V001: fix CdtrAgt unstructured nodes (small change per Marlies Excel) - CGI already has SAP Event 05 + CL_IDFI_CGI_CALL05_* country factory populating FPAYHX_FREF → structured mode works natively once CdtrAgt is correctly configured - ZERO ABAP needed **For CITI tree** (`/CITI/XML/UNESCO/DC_V3_01`): - Create V001 as copy of V000 - In V001: add TECH PstlAdr switch + structured Dbtr nodes reading from CITIPMW FREF - UltmtCdtr Worldlink → still BLOCKED by Q3 (data source) — may need to defer to V002 or keep as AdrLine in V001 if Q3 unresolved by Phase 2 - ZERO ABAP likely — CITIPMW factory already provides infrastructure **For SEPA tree** (`/SEPA_CT_UNES`): - Create V001 as copy of V000 - **Key decision**: does V001 add Event 05 infrastructure? - **Sub-option A**: V001 also registers Event 05 FM (SAP-std `FVD_SEPA_OL_CT_DMEE_05` or `FI_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_CGI_05`) — need to test compatibility in D01 first. If it works, SEPA gains full multi-mode parity with CGI. ZERO ABAP. - **Sub-option B**: V001 has new direct-read structured nodes (StrtNm←ZPFST, Ctry←ZLISO, TwnNm+PstCd parsed from ZPLOR via CV_RULE/MP_OFFSET). Simpler but ZPLOR parsing reliability depends on vendor master consistency. ZERO ABAP. - **Sub-option C**: V001 uses new UNESCO FM `Z_DMEE_UNESCO_SEPA_05`. Requires ABAP + D01 retrofit first. Skip unless A+B fail. **Recommended SEPA path**: try Sub-option A in D01 first (register `FVD_SEPA_OL_CT_DMEE_05` for `/SEPA_CT_UNES` V001 and test). If compatible → done. If not → fall back to Sub-option B (direct-read). ### Revised Phase 2 sequencing | Week | Work | Output | |---|---|---| | 1 | Create V001 on all 4 trees (copy V000, transport) | V001 INACTIVE in all 3 systems | | 2 | CGI V001 — fix CdtrAgt structured nodes | DMEE test run generates clean CGI structured file | | 2 | CITI V001 — add Dbtr structured nodes (UltmtCdtr held for Q3) | DMEE test run generates clean CITI Dbtr-structured file | | 3 | SEPA V001 — test Sub-option A, fall back to B if needed | DMEE test run generates structured SEPA file | | 3 | Z-payment method created for V001 routing (for test) | Z_SEPA_V001, Z_CGI_V001, Z_CITI_V001 payment methods | | 4 | F110 test: V000 (live) vs V001 (test) parallel runs | 2 files per batch during testing window | **Phase 2 compressed to 4 weeks, ZERO ABAP, version-safe rollback path end-to-end**. ### Finding L — Custom ABAP must be version-aware (user-raised 2026-04-24) User directive: *"el código abap custom debe reconocer las versiones"*. **SAP-native versioning reality**: the BAdI `IF_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_COUNTRIES->GET_VALUE` **does NOT receive a VERSION parameter**. When DMEE activates V001, SAP traverses V001 nodes — the BAdI sees the nodes of the ACTIVE version but without explicit version context. Most BAdI logic is inherently version-scoped (because the nodes it receives come from the active version's DMEE_TREE_NODE rows). **But there is one case where version-awareness matters**: stateful BAdI with cross-WHEN buffer variables. Our `YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FALLBACK_CM001::GET_CREDIT` does exactly this: ```abap " V000 behavior: name > 35 chars → save overflow in mv_cdtr_name buffer " then at StrtNm node → prepend buffer to c_value WHEN '<PmtInf><CdtTrfTxInf><Cdtr><Nm>'. mv_cdtr_name = c_value. ... WHEN '<PmtInf><CdtTrfTxInf><Cdtr><PstlAdr><StrtNm>'. IF i_fpayh = mv_fpayh AND mv_cdtr_name+35 IS NOT INITIAL. c_value = |{ mv_cdtr_name+35 } { c_value }|. ← corrupts real structured street in V001! ENDIF. ``` **In V001 (structured mode)**, StrtNm gets a REAL street value from FPAYP-REF01 (or similar). The BAdI's overflow-prepend would corrupt it. This is THE version-awareness issue in our stack. #### Resolution patterns **Pattern A (RECOMMENDED) — structure-aware, not version-aware**: ```abap WHEN '<PmtInf><CdtTrfTxInf><Cdtr><PstlAdr><StrtNm>'. IF i_fpayh = mv_fpayh AND mv_cdtr_name+35 IS NOT INITIAL AND c_value IS INITIAL. "V001 guard — only prepend if StrtNm source is empty" c_value = mv_cdtr_name+35. ELSEIF i_fpayh = mv_fpayh AND mv_cdtr_name+35 IS NOT INITIAL. c_value = |{ mv_cdtr_name+35 } { c_value }|. "V000 legacy behavior preserved" ENDIF. IF c_value+70 IS NOT INITIAL. CLEAR c_value+70. ENDIF. ``` - 1-2 line change, backward-compatible, reviewer N_MENARD only validates 3 lines - No DMEE VERSION parameter needed (doesn't exist in BAdI signature) - Works across all current + future DMEE versions **Pattern B — Separate tree IDs**: `/SEPA_CT_UNES` (V000) + `/SEPA_CT_UNES_V2` (new tree). BAdI checks `I_TREE_ID` for overflow hack. Zero ABAP change but duplicates trees (no atomic version-activation benefit). **Pattern C — Dynamic version detection in BAdI**: `SELECT SINGLE EX_STATUS FROM DMEE_TREE_HEAD WHERE TREE_ID = X AND EX_STATUS = 'A'` per call. Per-node DB overhead → rejected for performance. **Recommendation**: Pattern A. #### Design consequence — ONE ABAP change IS needed Revising earlier claim of "ZERO ABAP needed" for Phase 2. **Pattern A fix to `YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FALLBACK_CM001::GET_CREDIT` is required** to make the existing BAdI structure-aware (safe across V000 and V001). This: - Unblocks Phase 2 Week 2-3 (CGI + CITI + SEPA V001 deployment can proceed) - Respects SAP-native versioning - Requires D01 retrofit of the 5 P01-only objects FIRST (Finding I blocker still holds) - Reviewer = N_MENARD (class owner, Finding C) - One transport `D01K-BADI-FIX-01` with 1 method + 3 lines changed #### Broader principle — stateful BAdI buffers must be idempotent across structure variants Added as a design rule for future DMEE work at UNESCO: - Any BAdI with MEMBER/GLOBAL buffers shared across nodes (like `mv_cdtr_name`, `mv_fpayh`) must guard buffer write-back with "is target value already populated?" checks - Structure-aware > version-aware (fewer params, more resilient) - Applies to existing ZDMEE_EXIT_SEPA_21 + Z_DMEE_EXIT_TAX_NUMBER — need a quick audit of each for similar statefulness ### Remaining unknowns for this design 1. **Does Sub-option A work for SEPA?** — requires D01 test registration + F110 run (Phase 2 Week 3 first task) 2. **Does DMEE version activation transport cleanly between D01→V01→P01?** — SAP-standard, should work; to verify in Phase 2 Week 1 3. **CITI UltmtCdtr Q3** — unchanged blocker; may keep as AdrLine in V001 if unresolved by Phase 2 4. **XSLT `CGI_XML_CT_XSLT`** — does it process V001 output differently than V000? SAP-std XSLT typically reads the tree result structure, not version-dependent. To verify in Phase 3 test. ### Remaining unknowns (legitimate, not gaps I can close in this session) 1. **CITIPMW_V3_PAYMEDIUM_DMEE_05 source extraction failed** (RFC error on WITH_INCLUDE param). Need SAP authorization or alternative extraction. Blocks understanding of CITI UltmtCdtr/WHO→ICC case. 2. **YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_DE + _IT source** — RPY_CLASS_READ FU_NOT_FOUND. Need ADT extraction alternative. 3. **XSLT `CGI_XML_CT_XSLT` source** — not extracted. SAP-std so content should be documented externally or read via SE80. 4. **Q3 Worldlink UltmtCdtr data source** — still blocked, needs Citi TRM / DBS input. 5. **SEPA Option A testability** — whether `FVD_SEPA_OL_CT_DMEE_05` works with `/SEPA_CT_UNES` tree — requires D01 test registration and F110 run. ### Artifacts produced in Phase 0 (so far) | File | Purpose | |---|---| | `knowledge/domains/Payment/phase0/francesco_audit.md` | FP_SPEZZANO 70 total / 5 DMEE transports classified-pending | | `knowledge/domains/Payment/phase0/vendor_master_dq.md` | 5 missing-mandatory vendors out of 111k — risk LOW | | `knowledge/domains/Payment/phase0/cts_dmee_authors.md` | 8 DMEE authors 10-yr history, N_MENARD as BAdI owner identified | | `knowledge/domains/Payment/phase0/gap_005_static_analysis.md` | 0 hits in 986 ABAP → no UNESCO code writes Z-fields | | `knowledge/domains/Payment/phase0/gap_probe_results.json` | JSON report of pyrfc probes for GAP-002/003/004/006 | | `knowledge/domains/Payment/phase0/gap006_dmee_tree_nodes_full.csv` | 1,975 nodes across 4 target trees with source mapping | | `Zagentexecution/mcp-backend-server-python/phase0_gap_probe.py` | Reusable probe script | ### Phase 0 tasks remaining - [ ] Re-probe DMEE_TREE_NODE with `MP_EXIT_FUNC` column (not EXIT_FUNC) + inspect exit function distribution - [ ] GAP-002 broader search: BAdI impls for `FI_CGI_DMEE_EXIT_W_BADI`, `PAYMENT_MEDIUM` spots via SXS_ATTR - [ ] Write `gap_closure_report.md` (consolidated) + `xml_touch_points_complete.md` (single-source inventory) - [ ] Brain v2 updates: new claims (Marlies=31, N_MENARD as BAdI owner, no FPAYHX-Z* writes, FPAYHX Z-field real names), new objects (ADRC already indexed — add annotation; Step 9 (user exit) is the gate for steps 5, 7, and Dbtr work. Step 7 (CITI UltmtCdtr) is the only one blocked on an unresolved Q (Q3 data source) — scope it last or carve out to a separate transport if Q3 resolution takes time. ### Priority stratification — Hybrid-minimum first, Structured-preferred second Per reference architecture conclusion 1 (TwnNm+Ctry is the only mandatory pair): **Tier A (compliance survival — do first, week 1)**: ensure every `<PstlAdr>` in the 3 trees emits `<TwnNm>` + `<Ctry>` unconditionally. Even for the CGI Dbtr treasury-transfer case that currently has only `<Ctry>FR</Ctry>` (Marlies Excel row 10), we add TwnNm. No AdrLine change yet. **Tier B (preferred structured — week 2-3)**: add StrtNm, BldgNb, PstCd. AdrLine kept with "suppress if populated" condition for Hybrid fallback on vendors with incomplete data. **Tier C (cleanup — week 4, post bank spec confirmation)**: per-bank, decide whether to fully deprecate AdrLine or keep Hybrid indefinitely. Depends on bank spec strictness from Phase 1. ### User exit for UNESCO Dbtr address (handoff §5.2 — mandatory) Per handoff doc, Dbtr (UNESCO company address) is **NOT in FPAYHX/FPAYH** — needs custom FM. - **FM**: `Z_DMEE_UNESCO_DEBTOR_ADDR` (new) - **Logic**: `SELECT SINGLE * FROM ADRC WHERE ADDRNUMBER = (SELECT ADRNR FROM T001 WHERE BUKRS = I_FPAYH-ZBUKR)` → populate E_FPAYH-REF01..05 with STREET / HOUSE_NUM1 / POST_CODE1 / CITY1 / COUNTRY - **Registration**: OBPM4 Event 05 for all 3 PMW formats (SEPA, CITI, CGI) - **Reuse**: same FM for all 3 formats per handoff recommendation - **Traceability**: new class/FM under `extracted_code/FI/DMEE/` after write; transport `D01K-FMFI-001` ### Per-transport deliverables - `change_log.md` with node-by-node before/after - Sample XML generated from DMEE simulation mode, diffed against Marlies Tab 2 target - Reviewer sign-off (Marlies) before progression to next tree ### Exit gate Each tree's transport reviewed + signed by Marlies before next tree config starts. --- ## Phase 3 — June 2026 Unit Test in D01/V01 ### Test matrix (`test_matrix.csv`) **Dimensions**: 3 trees × vendor archetypes (Domestic / Foreign / PO-Box / Long-name>35 / Diacritic / Individual-STCD2) × countries (FR, US, GB, KR, NG, BR, MG, TN) × edge cases (street>35, city>35, missing PstCd, null Ctry, Arabic chars). **Priority tier 1**: ~50 cases (all 3 trees × 6 vendors × 3 countries + handoff UT-01..08 mandatory) **Full grid**: ~144 cases **Schema validation layer**: automated diff against pain.001.001.09 XSD + bank-specific XSDs (SocGen, Citi). ### BAdI regression Verify `YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FALLBACK_CM001.abap:13-31` (35-char StrtNm overflow from Cdtr.Nm) behavior in structured mode — either still triggers appropriately or is documented as dead. Don't let a 2-decade-old overflow handler silently break new structured output. ### Success criteria - 100% XSD pass rate on tier-1 cases - Zero regressions vs P01 baseline for payments that already work - Hybrid coexistence verified: tree emits structured AND AdrLine when vendor master has both; emits structured only when complete; emits AdrLine fallback when vendor incomplete ### Exit gate Pablo + Marlies + DBS sign `test_results_june.md`. --- ## Phase 4 — July 2026 UAT in V01 ### Deliverables - **Per-bank pilot file** sent to SocGen + Citi + CGI banks for acceptance validation at their gateway (not just schema-valid) - UAT scenarios per handoff §8.2 (UAT-01 to UAT-12), validated by: Finance/Treasury, HRM (Worldlink TND/MGA), UBO/UIS/IIEP/UIL entity owners - Bank acknowledgment emails archived ### Success criteria All 3 banks (+ CGI-routed banks) return written confirmation that structured address is accepted at their gateway (not just schema-valid at XSD level). ### Exit gate Treasury head + all 4 entity finance leads sign UAT close-out. --- ## Phase 5 — August–November 2026 Deploy & Monitor ### Cutover order **CGI first** (narrowest change = CdtrAgt only, low business impact) → **SEPA** (medium) → **CITI last** (highest volume, Ctry fix touches every Worldlink currency). Staggered 2-week windows. ### Rollback strategy (per tree, 3 layers) 1. **Transport revert** — prior TR is TOC-able via DBS, revert DMEE_TREE_NODES to P-1 state 2. **Config revert** — T042Z/T042E/T042I changes captured in transports, same revert path 3. **Code revert** — git tag `baseline-pre-phase2-2026-04-30` on `extracted_code/FI/DMEE/` + ABAP transport of prior class version **Rollback trigger**: >2 bank rejects in 24h post-cutover **OR** schema validation failure rate >1%. ### Post-go-live monitoring Daily BCM batch reject count per tree for 30 days post-each-cutover. Dashboard: extend `companions/payment_bcm_companion.html` with a rejections tab. ### Exit criteria Nov 2026 CBPR+ deadline met; all 3 trees emit compliant address format; zero address-attributable rejects for 14 days straight. --- ## Companion HTML — Single Source of Truth (user directive) **File**: `companions/BCM_StructuredAddressChange.html` · versioned v1 (end Phase 0), v2 (end Phase 1), v3 (mid Phase 2), etc. **Pattern**: reuse styling of existing `companions/payment_bcm_companion.html` (dark theme, tab-based, self-contained single HTML). **Rule**: everything relevant to this change lives here. **The plan in this file is reproduced inside the companion**. Verification — how to test end-to-end ### Phase 1 (baseline + spec + audit) - `python Zagentexecution/mcp-backend-server-python/h18_dmee_tree_probe.py --tree /SEPA_CT_UNES --system P01 --dump-all --out baselines/2026-04-30_P01/` — dumps 7 DMEE tables; verify file count + row counts match prior h18 P01 baseline (2026-04-06) (sanity check). - `change_matrix.csv` parses cleanly; every row has target_src_type filled; no UNKNOWNs. - `francesco_audit.md` classifies all 5 transports; any BLOCK transports have an alignment meeting minuted. ### Phase 2 (config) - DMEE Tx → tree → Test mode: render sample payment → confirm XML contains `<StrtNm>Place de Fontenoy</StrtNm><BldgNb>7</BldgNb><PstCd>75007</PstCd><TwnNm>PARIS</TwnNm><Ctry>FR</Ctry>` for UNESCO Dbtr, matching Marlies Tab 2. - F110 proposal mode in D01: generate XML, no posting. Diff against target. - Transport export via SE10; verify TOC contains DMEE objects of correct scope only. ### Phase 3 (unit test) - F110 proposals in V01 for 50 tier-1 test cases. - XSD validation script runs against pain.001.001.09 schema — 100% pass required. - BAdI regression: payment with Cdtr.Nm >35 chars → verify overflow behaves per legacy OR fails loud if deprecated. - Hybrid coexistence test: vendor with full ADRC → structured-only output; vendor with partial ADRC → Hybrid fallback. ### Phase 4 (UAT) - Each bank receives pilot file → written acceptance - Business users run 12 UAT scenarios per handoff §8.2 - All sign-offs archived ### Phase 5 (deploy) - Post-cutover: BCM rejects < P-1 baseline + 1% - Daily monitor for 14 days per tree - 2026-11-01: formal CBPR+ compliance letter to internal audit --- ## Open architectural decisions (require Pablo + Marlies alignment pre-Phase-2) 1. **Per-bank strictness**: Fully structured vs Hybrid per bank — decided in Phase 1 after bank specs. Default: Hybrid-coexistence (per user directive). 2. **BAdI overflow logic fate**: keep / deprecate / refactor — decided during Phase 3 based on test. 3. **D01 draft purge on CGI trees**: the 2× node delta may be unrelated to structured address but may still block our changes. Decide after Francesco audit. 4. **UltmtCdtr data source for Worldlink** (Citi): vendor master / Z-table / user exit — handoff Q3, depends on Citi spec + DBS input in Phase 1. 5. **Separate PMW formats per entity** (IIEP/UIL for SEPA; UBO/UIS for CITI): per handoff Q4+Q5 — check FBZP during Phase 1. --- ## Non-obvious risks 1. **Marlies is the author AND the reviewer** (28 prior transports) — she may prefer to edit directly, bypassing the audit trail. **Mitigation**: change_matrix as shared single source; both sign each row before Phase 2 execution. 2. **Francesco territory on CGI D01** — his most recent transport (2025-03-20) is on `/CGI_XML_CT_UNESCO`. Editing could overwrite uncommitted WIP. **Mitigation**: Phase 1 audit precedes any CGI D01 edit; BLOCK classifications trigger 3-way alignment. 3. **BAdI wiring ambiguity**: `YCL_IDFI_CGI_DMEE_FALLBACK_CM001` has PstlAdr/StrtNm boilerplate — unknown if live trees invoke it. Silent break risk. **Mitigation**: trace MP_FCODE / exit-function column per Cdtr node in `h18_dmee_tree_nodes.csv` during Phase 1. 4. **Worldlink exotic currencies** (TND 3-decimal, MGA no-IBAN, BRL STCD2, ARS 90-day hold — `payment_full_landscape.md:114-128`) interact with structured address non-trivially. **Mitigation**: tier-1 test matrix must include BR, MG, TN, AR scenarios. 5. **Vendor master DQ**: the handoff SQL query will surface a count of non-compliant vendors. If the count is high (>5% of active), Phase 3 UAT is at risk. **Mitigation**: Phase 1 counts first; remediation plan with Master Data team before Phase 2 ends. 6. **Push blocker (prior session)** — local git only. **Mitigation**: all artifacts committed locally with safety tags; remote push decision deferred per user. 7. **"Francesco no sabía"** — user's directive says audit his transports as context but don't assume pattern. He may know more than it appears OR less. **Mitigation**: audit is evidence-only; if his transports surface relevant work, flag to user for decision; do not assume. --- ## Not in scope - Migration to pain.001.001.09 (from current .03 version) — that's a parallel SAP-upgrade topic handled via SAP Notes 2944738 / 2668719, tracked separately. - Consolidation of SEPA into CGI_XML_CT (some SAP customers have done this) — handoff Q8 says LOW priority, park for post-go-live. - Vendor master cleanup for non-active vendors (LOEVM = 'X'). - Non-payment address flows (e.g., customer master, BP master addresses in non-payment contexts). - BCM dual-control remediation (H13 — separate track, already in PMO). --- ## Timeline (gated) | Phase | Period | Owner | Gate | |---|---|---|---| | **0 — 100% Code Inventory Closure** | **2026-04-24 → 04-27** | **Pablo** | **`xml_touch_points_complete.md` signed; 0 UNKNOWN in "Change required" column** | | 1 — Config matrix + bank specs | 2026-04-27 → 04-30 | Pablo + Marlies | Matrix + bank specs + DQ count signed | | 2 — Config D01 | 2026-05-01 → 05-31 | Pablo (config) + Marlies (review) | Each tree transport signed before next | | 3 — Unit Test | 2026-06-01 → 06-30 | Pablo + DBS + Marlies | 100% XSD pass + BAdI regression green | | 4 — UAT V01 | 2026-07-01 → 07-31 | Marlies (business) + Pablo (tech) | 3 bank acceptances + all UAT scenarios signed | | 5 — Deploy | 2026-08-01 → 11-01 | DBS (transport) + Pablo (monitoring) | Nov 2026 CBPR+ compliance |

References (exhaustive, evidence-anchored)

Why an exhaustive reference list?

Every claim in this companion can be traced to a primary source: a Marlies email, a NMENARD spec, an extracted SAP table, a brain claim with TIER_1 evidence. The reference list below is the citation index — if you read something in any tab and want to see the original evidence, you find it here. The discipline is per CP-003 (precision, evidence, facts): every recommendation in this project must be anchored in checkable facts, not opinion.

How to use the four sections

  • A — UNESCO-internal user-provided: the primary inputs (Marlies email, handoff doc, original Excel). Authoritative for "what does the business want?"
  • B — UNESCO-internal baselines: project-extracted artefacts (CSV dumps, JSON inventories, gap-closure reports). Authoritative for "what exists in P01 today?"
  • C — N_MENARD spec attachments (PPC, Pattern A): the only documents that carry SocGen's bank-mandated requirement and the PPC dispatch infrastructure. Authoritative for "why does this exist?"
  • D — Brain claims + rules: TIER_1 evidence-backed assertions and behavioural rules. Authoritative for "why is this design decision the way it is?"
